This skill should be used when users want to create a new skill (or update an existing skill) that extends Codex's capabilities with specialized knowledge, workflows, or tool integrations. (file: C:/Users/ai/.codex/skills/.system/skill-creator/SKILL.md)

### How to use skills
- Discovery: The list above is the skills available in this session (name + description + file path). Skill bodies live on disk at the listed paths.
- Trigger rules: If the user names a skill (with $SkillName or plain text) OR the task clearly matches a skill's description shown above, you must use that skill for that turn. Multiple mentions mean use them all. Do not carry skills across turns unless re-mentioned.
- Missing/blocked: If a named skill isn't in the list or the path can't be read, say so briefly and continue with the best fallback.
- How to use a skill (progressive disclosure):
1) After deciding to use a skill, open its SKILL.md. Read only enough to follow the workflow.
2) When SKILL.md references relative paths (e.g., scripts/foo.py), resolve them relative to the skill directory listed above first, and only consider other paths if needed.
3) If SKILL.md points to extra folders such as references/, load only the specific files needed for the request; don't bulk-load everything.
4) If scripts/ exist, prefer running or patching them instead of retyping large code blocks.
5) If assets/ or templates exist, reuse them instead of recreating from scratch.
- Coordination and sequencing:
- If multiple skills apply, choose the minimal set that covers the request and state the order you'll use them.
- Announce which skill(s) you're using and why (one short line). If you skip an obvious skill, say why.
- Context hygiene:
- Keep context small: summarize long sections instead of pasting them; only load extra files when needed.
- Avoid deep reference-chasing: prefer opening only files directly linked from SKILL.md unless you're blocked.
- When variants exist (frameworks, providers, domains), pick only the relevant reference file(s) and note that choice.
- Safety and fallback: If a skill can't be applied cleanly (missing files, unclear instructions), state the issue, pick the next-best approach, and continue.
</skills_instructions>

name: memorytree-workflow
description: Detect, initialize, and maintain a reusable MemoryTree project-memory workspace for any code repository. On activation, immediately detect and report the repo's MemoryTree state.
---

# MemoryTree

Use this skill for repo-level project memory. Do not treat it as an application runtime feature unless the user explicitly asks to productize it.

## On Activation

When this skill is invoked, immediately perform these steps without waiting for further user input:

1. Detect the repo state (`not-installed`, `partial`, or `installed`) using `references/project-detection.md`.
2. Check `~/.memorytree/alerts.json`. If pending alerts exist, display them to the user before proceeding.
3. If `not-installed`: run `memorytree init` to scaffold the workspace, then report what was created.
4. If `partial`: run `memorytree upgrade` to add missing pieces, then report what was added.
5. If `installed`: read the active goal, bound todo, and latest chat log. Report the current state (goal summary, todo progress, pending tasks) and ask the user what they want to work on next. If `memorytree daemon status` shows the heartbeat is not registered, ask the user for their preferred heartbeat interval, auto_push preference, and scope, then offer to run `memorytree daemon install`. Use plain-text questions compatible with all AI assistants, not client-specific UI components.

Do not stop after detection to ask whether you should proceed. Act on the result immediately.

## Core Behavior

1. Detect the repo state before changing files. Use `references/project-detection.md`.
2. If MemoryTree is missing, initialize it with `memorytree init`. If the CLI is not available, create the files from `assets/templates/`.
3. If MemoryTree is partial, upgrade it with `memorytree upgrade` before manual maintenance.
4. If MemoryTree is already installed, maintain only the active goal, bound todo, and current chat log. Use `references/update-rules.md`.
5. Keep the installation compatible with the host repo's branch, PR, CI, and review rules. Use `references/git-policy.md`.
6. Prefer safe defaults: do not add reply suffix requirements unless the host repository already requires them, do not mix code-and-memory commits by default, and do not override branch policy. MemoryTree-only git automation is allowed only inside the isolated flow in `references/git-policy.md`.
7. When locale is not explicit, choose it from repo language first, then system language. Use `references/locale-selection.md`.
8. Keep reply language aligned with user language first, then repo locale. Use `references/response-language.md`.
9. For partial repos, use the non-destructive upgrade path before manual maintenance. Use `references/upgrade-path.md`.
10. When transcript archival is enabled, import transcripts with deterministic code, preserve raw transcripts as evidence in both the current repo mirror and the global archive, generate cleaned Markdown for indexing, keep cross-project backfills and ambiguous ownership cases in the global archive only, and ask once per repository whether raw transcript files may be committed or pushed. Use `references/transcript-archive.md`.
11. When CLI commands are needed, use `memorytree <subcommand>` (requires Node.js ≥ 20). If Node.js is not available, fall back to manual scaffolding from `assets/templates/`. See `references/execution-environment.md`.
12. Transcript discovery, import, cleaning, and push are handled by the background heartbeat process. The model only writes chat log summaries and updates goals and todos. See `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`.
13. Global configuration is stored in `~/.memorytree/config.toml`. See `references/global-configuration.md`.
14. When the user asks to see their most recent conversation, trigger an on-demand transcript sync for the current project, locate the latest session across all three clients, and generate a continuation summary. See `references/transcript-archive.md` and `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`.
15. All interactive prompts (heartbeat install, configuration, session continuity) must use plain-text questions compatible with every AI assistant that supports this skill. Do not rely on client-specific UI components. See `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`.

## Read Order

1. Repo `AGENTS.md`, if present.
2. Latest file in `Memory/01_goals/`.
3. Latest todo bound to that goal in `Memory/02_todos/`.
4. `Memory/04_knowledge/` only when needed.
5. `Memory/06_transcripts/clean/`, transcript manifests, and repo-local raw transcript mirrors only when transcript history or cross-project memory search is relevant.
6. `Memory/03_chat_logs/` and `Memory/05_archive/` only when needed.

## Detect

1. Check whether `Memory/` exists and matches the layout in `references/memory-layout.md`.
2. Classify the repo as `not-installed`, `partial`, or `installed`.
3. If the repo already has stronger rules than the generated templates, preserve the repo rules and only add missing MemoryTree pieces.

## Upgrade

1. Use `memorytree upgrade` for repositories that already have `AGENTS.md`, custom policy files, or partial `Memory/` content.
2. Preserve existing repo policy files by default.
3. Create only the missing MemoryTree pieces.
4. Read the upgrade result and treat `agents_merge_required=true` as a manual review task, not an overwrite instruction.

## Initialize

1. Run `memorytree init --root <repo>` and pass `--project-name`, `--goal-summary`, and `--locale` when the user already provided them.
2. Use fresh init only when the repo does not already have `AGENTS.md` or another repo policy source such as a policy-bearing `CONTRIBUTING.md`, PR templates, `CODEOWNERS`, or commitlint config. If repo policy already exists, switch to `memorytree upgrade` instead of trying to skip `AGENTS.md`.
3. Review the generated `AGENTS.md` before keeping it. Merge it with the repo's existing policy if needed.
4. Keep the initial installation minimal: `Memory/01_goals`, `02_todos`, `03_chat_logs`, optional `04_knowledge`, `05_archive`, and `06_transcripts` only when transcript archival is enabled for the repo or needed for transcript import.
5. Use the locale-specific template files in `assets/templates/<locale>/` as the source of truth for first-run scaffolding.
6. Prefer `--locale auto` when the user did not request a language explicitly.
7. Use `memorytree locale` when you need a deterministic locale check without scaffolding files.
8. If Node.js is not available, create first-run files directly from `assets/templates/` instead of requiring a runtime installation.
9. If transcript archival is enabled for the repo, use `memorytree import --source <file>` for one explicit source file and `memorytree discover` when scanning local client stores. Matching transcripts must update both the repo mirror and the global archive, while unrelated projects, ambiguous ownership cases, or mismatched explicit sources are archived in the global archive only. Let the CLI generate cleaned transcripts deterministically without spending model tokens on the cleaning step.
10. Ask once whether raw transcript files may also be committed to the repository. Record the answer in `AGENTS.md`, keep the files in the repo either way, and exclude `raw` files from automatic staging until the user says yes.

## Maintain

1. Change the active goal only after explicit user confirmation of a scope or requirement change.
2. Update the active todo when progress changes, milestones move, or the next task becomes clearer.
3. Append chat logs only. Never rewrite or delete prior entries.
4. Keep active files small. Move stale context to archive or knowledge files instead of bloating the active goal or todo.
5. Treat product ideas, architecture decisions, and operating constraints as goal or knowledge content. Treat step-by-step execution state as todo content.
6. Treat cleaned transcript indexes as discovery aids, not as the final source of truth. When exact wording matters, confirm against the raw transcript archive.
7. Prefer deterministic CLI-based transcript cleaning over manual rewriting. Do not spend model tokens to restate or normalize transcript content when `memorytree import` can do it.
8. Reply in the user's language when clear; otherwise align with repo locale without rewriting existing files just to translate them.

## Git And Safety

1. Never assume MemoryTree can override the repo's branch model.
2. Default to isolated MemoryTree-only Git operations: stage only MemoryTree-owned files, use a MemoryTree-scoped commit title, push to a dedicated branch, and open a dedicated PR.
3. Enable auto-merge only for MemoryTree-only PRs, and only when the repository still enforces its required review and CI checks.
4. Keep repo-local raw transcript mirrors and the global transcript archive synchronized on every import. The global index must remain safe for concurrent multi-project updates.
5. Keep the repository mirror limited to transcripts that belong to the current repository. Unrelated or ambiguous transcripts belong in the global archive only.
6. Keep raw transcript files under `Memory/06_transcripts/raw/**` in the repo, but exclude them from automatic staging until the user explicitly approved raw transcript uploads for that repository.
7. If the diff mixes product code, shared policy files, cross-project transcript archives, or unclear ownership, stop and ask the user before committing or pushing.
8. If the repo has protected branches or PR-only rules, follow them even if older MemoryTree rules say otherwise.
9. When `auto_push` is enabled, the heartbeat process pushes automatically after committing. If no Git remote is configured, the push is skipped. If a push fails, the heartbeat retries once. In either case an alert is written to `~/.memorytree/alerts.json`. See `references/git-policy.md`.
10. During transcript cleaning, the heartbeat scans for sensitive information (API keys, passwords, tokens). Matches are logged as warnings only — no automatic deletion or redaction. See `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`.

11. Do not modify the host repository's CI or E2E workflow definitions by default. If the user explicitly approves a MemoryTree-only optimization, prefer path-filtered or lightweight workflows for `Memory/**` and managed `AGENTS.md` PRs without weakening required branch protection.

## Resources

- `references/project-detection.md`: detect install state and choose init vs maintain.
- `references/memory-layout.md`: folder and file naming rules.
- `references/update-rules.md`: when to version goals, todos, and session logs.
- `references/git-policy.md`: safe Git defaults and policy merge guidance.
- `references/locale-selection.md`: locale choice rules and alias behavior.
- `references/response-language.md`: reply-language precedence and translation safety.
- `references/transcript-archive.md`: raw transcript archival, clean transcript indexing, per-client source rules, and repo upload confirmation rules.
- `references/upgrade-path.md`: safe adoption flow for partial repos.
- `references/execution-environment.md`: how to run MemoryTree CLI (requires Node.js ≥ 20).
- `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`: background heartbeat architecture, daemon CLI, and execution flow.
- `references/global-configuration.md`: `~/.memorytree/` directory layout, `config.toml` schema, and `alerts.json` format.
- `assets/templates/en/` and `assets/templates/zh-cn/`: seed files for English and Simplified Chinese initialization.
- CLI commands: `memorytree init`, `memorytree upgrade`, `memorytree import`, `memorytree discover`, `memorytree locale`, `memorytree recall`, `memorytree daemon install|uninstall|run-once|watch|status`.

# 视频预处理阶段代码审计报告

## 结论摘要

- 审计范围：`domain/video/pre/stage` 及其在 `domain/video/pre/main/pipeline.py` 中的接线关系。
- 目录职责：这是一个仍被主流程调用的旧式 0 到 9 阶段视频预处理流水线，不是单独的“字幕模块”。它负责清理状态、转码、去静音、视频修复、ASR、AI 改写剪辑文案、二次剪辑、字幕校正/烧录、封面标题生成、最终文件整理。
- 审计结论：高置信缺陷 11 个，重要改进项 8 个。整体风险等级：高。
- 测试现状：主流程阶段基本没有自动化测试；当前能看到的测试主要集中在 `domain/video/pre/stage/subtitle/tests/test_formatter.py` 和 `domain/video/pre/stage/subtitle/tests/test_parser.py`。

## 一、高置信缺陷（11个）

### 1. `stage9.py` 在清理失败时会强杀整机所有 `python.exe`

位置：`domain/video/pre/stage/stage9.py:352`、`domain/video/pre/stage/stage9.py:454`

影响：可能直接杀掉当前主进程、同机其他 Python 服务、调度器、训练任务或 IDE 后台任务。这个行为远远超出了“删除日志/临时目录”的职责边界。

说明：清理目录失败后执行 `taskkill /F /IM python.exe /T`，属于破坏性兜底。

建议：仅关闭本进程自己创建的句柄或子进程；删除失败就显式报错，不要使用按进程名全局清理。

### 2. `stage4.py` 用 `os.system` 拼接字符串执行命令，路径带空格或特殊字符时会失败，并存在命令注入面

位置：`domain/video/pre/stage/stage4.py:57-70`

影响：视频路径或输出目录只要包含空格、`&`、`(` 等 shell 敏感字符，就可能执行失败；若路径来源不可控，还会引入命令注入风险。

说明：先将参数 `join` 成字符串，再传给 `os.system`。

建议：改为 `subprocess.run([...], check=False)`，严格使用参数列表，不经 shell。

### 3. `utils.run_command` 顺序读取 `stdout` 和 `stderr`，存在子进程管道死锁风险

位置：`domain/video/pre/stage/utils.py:297-345`

影响：当子进程持续向 `stderr` 写大量数据时，`stderr` 缓冲区可能先被写满；父进程此时仍阻塞在读取 `stdout`，导致整体卡死。

说明：代码先完整读取 `process.stdout`，再读取 `process.stderr`。

建议：使用 `communicate()`、异步 IO，或两个线程并发消费两个流。

### 4. `utils.handle_ffmpeg_process` 也有同类顺序读管道问题

位置：`domain/video/pre/stage/utils.py:158-235`

影响：FFmpeg 本身就经常把大量进度和告警写到 `stderr`，这里比普通子进程更容易卡死。

说明：同样是先读 `stdout`，再读 `stderr`。

建议：与上一条一起统一改为并发消费或 `communicate()`。

### 5. `utils.input_with_timeout` 在 Windows 分支会泄漏阻塞在 `input()` 上的守护线程

位置：`domain/video/pre/stage/utils.py:95-118`

影响：多次调用后会积累无法回收的输入线程，控制台行为会变得不可预测，长期运行时尤其危险。

说明：超时返回后，启动的线程没有停止机制，也没有被 `join` 或回收。

建议：把交互逻辑移到 CLI 层；如果必须超时输入，使用可中断的控制台读取实现，不要在线程里永久阻塞 `input()`。

### 6. `stage5.py` 中 `wait_time` 可能未定义，触发 `UnboundLocalError`

位置：`domain/video/pre/stage/stage5.py:97-107`、`domain/video/pre/stage/stage5.py:149`、`domain/video/pre/stage/stage5.py:172`

影响：只要 `from pre.stage.config import get_config` 或 `get_config()` 进入 `except` 分支，后面仍会访问 `wait_time`，流程会直接崩。

说明：`wait_time` 只在 `try` 内赋值，`except` 里没有补默认值。

建议：在 `try` 前初始化默认值，例如 `wait_time = 5`。

### 7. `stage8.py` 在模块导入时直接关闭全局日志处理器

位置：`domain/video/pre/stage/stage8.py:37-50`

影响：只要导入该模块，整个进程里其他模块配置的 logger 也会被破坏，导致日志丢失、文件句柄异常或日志链路断裂。

说明：顶层代码遍历 `logging.root.manager.loggerDict` 并执行 `removeHandler/close`。

建议：日志初始化只能在主入口统一做；模块内部只获取本模块 logger，不得改全局 root handler。

### 8. `stage9.py` 在模块导入和函数执行时都在破坏全局日志状态

位置：`domain/video/pre/stage/stage9.py:24-37`、`domain/video/pre/stage/stage9.py:138-151`、`domain/video/pre/stage/stage9.py:425-436`

影响：比 `stage8.py` 更严重，因为它不仅导入时执行，进入 `step9_organize_files` 和 `clean_logs_and_state` 时也会再次清空全局日志。

说明：这是跨模块副作用，不是本模块自清理。

建议：删除这类全局 handler 清理逻辑，只处理本模块显式创建的 handler。

### 9. `stage5_0.py` 会在运行或导入时修改仓库源码树

位置：`domain/video/pre/stage/stage5_0.py:39-47`

影响：运行时自动创建 `funclip/utils/__init__.py`，会让部署结果依赖“是否先运行过脚本”，并破坏只读部署和镜像一致性。

说明：业务阶段代码不应修补包结构。

建议：通过打包、安装脚本或仓库修复一次性解决，不要在运行时写源码。

### 10. `stage5_1.py` 会在运行或导入时自动生成源码文件

位置：`domain/video/pre/stage/stage5_1.py:39-46`、`domain/video/pre/stage/stage5_1.py:57-82`、`domain/video/pre/stage/stage5_1.py:127-142`

影响：该模块不仅会写 `__init__.py`，还会生成 `subtitle_utils.py` 和兜底版 `process_video.py`。这会导致环境越脏越“能跑”，问题被掩盖，而且不同机器上的运行结果不一致。

说明：这是运行时热修仓库，不是业务逻辑。

建议：缺依赖就失败并给出安装说明，不要在生产流程里写代码文件。

### 11. `forum_hotword_extractor_v2.py` 依赖的 `forum_data_manager` 在仓库中不存在，数据库分支实际上是死代码

位置：`domain/video/pre/stage/forum_hotword_extractor_v2.py:41-46`、`domain/video/pre/stage/forum_hotword_extractor_v2.py:64`

影响：该模块会静默降级为无 data manager 分支，热词提取能力与设计不一致，且问题不会在启动时被及时暴露。

说明：全仓检索仅发现这里引用了 `forum_data_manager/get_data_manager`，没有对应实现文件。

建议：明确删掉死分支，或补齐依赖并在启动时做健康检查。

## 二、可改进点（8项）

### 1. `utils.py` 在导入时就执行 `setup_logging()`，并清空 root handlers

位置：`domain/video/pre/stage/utils.py:29-62`

问题：这和 `stage8.py`、`stage9.py` 一样属于全局副作用，只是破坏性稍低。

建议：日志配置放到 `pre/main/pipeline.py` 或专门的 logging manager。

### 2. `stage7.py` 把字幕输入硬编码为 `output_dir/total.ass`

位置：`domain/video/pre/stage/stage7.py:215-227`

问题：`stage4.py` 明确会产出 `total.srt`，而 `total.ass` 只是“如果生成了就用”。当前实现没有兜底到 `total.srt`，耦合过死。

建议：先找 `total.ass`，找不到就回退到 `total.srt`，再决定是否转换。

### 3. `normalize_subtitle_numbers()` 把字幕编号从 `0` 开始重排

位置：`domain/video/pre/stage/utils.py:640-674`

问题：标准 SRT 序号通常从 `1` 开始。虽然部分播放器容忍，但这会制造不必要的兼容性风险。

建议：从 `1` 开始编号，并补一组兼容性测试。

### 4. 目录里大量使用 `sys.path.append/insert` 和“包内导入失败再本地导入”的双轨模式

涉及：`stage1.py`、`stage3.py`、`stage4.py`、`stage5.py`、`stage5_0.py`、`stage5_1.py`、`stage6.py`、`stage8.py`、`stage9.py` 等

问题：导入行为取决于当前工作目录和运行方式，难以稳定复现。

建议：把 `domain/video/pre` 做成清晰的可安装包，统一入口执行。

### 5. 交互式输入直接混在阶段逻辑里，自动化能力差

涉及：`stage3.py`、`stage5.py`、`stage6.py`、`stage7.py`、`stage5_1.py`

问题：同一套代码既想做库，又想做交互脚本，导致 CI、批处理、服务化都困难。

建议：阶段函数只接收参数，不直接 `input()`；交互交给 CLI 或 UI 层。

### 6. 模块过大、职责混杂，维护成本高

证据：`stage8.py` 约 67 KB，`stage5_1.py` 约 54 KB，`stage6.py` 约 27 KB。

问题：单文件同时包含路径处理、模型调用、字幕逻辑、视频拼接、异常降级，缺少清晰边界。

建议：按“输入解析、业务服务、外部命令适配、文件管理”拆分。

### 7. 主流程几乎没有自动化测试

现状：当前能明确看到的测试主要是 `subtitle/tests/test_formatter.py` 和 `subtitle/tests/test_parser.py`。

问题：`stage0` 到 `stage9` 的联动、异常分支、降级路径几乎没有保护网。

建议：至少补三层测试。第一层：`utils` 与路径/命令适配单测。第二层：`stage4/5/7/9` 的失败分支单测。第三层：一条最小样例视频的端到端冒烟测试。

### 8. 返回值风格不统一，错误传播方式混乱

现状：有的函数返回 `bool, path`，有的抛异常，有的只 `print`，还有的静默降级。

问题：主流程难以稳定判断“可继续失败”和“必须中止失败”。

建议：统一成明确的结果对象或异常层级，至少规范 `success / artifact / error_message` 三元结构。

## 三、这个目录到底在做什么

从 `domain/video/pre/main/pipeline.py:35-44` 与 `domain/video/pre/main/pipeline.py:470-545` 可以确认，`domain/video/pre/stage` 不是孤立工具集，而是主流程仍在调用的旧式视频预处理流水线。它的职责大致如下。

`stage0.py`

清理 `output` 目录中的 JSON 状态文件，避免上次运行结果污染本次任务。

`stage1.py`

做视频转码，统一编码与音视频参数。

`stage2.py`

调用 `auto-editor` 去静音或去空白片段，产出更短的中间视频。

`stage3.py`

做视频完整性检查与兼容性修复，主要面向封装、尾帧、时间戳异常。

`stage4.py`

做 ASR 识别，输出 `script.txt`、`total.srt`，并尝试接入论坛热词来改善识别效果。

`stage5.py`

让大模型处理识别文本，生成后续剪辑要用的 `clip_text.txt` 等文本产物。

`stage5_0.py`

对长文本做分段预处理，尽量把大模型输入切成更适合处理的段落。

`stage5_1.py`

做逐句或逐段的视频细粒度处理：再次切分、再次识别、再次处理文本、再次裁剪，最后再合并片段。它更像一套“实验性增强流程”。

`stage6.py`

依据 `clip_text` 等结果调用 FunClip 或 videoclipper 的第二阶段做实际剪辑。

`stage7.py` 与 `subtitle/*`

负责字幕校正、字幕样式处理和字幕烧录。

`stage8.py`

根据内容或标题信息生成封面标题画面，把标题页加到视频开头。

`stage9.py`

整理最终产物，把输出文件归档到按原视频名命名的目录，并清理日志和状态文件。

`unified_content_processor.py` 与 `forum_hotword_*.py`

这部分是论坛内容结构化、热词提取、封面标题生成的辅助层，主要服务 `stage4.py` 和 `stage8.py`。

综合来看，这个目录本质上是一套“脚本化、强副作用、依赖外部命令和文件状态”的旧流水线，而不是边界清晰的可复用业务模块。

## 四、建议的整改优先级

### P0，本周必须处理

- 删除 `stage9.py` 中按进程名强杀 `python.exe` 的逻辑。
- 把 `stage4.py` 的 `os.system` 改成参数化 `subprocess.run`。
- 修复 `utils.run_command` 和 `utils.handle_ffmpeg_process` 的管道死锁问题。
- 修复 `stage5.py` 的 `wait_time` 未初始化问题。

### P1，紧随其后

- 移除 `stage8.py`、`stage9.py`、`utils.py` 的全局日志副作用。
- 删除 `stage5_0.py`、`stage5_1.py` 的运行时写源码逻辑。
- 明确 `forum_hotword_extractor_v2.py` 的真实依赖边界。

### P2，结构治理

- 去掉分散的 `sys.path` 操作。
- 拆分超大模块。
- 补主流程测试，尤其是失败和降级路径。

## 五、最终判断

这个目录当前“能跑”，但工程质量明显偏脚本型，且包含多个会导致卡死、误杀进程、全局日志失效、运行时污染源码树的高风险缺陷。

如果按工程风险评估，我会给这一目录打 `高风险，建议先治理再继续叠加功能`。

CloneCut 是面向生产的任务处理平台骨架项目，目标是平滑承接现有 FunClip/TTS 生产链路，并支持后续模块化扩展。

- 已完成目录分层骨架
- 已完成开发基线文档

- 已接入阶段2增量能力：内置 `VideoPipeline`（stage0~9）与 ASR/剪辑基础实现
- 已提供真实样本回归对比与 B1 门槛判定脚本：`scripts/regression_compare.py`、`scripts/regression_gate.py`
- 已提供 nightly 回归门槛 workflow：`.github/workflows/nightly-regression-gate.yml`
- 已补最终验收闭环脚本：`scripts/forum_e2e_regression.py`、`scripts/resource_monitor_benchmark.py`、`scripts/regression_nightly_backfill.py`
- `use_internal_pipeline` 默认已切为 `true`（B1 达标后执行）

- 核心目标已达成，最终验收仍有 3 项待收口（论坛实网回归/监控压测/回归扩样）
- 推荐运行环境：`uv` + Python `3.10.x`（统一使用 `uv` 管理虚拟环境与依赖）

## 快速开始（骨架阶段）

0. 准备环境（推荐统一使用 `uv`）
- `uv python install 3.10`
- `uv venv --python 3.10 .venv`
- `.\.venv\Scripts\Activate.ps1`
- `uv pip install -e ".[asr,llm,forum,test]"`
- 说明：后续命令默认使用 `uv run python ...` 执行，可不依赖激活环境。

1. 复制配置模板
- `config/settings.yaml.example` -> `config/settings.yaml`
- `config/forum_settings.yaml.example` -> `config/forum_settings.yaml`
- `machines.txt.example` -> `machines.txt`

2. 启动监控节点（示例）
- `1-启动监控节点.bat`

3. 启动工作节点（示例）
- `2-启动工作节点.bat`
- 启动脚本默认优先使用 `.venv-t13\Scripts\python.exe`，不存在时回退到 PATH 中的 `python`

4. 高端口联调（防冲突）
- `scripts/3-高端口联调启动.bat`
- `scripts/4-运行冒烟测试.bat`
- `scripts/5-灰度回滚停服.bat`


## 回归门槛（B1）

```powershell
uv run python scripts/regression_compare.py `
  --legacy-dir data/regression/legacy `
  --clonecut-dir data/regression/clonecut `
  --manifest data/regression/manifest/samples_v2_30.json `
  --output-json reports/regression/baseline_v30.json `
  --output-markdown reports/regression/baseline_v30.md `
  --duration-tolerance-seconds 1.0 `
  --frame-tolerance 24 `
  --subtitle-cue-tolerance 2 `
  --subtitle-line-tolerance 4 `
  --audio-duration-tolerance-seconds 1.0
```

```powershell
uv run python scripts/regression_gate.py `
  --report reports/regression/baseline_v30.json `
  --output-json reports/regression/b1_gate_v30.json `
  --output-markdown reports/regression/b1_gate_v30.md `
  --min-samples 30 `
  --min-pass-rate 0.9 `
  --max-subtitle-presence-mismatch-ratio 0.05 `
  --max-duration-frame-exceed-ratio 0.10 `
  --max-fallback-used-ratio 0.10
```

## 最终验收收口脚本（独立执行）

- 论坛实网端到端回归（发现 -> 下载 -> 处理 -> 回帖/附件上传）  
  使用 `clonecut` 自身配置/环境变量，不依赖旧项目路径：

```powershell
$env:FORUM_BASE_URL = "https://your.forum.host"
$env:FORUM_TARGET_URL = "https://your.forum.host/forum-2-1.html"
$env:FORUM_USERNAME = "your_forum_user"
$env:FORUM_PASSWORD = "your_forum_password"
```

```powershell
uv run python scripts/forum_e2e_regression.py `
  --forum-config config/forum_settings.yaml `
  --monitor-url http://127.0.0.1:18200 `
  --worker-url http://127.0.0.1:18205 `
  --cycles 3 `
  --execute-reply `
  --stop-on-failure
```

- 资源监控精度与性能压测（CPU/内存/GPU）：

```powershell
uv run python scripts/resource_monitor_benchmark.py `
  --monitor-interval-seconds 1.0 `
  --sample-interval-seconds 1.0 `
  --cpu-workers 2 `
  --memory-load-mb 512
```

- nightly 失败回灌与长期趋势：

```powershell
uv run python scripts/regression_nightly_backfill.py `
  --report-json reports/regression/baseline_nightly.json `
  --gate-json reports/regression/b1_gate_nightly.json `
  --source-manifest data/regression/manifest/samples_v2_30.json `
  --failed-manifest data/regression/manifest/samples_failed_backfill.json `
  --history-jsonl reports/regression/nightly_history.jsonl `
  --summary-markdown reports/regression/nightly_backfill_summary.md
```

## 可选执行引擎

- TTS/音色克隆内置引擎（默认开启）：`CLONECUT_TTS_ENABLE=true`
- TTS 引擎选择：`CLONECUT_TTS_ENGINE=local|http|auto`（默认 `local`）
- 缺省音色补全（可选）：`CLONECUT_TTS_DEFAULT_VOICE=...`
- 外部视频命令桥接（默认关闭）：`CLONECUT_VIDEO_COMMAND_TEMPLATE=...`
- stage6 可选时长引导：`CLONECUT_STAGE6_DURATION_GUIDE_PATH=...`
- 扩样清单（30样本）：`data/regression/manifest/samples_v2_30.json`

### 内置链路说明（2026-02-26）

- 目标：不依赖旧项目运行时，保持 CloneCut 内置链路可独立运行。
- 行为：
  - `stage4_asr` 只使用 `faster_whisper` / sidecar / timeline fallback；
  - `stage6_clip` 支持文本匹配剪辑与时长引导：
    - 时长引导：`CLONECUT_STAGE6_DURATION_GUIDE_PATH=...`
    - 文本匹配剪辑：`CLONECUT_STAGE6_CLIP_TEXT_MATCH=true`
  - 其余 stage 继续走新架构链路。
  - 严格等价模式：`CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE=true` 时禁止 stage2/4/6/7 的 copy/timeline fallback。
- 验证结果：`uv run python -m pytest -q` -> `72 passed, 1 skipped`（2026-02-26 本地校验）；30 样本独立态回归 `baseline_v30_independent_20260226` 为 `100%`，对应 B1 `b1_gate_v30_independent_20260226` 为 `PASS`。

## 生产并行运行建议

- 旧系统：`8000/8005`
- CloneCut：`8200/8205`
- Redis 前缀：`clonecut_monitor:`、`clonecut_worker:`

### 常见自动生成目录（不纳入主目录树）

- `.venv/`、`.venv-t13/`：本地虚拟环境目录。
- `.pytest_cache/`、`__pycache__/`：测试/解释器缓存目录。
- `.git/`：Git 内部元数据目录。
- `clonecut.egg-info/`：打包元数据目录。
- `data/clonecut.db`：本地运行过程生成的 SQLite 数据库文件。

### 目录解释（按职责）

- `.github/workflows/`：CI/CD 自动化流程；`nightly-regression-gate.yml` 用于 nightly 回归门槛检查。
- `adapters/`：外部系统适配层，只处理“协议/驱动/第三方接口”，不承载业务规则。
- `adapters/forum_discuz/`：论坛发现、抓取、内容处理、回帖的 Discuz 适配实现。
- `adapters/llm/`：多 LLM 供应商实现与工厂路由，统一上层调用方式。
- `adapters/queue_redis/`：Redis 队列与分发队列适配器，负责任务排队/取出。
- `adapters/storage_db/`：SQLite 存储实现（任务、状态等持久化）。
- `adapters/storage_local/`：本地文件系统存储相关适配（轻量占位）。
- `adapters/tts_engine/`：TTS 引擎接入（本地引擎与 HTTP 引擎）。
- `adapters/video_pipeline/`：视频处理命令桥接层（命令组装与执行）。
- `adapters/worker_client_http/`：Monitor 调用 Worker 的 HTTP 客户端。
- `apps/`：应用入口层（进程入口、路由装配、服务启动），是“可运行单元”的边界。
- `apps/api/`：统一 API 入口，常用于健康检查和任务入口聚合。
- `apps/monitor/`：监控节点入口与服务实现，负责任务接入与分发编排。
- `apps/worker/`：工作节点入口与服务实现，负责消费任务并驱动处理流水线。
- `apps/web/`：监控/工作台页面模板、静态资源和演示数据。
- `apps/gradio_ui/`：Gradio UI 启动与后端桥接逻辑。
- `config/`：运行配置文件；`*.example` 是模板，复制后形成本地实际配置。
- `data/`：数据与回归样本资产目录；运行时可能在其中生成 `clonecut.db`。
- `docs/`：项目文档中心，覆盖开发规范、配置规范、测试验证、阶段方案与验收清单。
- `domain/`：领域层，承载核心业务模型和流程，不依赖具体外部实现细节。
- `domain/task/`：任务模型、任务管理、路由与注册逻辑。
- `domain/forum/`：论坛业务对象、配置与集成编排逻辑。
- `domain/video/`：视频主链路；`pipeline.py` 串联 stage0~stage9，`asr/` 与 `subtitle/` 提供子能力。
- `infra/`：基础设施能力（配置加载、日志、健康检查、资源监控、模型管理）。
- `reports/`：测试与验收产物沉淀目录（acceptance/performance/regression）。
- `scripts/`：运维与验收脚本集合；`*.bat` 负责本地快速启动，`*.py` 负责回归与基准。
- `shared/`：跨模块复用的公共类型、错误定义、工具函数。
- `tests/`：测试集合；`unit/` 单元测试，`integration/` 集成测试，`smoke/` 冒烟验证。
- `input/`：待处理输入资源目录（如视频源文件）。
- `output/`：处理结果输出目录（默认产物落盘位置）。
- `logs/`：运行日志目录。
- `.env(.example)`：环境变量模板与本地覆盖。
- `.gitignore`：Git 忽略规则定义文件。
- `check_deps.py`：本地依赖检查脚本（用于快速验证环境完整性）。
- `environment.yml`：Conda 环境定义。
- `machines.txt(.example)`：机器节点配置模板与本地实例。
- `pyproject.toml`：Python 项目元数据、依赖、测试工具配置。

### 阅读顺序建议

- 新同学先读：`README.md` -> 本文（`如何使用.md`）-> `docs/开发文档.md`。
- 想看运行链路：`apps/monitor|worker` -> `domain/task` -> `domain/video/pipeline.py` -> `domain/video/stages/`。
- 想看外部集成：`adapters/` 下按领域进入（forum/llm/tts/queue/storage）。
- 想看质量保障：`tests/` + `scripts/regression_*.py` + `reports/regression/`。

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass, field
import logging
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Callable, Dict, List, Optional

from domain.video.config import VideoPipelineConfig
from domain.video.stages import (
    run_stage0_clean,
    run_stage1_transcode,
    run_stage2_silence,
    run_stage3_repair,
    run_stage4_asr,
    run_stage5_ai_text,
    run_stage6_5_resub,
    run_stage6_clip,
    run_stage7_correct,
    run_stage7_subtitle,
    run_stage8_cover,
    run_stage9_organize,
)
from domain.video.stages.base import StageResult
from domain.video.stages.utils import probe_duration_seconds


@dataclass
class PipelineResult:
    success: bool
    output_file: Optional[str] = None
    error_message: Optional[str] = None
    executed_stages: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    performance_summary: str = ""
    current_stage: int = 0
    last_stage: Optional[str] = None
    failed_stage: Optional[str] = None
    performance_report: Optional[Any] = None


class VideoPipeline:
    """Internal multi-stage video pipeline."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        config: VideoPipelineConfig,
        logger: Optional[logging.Logger] = None,
        performance_tracker: Any = None,
        resource_monitor: Any = None,
    ) -> None:
        self.config = config
        self.logger = logger or logging.getLogger("clonecut.domain.video.pipeline")
        self.performance_tracker = performance_tracker
        self.resource_monitor = resource_monitor
        self._stages: List[tuple[str, Callable[..., StageResult]]] = [
            ("stage0_clean", self._stage0),
            ("stage1_transcode", self._stage1),
            ("stage2_silence", self._stage2),
            ("stage3_repair", self._stage3),
            ("stage4_asr", self._stage4),
            ("stage5_ai_text", self._stage5),
            ("stage6_clip", self._stage6),
            ("stage6_5_resub", self._stage6_5),
            ("stage7_correct", self._stage7_correct),
            ("stage7_subtitle", self._stage7),
            ("stage8_cover", self._stage8),
            ("stage9_organize", self._stage9),
        ]

    def run(
        self,
        input_video: str,
        task_id: str,
        start_from_stage: int = 0,
        forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
    ) -> PipelineResult:
        current = input_video
        executed: List[str] = []
        stage_start = max(0, int(start_from_stage))
        context: Dict[str, Any] = {"forum_post_info": _normalize_forum_post_info(forum_post_info)}
        last_stage_index = max(0, min(stage_start, len(self._stages) - 1 if self._stages else 0))
        last_stage_name: Optional[str] = None
        gpu_stage_indexes = {1, 2, 4, 6}
        tracking_started = False

        if self.performance_tracker is not None:
            try:
                path = Path(input_video)
                file_size_mb = 0.0
                if path.exists():
                    file_size_mb = path.stat().st_size / (1024 * 1024)
                duration_seconds = probe_duration_seconds(input_video)
                self.performance_tracker.start_video_processing(
                    task_id=task_id,
                    video_filename=path.name,
                    original_filename=path.name,
                    file_size_mb=file_size_mb,
                    video_duration_seconds=duration_seconds,
                )
                tracking_started = True
            except Exception as exc:
                self.logger.warning("start performance tracking failed: task=%s err=%s", task_id, exc)

        for idx, (stage_name, handler) in enumerate(self._stages):
            if idx < stage_start:
                continue

            if self.resource_monitor is not None:
                try:
                    self.resource_monitor.record_step_resource(
                        step_num=idx,
                        step_name=stage_name,
                        task_id=task_id,
                    )
                except Exception as exc:
                    self.logger.debug("resource snapshot failed: task=%s stage=%s err=%s", task_id, stage_name, exc)
            if self.performance_tracker is not None:
                try:
                    self.performance_tracker.start_stage(
                        task_id=task_id,
                        stage_name=stage_name,
                        gpu_accelerated=(idx in gpu_stage_indexes),
                    )
                except Exception:
                    pass
            try:
                result = handler(current, task_id=task_id, stage_name=stage_name, context=context)
            except Exception as exc:
                if self.performance_tracker is not None:
                    try:
                        self.performance_tracker.end_stage(
                            task_id=task_id,
                            stage_name=stage_name,
                            success=False,
                            error_message=str(exc),
                        )
                        self.performance_tracker.add_error(task_id, str(exc))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                perf_report = self._finish_tracking(task_id, tracking_started)
                return PipelineResult(
                    success=False,
                    output_file=current,
                    error_message=f"{stage_name} exception: {exc}",
                    executed_stages=executed,
                    current_stage=idx,
                    last_stage=last_stage_name,
                    failed_stage=stage_name,
                    performance_report=perf_report,
                )

            executed.append(stage_name)
            last_stage_index = idx
            last_stage_name = stage_name
            if not result.success:
                if self.performance_tracker is not None:
                    try:
                        self.performance_tracker.end_stage(
                            task_id=task_id,
                            stage_name=stage_name,
                            success=False,
                            error_message=str(result.error_message or ""),
                        )
                        self.performance_tracker.add_error(
                            task_id,
                            str(result.error_message or f"{stage_name} failed"),
                        )
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                perf_report = self._finish_tracking(task_id, tracking_started)
                return PipelineResult(
                    success=False,
                    output_file=current,
                    error_message=result.error_message or f"{stage_name} failed",
                    executed_stages=executed,
                    current_stage=idx,
                    last_stage=last_stage_name,
                    failed_stage=stage_name,
                    performance_report=perf_report,
                )
            if self.performance_tracker is not None:
                try:
                    self.performance_tracker.end_stage(
                        task_id=task_id,
                        stage_name=stage_name,
                        success=True,
                    )
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if result.output_file:
                current = result.output_file

        perf_report = self._finish_tracking(task_id, tracking_started)
        summary = f"internal pipeline executed stages={len(executed)}"
        if perf_report is not None:
            try:
                ratio = float(getattr(perf_report, "processing_speed_ratio", 0.0))
                if ratio > 0:
                    summary = f"internal pipeline executed stages={len(executed)} speed={ratio:.2f}x"
            except Exception:
                pass
        return PipelineResult(
            success=True,
            output_file=current,
            executed_stages=executed,
            performance_summary=summary,
            current_stage=last_stage_index,
            last_stage=last_stage_name,
            performance_report=perf_report,
        )

    def _finish_tracking(self, task_id: str, tracking_started: bool) -> Optional[Any]:
        if not tracking_started or self.performance_tracker is None:
            return None
        try:
            return self.performance_tracker.end_video_processing(task_id)
        except Exception:
            return None

    def _stage0(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage0_clean(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage1(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage1_transcode(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage2(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage2_silence(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage3(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage3_repair(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage4(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        forum_info = context.get("forum_post_info") or {}
        hotwords = _normalize_hotwords(forum_info.get("hotwords"))
        speaker = str(forum_info.get("speaker", "")).strip()
        return run_stage4_asr(
            current,
            self.config.output_dir,
            task_id,
            forum_post_info=forum_info,
            hotwords=hotwords,
            speaker=speaker,
        )

    def _stage5(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage5_ai_text(
            current,
            self.config.output_dir,
            task_id,
            forum_post_info=context.get("forum_post_info") or {},
        )

    def _stage6(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage6_clip(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage6_5(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage6_5_resub(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage7_correct(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage7_correct(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage7(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage7_subtitle(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage8(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        forum_info = _normalize_forum_post_info(context.get("forum_post_info"))
        context["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
        return run_stage8_cover(
            current,
            self.config.output_dir,
            task_id,
            forum_post_info=forum_info,
        )

    def _stage9(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        forum_info = _normalize_forum_post_info(context.get("forum_post_info"))
        original_filename = str(forum_info.get("original_filename", "")).strip()
        return run_stage9_organize(
            current,
            output_dir=self.config.output_dir,
            task_id=task_id,
            keep_intermediate_files=self.config.keep_intermediate_files,
            forum_post_info=forum_info,
            original_filename=original_filename,
        )


def _normalize_forum_post_info(raw: Optional[dict]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    if not isinstance(raw, dict):
        return {}

    info: Dict[str, Any] = dict(raw)
    hotwords = _normalize_hotwords(info.get("hotwords"))
    info["hotwords"] = hotwords

    speaker = _pick_first_text(
        info,
        keys=("speaker", "speaker_id", "spk", "target_speaker"),
    )
    if speaker:
        info["speaker"] = speaker

    cover_titles = _normalize_cover_titles(info.get("cover_titles"))
    cover_up = _pick_first_text(info, keys=("cover_title_up", "封面标题上"))
    cover_middle = _pick_first_text(info, keys=("cover_title_middle", "封面标题中"))
    cover_down = _pick_first_text(info, keys=("cover_title_down", "封面标题下"))

    if not cover_up and len(cover_titles) >= 1:
        cover_up = cover_titles[0]
    if not cover_middle and len(cover_titles) >= 2:
        cover_middle = cover_titles[1]
    if not cover_down and len(cover_titles) >= 3:
        cover_down = cover_titles[2]

    compact_titles = [item for item in (cover_up, cover_middle, cover_down) if item]
    if compact_titles:
        cover_titles = compact_titles

    info["cover_title_up"] = cover_up
    info["cover_title_middle"] = cover_middle
    info["cover_title_down"] = cover_down
    info["封面标题上"] = cover_up
    info["封面标题中"] = cover_middle
    info["封面标题下"] = cover_down
    info["cover_titles"] = cover_titles

    return info


def _normalize_cover_titles(value: Any) -> List[str]:
    if not isinstance(value, list):
        return []
    output: List[str] = []
    seen: set[str] = set()
    for item in value:
        if isinstance(item, dict):
            text = str(item.get("text", "")).strip()
        else:
            text = str(item or "").strip()
        normalized = " ".join(text.split())
        if not normalized:
            continue
        if normalized in seen:
            continue
        seen.add(normalized)
        output.append(normalized)
        if len(output) >= 3:
            break
    return output


def _normalize_hotwords(value: Any) -> List[str]:
    candidates: List[str] = []
    if isinstance(value, list):
        candidates = [str(item).strip() for item in value]
    elif isinstance(value, str):
        candidates = [item.strip() for item in value.replace("\uFF0C", ",").split(",")]

    output: List[str] = []
    seen: set[str] = set()
    for item in candidates:
        text = str(item or "").strip()
        if not text:
            continue
        dedup_key = text.lower()
        if dedup_key in seen:
            continue
        seen.add(dedup_key)
        output.append(text)
    return output


def _pick_first_text(info: Dict[str, Any], keys: tuple[str, ...]) -> str:
    for key in keys:
        value = str(info.get(key, "")).strip()
        if value:
            return value
    return ""

def create_app(service: WorkerService) -> Flask:
    app = Flask(
        __name__,
        template_folder=str(TEMPLATE_DIR),
        static_folder=str(STATIC_DIR),
        static_url_path="/web/static",
    )
    if app.jinja_loader is not None:
        app.jinja_loader = ChoiceLoader([app.jinja_loader, FileSystemLoader(str(TEMPLATE_DIR))])

    _api_token: str = os.getenv("CLONECUT_API_TOKEN", "").strip()
    _web_mock_mode = os.getenv("CLONECUT_WEB_MOCK_MODE", "").strip().lower() == "true"

    def _mock_mode_from_request() -> bool:
        if _web_mock_mode:
            return True
        raw = request.args.get("mock", "").strip().lower()
        return raw in {"1", "true", "yes"}

    def _require_token(f):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        @wraps(f)
        def decorated(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> Any:
            if not _api_token:
                return f(*args, **kwargs)
            auth = request.headers.get("Authorization", "")
            token = auth.removeprefix("Bearer ").strip() if auth.startswith("Bearer ") else ""
            if not token:
                token = request.args.get("token", "").strip()
            if token != _api_token:
                return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "unauthorized"}), 401
            return f(*args, **kwargs)

        return decorated

    @app.get("/")
    def dashboard() -> Any:
        return render_worker_dashboard(
            {
                "page_title": "CloneCut API Dashboard",
                "dashboard_mode": "worker",
                "api_base": "/api",
                "mock_mode": "true" if _mock_mode_from_request() else "false",
            }
        )

    @app.get("/web/worker")
    def worker_dashboard() -> Any:
        return render_worker_dashboard(
            {
                "page_title": "CloneCut API Dashboard",
                "dashboard_mode": "worker",
                "api_base": "/api",
                "mock_mode": "true" if _mock_mode_from_request() else "false",
            }
        )

    @app.get("/health")
    def health() -> Any:
        return jsonify({"status": "ok", "service": "api"})

    @app.get("/api/ping")
    def ping() -> Any:
        return jsonify({"success": True, "message": "clonecut api online"})

    @app.get("/web/mock/worker/status")
    def mock_worker_status() -> Any:
        return jsonify({"success": True, **build_worker_status()})

    @app.get("/web/mock/worker/resources")
    def mock_worker_resources() -> Any:
        return jsonify({"success": True, "resources": build_worker_resources()})

    @app.get("/web/mock/worker/tasks")
    def mock_worker_tasks() -> Any:
        limit_raw = request.args.get("limit", "10")
        try:
            limit = max(1, min(200, int(limit_raw)))
        except ValueError:
            limit = 10
        tasks = build_worker_tasks(limit=limit)
        return jsonify({"success": True, "tasks": tasks, "total": len(tasks), "limit": limit, "offset": 0})

    @app.post("/web/mock/worker/tasks")
    def mock_worker_submit() -> Any:
        payload = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}
        source_url = str(payload.get("source_url", "")).strip()
        if not source_url:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "missing source_url"}), 400
        task_id = f"mock-submit-{datetime.now().strftime('%H%M%S')}-{uuid.uuid4().hex[:6]}"
        return jsonify({"success": True, "task_id": task_id}), 201

    @app.get("/api/status")
    def status() -> Any:
        return jsonify({"success": True, **service.get_status()})

    @app.get("/api/queues")
    def queue_status() -> Any:
        payload = service.get_status()
        return jsonify(
            {
                "success": True,
                "queue_sizes": payload.get("queue_sizes", {}),
                "queues": payload.get("queues", {}),
                "task_status_counts": payload.get("task_status_counts", {}),
                "timestamp": payload.get("timestamp"),
            }
        )

    @app.get("/api/resources")
    def resources_current() -> Any:
        return jsonify({"success": True, "resources": service.get_resources()})

    @app.get("/api/resources/history")
    def resources_history() -> Any:
        try:
            minutes = max(1, min(1440, int(request.args.get("minutes", "60"))))
        except ValueError:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "invalid minutes param"}), 400
        return jsonify(
            {"success": True, "minutes": minutes, "history": service.get_resources_history(minutes=minutes)}
        )

    @app.get("/api/tasks")
    def list_tasks() -> Any:
        status = request.args.get("status")
        limit_raw = request.args.get("limit", "20")
        offset_raw = request.args.get("offset", "0")
        try:
            limit = max(1, min(200, int(limit_raw)))
            offset = max(0, int(offset_raw))
        except ValueError:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "invalid pagination params"}), 400

        try:
            payload = service.list_tasks(status=status, limit=limit, offset=offset)
        except ValueError as exc:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": str(exc)}), 400
        return jsonify({"success": True, **payload})

    @app.post("/api/tasks")
    @_require_token
    def create_task() -> Any:
        data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}
        ok, task_id, error = service.submit(data)
        if not ok:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": error or "invalid task payload"}), 400
        return jsonify({"success": True, "task_id": task_id}), 201

    @app.get("/api/tasks/<task_id>")
    def task_detail(task_id: str) -> Any:
        task = service.get_task(task_id)
        if task is None:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "task not found"}), 404
        return jsonify({"success": True, "task": task})

    @app.post("/api/tasks/<task_id>/cancel")
    @_require_token
    def cancel_task(task_id: str) -> Any:
        ok, error = service.cancel_task(task_id)
        if not ok:
            code = 404 if error == "task not found" else 409
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": error}), code
        return jsonify({"success": True, "task_id": task_id})

    @app.post("/api/tasks/<task_id>/retry")
    @_require_token
    def retry_task(task_id: str) -> Any:
        ok, error = service.retry_task(task_id)
        if not ok:
            code = 404 if error == "task not found" else 409
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": error}), code
        return jsonify({"success": True, "task_id": task_id})

    return app


def _run_http(app: Flask, host: str, port: int, logger: logging.Logger) -> None:
    try:
        from waitress import serve

        logger.info("serving with waitress on %s:%s", host, port)
        serve(app, host=host, port=port)
    except Exception:
        logger.info("waitress unavailable, fallback to flask builtin server on %s:%s", host, port)
        app.run(host=host, port=port, debug=False, use_reloader=False)


def main() -> int:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="CloneCut API service")
    parser.add_argument("--port", type=int, default=None, help="override service port")
    parser.add_argument("--host", type=str, default=None, help="override service host")
    parser.add_argument("--config", type=str, default="config/settings.yaml", help="config path")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    cfg = load_app_config(args.config)
    cfg.role = "api"
    cfg.port = args.port or cfg.port
    cfg.host = args.host or cfg.host
    if cfg.redis_namespace == "clonecut_monitor:":
        cfg.redis_namespace = "clonecut_worker:"

    setup_logging(cfg.log_dir, cfg.role)
    logger = logging.getLogger("apps.api")
    logger.info("api booting env=%s host=%s port=%s", cfg.env, cfg.host, cfg.port)

    service = WorkerService(config=cfg, logger=logger)
    app = create_app(service)
    _run_http(app, cfg.host, cfg.port, logger)
    return 0


if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

class RetryableUploadError(RuntimeError):
    """Upload failure that should be retried by queue scheduler."""


class NonRetryableUploadError(RuntimeError):
    """Upload failure that must not be retried by queue scheduler."""


class WorkerService:
    def __init__(self, config: Any, logger: Optional[logging.Logger] = None) -> None:
        self.config = config
        self.logger = logger or logging.getLogger("clonecut.worker.service")
        self.booted_at = time.time()
        self.redis_client = build_redis_client(
            host=str(getattr(config, "redis_host", "127.0.0.1")),
            port=int(getattr(config, "redis_port", 6379)),
            db=int(getattr(config, "redis_db", 0)),
            password=str(getattr(config, "redis_password", "")),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.registry = RedisTaskRegistry(
            redis_client=self.redis_client,
            namespace=str(getattr(config, "redis_namespace", "clonecut_worker:")),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.dedup_ttl_seconds = max(60, int(self._get_queue_cfg("dedup_ttl_seconds", 24 * 3600)))
        self.queue_adapter = RedisQueueAdapter(
            redis_client=self.redis_client,
            namespace=str(getattr(config, "redis_namespace", "clonecut_worker:")),
            dedup_ttl_seconds=self.dedup_ttl_seconds,
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.use_redis_queue = self.queue_adapter.is_persistent()
        self.task_storage = self._init_task_storage()
        self.lock = RLock()
        self.stop_event = Event()
        self.worker_threads: List[Thread] = []
        self.active_workers: Dict[str, int] = {
            "download": 0,
            "process": 0,
            "upload": 0,
        }

        self.stats: Dict[str, int] = {
            "received": 0,
            "completed": 0,
            "failed": 0,
            "running": 0,
            "retried": 0,
            "zombie_reclaimed": 0,
        }

        self.max_download_workers = max(1, int(self._get_worker_cfg("max_download_workers", 2)))
        self.max_process_workers = max(1, int(self._get_worker_cfg("max_process_workers", 2)))
        self.max_upload_workers = max(1, int(self._get_worker_cfg("max_upload_workers", 2)))
        self.download_timeout_seconds = max(
            30,
            int(self._get_worker_cfg("download_timeout_seconds", 600)),
        )
        self.download_chunk_size = max(
            1024,
            int(self._get_worker_cfg("download_chunk_size", 8192)),

        self.active_task_ids: set[str] = set()
