                self.upload_storage_backend,
            )
            self.upload_storage_backend = "local"
        self.storage_adapter: UploadStorageAdapter = build_default_storage_adapter(
            upload_root=str(self.upload_root),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.forum_upload_enabled = self._bool_cfg(
            os.getenv("CLONECUT_FORUM_UPLOAD_ENABLED"),
            bool(self._get_worker_cfg("forum_upload_enabled", True)),
        )
        self.forum_reply_content = str(
            self._get_worker_cfg("forum_reply_content", "Video processing completed")
        ).strip() or "Video processing completed"
        self.forum_settings_path = str(
            self._get_worker_cfg("forum_settings_path", "config/forum_settings.yaml")
        ).strip() or "config/forum_settings.yaml"

        self.tts_adapter_enabled = self._bool_cfg(
            os.getenv("CLONECUT_TTS_ENABLE"),
            bool(self._get_worker_cfg("tts_enable", True)),
        )
        tts_engine_mode_raw = str(
            os.getenv("CLONECUT_TTS_ENGINE", self._get_worker_cfg("tts_engine", "local"))
        ).strip().lower()
        if tts_engine_mode_raw not in {"local", "http", "auto"}:
            tts_engine_mode_raw = "local"
        self.tts_engine_mode = tts_engine_mode_raw
        tts_default_voice = str(self._get_worker_cfg("tts_default_voice", ""))
        tts_api_endpoint = str(self._get_worker_cfg("tts_api_endpoint", ""))
        tts_api_timeout_raw = self._get_worker_cfg("tts_api_timeout_seconds", 15)
        tts_local_sample_rate_raw = self._get_worker_cfg("tts_local_sample_rate_hz", 24000)
        try:
            tts_api_timeout = float(tts_api_timeout_raw)
        except Exception:
            tts_api_timeout = 15.0
        try:
            tts_local_sample_rate = int(tts_local_sample_rate_raw)
        except Exception:
            tts_local_sample_rate = 24000
        tts_local_sample_rate_env = os.getenv(
            "CLONECUT_TTS_LOCAL_SAMPLE_RATE_HZ",
            str(tts_local_sample_rate),
        )
        try:
            tts_local_sample_rate_value = int(tts_local_sample_rate_env)
        except Exception:
            tts_local_sample_rate_value = tts_local_sample_rate
        self.tts_local_adapter = LocalTtsAdapter(
            enabled=self.tts_adapter_enabled,
            output_dir=self.config.output_dir,
            default_voice=os.getenv("CLONECUT_TTS_DEFAULT_VOICE", tts_default_voice),
            sample_rate_hz=tts_local_sample_rate_value,
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.tts_http_adapter = HttpTtsAdapter(
            enabled=self.tts_adapter_enabled,
            default_voice=os.getenv("CLONECUT_TTS_DEFAULT_VOICE", tts_default_voice),
            api_endpoint=os.getenv("CLONECUT_TTS_API_ENDPOINT", tts_api_endpoint),
            api_timeout_seconds=float(
                os.getenv("CLONECUT_TTS_API_TIMEOUT_SECONDS", str(tts_api_timeout))
            ),
            logger=self.logger,
        )

        video_cmd = str(self._get_worker_cfg("video_command_template", ""))
        video_timeout_raw = self._get_worker_cfg("video_command_timeout_seconds", 7200)
        try:
            video_timeout = int(video_timeout_raw)
        except Exception:
            video_timeout = 7200
        self.video_adapter = ExternalVideoCommandAdapter(
            output_dir=self.config.output_dir,
            command_template=os.getenv("CLONECUT_VIDEO_COMMAND_TEMPLATE", video_cmd),
            timeout_seconds=int(
                os.getenv("CLONECUT_VIDEO_COMMAND_TIMEOUT_SECONDS", str(video_timeout))
            ),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.internal_pipeline_enabled = self._bool_cfg(
            os.getenv("CLONECUT_USE_INTERNAL_PIPELINE"),
            bool(self._get_worker_cfg("use_internal_pipeline", False)),
        )

        # --- telemetry ---
        telemetry_interval = float(self._get_worker_cfg("resource_monitor_interval_seconds", 5.0))
        report_dir = str(self._get_worker_cfg("performance_report_dir", "logs/performance_reports"))
        self.resource_monitor = ResourceMonitor(
            interval_seconds=telemetry_interval,
            disk_path=str(self.config.output_dir),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.performance_tracker = PerformanceTracker(resource_monitor=self.resource_monitor)
        self.report_generator = ReportGenerator(report_dir=report_dir, logger=self.logger)

    def start(self) -> None:
        if any(thread.is_alive() for thread in self.worker_threads):
            return

        self.resource_monitor.start()
        recovered = self._recover_stuck_tasks()
        restored_retries = self._restore_retry_schedule()
        self.stop_event.clear()
        self.worker_threads = []
        self._spawn_workers("download", self.max_download_workers, self._download_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("process", self.max_process_workers, self._process_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("upload", self.max_upload_workers, self._upload_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("retry", 1, self._retry_scheduler_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("zombie", 1, self._zombie_cleaner_loop)

        self.logger.info(
            "worker adapters: tts_enabled=%s tts_engine=%s tts_http_ready=%s video_cmd_enabled=%s internal_pipeline=%s redis_registry=%s redis_queue=%s recovered=%s restored_retries=%s",
            self.tts_adapter_enabled,
            self.tts_engine_mode,
            self.tts_http_adapter.is_ready(),
            self.video_adapter.is_enabled(),
            self.internal_pipeline_enabled,
            self.registry.is_persistent(),
            self.use_redis_queue,
            recovered,
            restored_retries,
        )
        self.logger.info(
            "worker pools started: download=%s process=%s upload=%s retry_scheduler=%s zombie_timeout=%ss zombie_by_status=%s",
            self.max_download_workers,
            self.max_process_workers,
            self.max_upload_workers,
            1,
            self.zombie_timeout_seconds,
            self.zombie_timeout_by_status_seconds,
        )

    def stop(self) -> None:
        self.stop_event.set()
        for thread in self.worker_threads:
            thread.join(timeout=2.0)
        self.resource_monitor.stop()
        self.logger.info("worker service stopped")

    def submit(self, raw_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, str, Optional[str]]:
        try:
            task = self._build_task(raw_data)
        except ValueError as exc:
            return False, "", str(exc)

        existing_task_id = self.queue_adapter.check_duplicate(task)
        if existing_task_id:
            self.logger.info(
                "duplicate task ignored: incoming=%s existing=%s",
                task.task_id,
                existing_task_id,
            )
            return True, existing_task_id, None

        self._persist_task(task)
        self.queue_adapter.remember_dedup(task, ttl_seconds=self.dedup_ttl_seconds)
        self._enqueue_task(self._initial_queue_for_task(task), task)

        with self.lock:
            self.stats["received"] += 1

        self.logger.info(
            "task received: task_id=%s type=%s queued=%s",
            task.task_id,
            task.task_type.value,
            self._initial_queue_for_task(task),
        )
        return True, task.task_id, None

    def get_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        queue_sizes = self.queue_adapter.get_queue_sizes()
        queued_total = (
            int(queue_sizes.get("download", 0))
            + int(queue_sizes.get("process", 0))
            + int(queue_sizes.get("upload", 0))
        )
        task_status_counts = self.get_task_status_counts()

        with self.lock:
            running = sum(self.active_workers.values())
            stats = dict(self.stats)
            active_workers = dict(self.active_workers)
        active_task_count = (
            int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.PENDING.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.ASSIGNED.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value, 0))
        )
        status_metrics = {
            "total": int(task_status_counts.get("total", 0)),
            "completed": int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.COMPLETED.value, 0)),
            "failed": int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.FAILED.value, 0)),
            "active": int(active_task_count),
            "zombie": int(stats["zombie_reclaimed"]),
            "retried": int(stats["retried"]),
            "received": int(stats["received"]),
        }

        return {
            "status": "online",
            "is_busy": running > 0 or queued_total > 0,
            "total_queue_size": queued_total + running,
            "queue_sizes": queue_sizes,
            "queues": {
                "download": int(queue_sizes.get("download", 0)),
                "process": int(queue_sizes.get("process", 0)),
                "upload": int(queue_sizes.get("upload", 0)),
                "pending": queued_total,
                "processing": active_workers.get("process", 0),
                "completed": stats["completed"],
                "failed": stats["failed"],
                "retried": stats["retried"],
                "received": stats["received"],
                "active": active_task_count,
                "total": int(task_status_counts.get("total", 0)),
                "zombie_reclaimed": stats["zombie_reclaimed"],
                "zombie": stats["zombie_reclaimed"],
            },
            "workers": active_workers,
            "status_metrics": status_metrics,
            "task_status_counts": task_status_counts,
            "uptime_seconds": int(max(0, time.time() - self.booted_at)),
            "timestamp": time.time(),
        }

    def get_resources(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return self.resource_monitor.get_current()

    def get_resources_history(self, minutes: int = 60) -> list:
        return self.resource_monitor.get_history(minutes=minutes)

    def get_task(self, task_id: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        task = self.registry.get(task_id)
        if task is None:
            return None
        return task.to_dict()

    def get_task_status_counts(self) -> Dict[str, int]:
        counts: Dict[str, int] = {}
        for status in self._queryable_statuses():
            counts[status.value] = int(self.registry.count_by_status(status))
        counts["total"] = sum(counts.values())
        return counts

    def list_tasks(
        self,
        status: Optional[str] = None,
        limit: int = 20,
        offset: int = 0,
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        size = max(1, min(200, int(limit)))
        start = max(0, int(offset))
        target_statuses = self._resolve_status_filter(status)
        read_limit = min(5000, start + size)

        if len(target_statuses) == 1:
            selected = target_statuses[0]
            total = int(self.registry.count_by_status(selected))
            tasks = self.registry.list_by_status(selected, limit=max(1, read_limit))
        else:
            total = 0
            merged: Dict[str, UnifiedTask] = {}
            for st in target_statuses:
                total += int(self.registry.count_by_status(st))
                for task in self.registry.list_by_status(st, limit=max(1, read_limit)):
                    merged[task.task_id] = task
            tasks = list(merged.values())
            tasks.sort(key=lambda item: item.created_at, reverse=True)

        selected_tasks = tasks[start : start + size]
        return {
            "total": total,
            "limit": size,
            "offset": start,
            "tasks": [item.to_dict() for item in selected_tasks],
        }

    def cancel_task(self, task_id: str) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        task = self.registry.get(task_id)
        if task is None:
            return False, "task not found"
        if task.status == TaskStatus.CANCELLED:
            return True, ""
        if task.status == TaskStatus.COMPLETED:
            return False, "completed task cannot be cancelled"
        if task.status in {TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING, TaskStatus.PROCESSING, TaskStatus.UPLOADING}:
            return False, f"task is running in status={task.status.value}, cannot be cancelled safely"

        transitioned = self._transition_status(task, TaskStatus.CANCELLED, strict=False)
        if not transitioned:
            return False, f"illegal transition: {task.status.value} -> cancelled"
        task.stage_checkpoint = "cancelled"
        task.error_message = None
        task.metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        task.metadata["cancelled_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
        self._persist_task(task)
        return True, ""

    def retry_task(self, task_id: str) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        task = self.registry.get(task_id)
        if task is None:
            return False, "task not found"
        if task.status != TaskStatus.FAILED:
            return False, f"only failed task can retry, current={task.status.value}"

        self._remove_retry_schedule(task.task_id)
        if int(task.retry_count) >= int(task.max_retries):
            task.max_retries = int(task.retry_count) + 1

        task.metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        task.metadata["manual_retry"] = True
        task.metadata["manual_retry_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
        self._enqueue_retry_task(task)
        with self.lock:
            self.stats["retried"] += 1
        return True, ""

    def _download_loop(self) -> None:
        while not self.stop_event.is_set():
            task = self._dequeue_stage_task("download")
            if task is None:
                continue
            self._mark_stage_active("download", +1)
            self._mark_task_active(task.task_id, True)
            try:
                self._ru…13332 tokens truncated…      payload.get("hotwords"),
            metadata.get("hotwords"),
            merged.get("keywords"),
            payload.get("keywords"),
            metadata.get("keywords"),
        )
        if hotwords:
            merged["hotwords"] = hotwords

        cover_up = self._pick_first_text(
            merged.get("cover_title_up"),
            merged.get("封面标题上"),
            payload.get("cover_title_up"),
            payload.get("封面标题上"),
            metadata.get("cover_title_up"),
            metadata.get("封面标题上"),
        )
        cover_middle = self._pick_first_text(
            merged.get("cover_title_middle"),
            merged.get("封面标题中"),
            payload.get("cover_title_middle"),
            payload.get("封面标题中"),
            metadata.get("cover_title_middle"),
            metadata.get("封面标题中"),
        )
        cover_down = self._pick_first_text(
            merged.get("cover_title_down"),
            merged.get("封面标题下"),
            payload.get("cover_title_down"),
            payload.get("封面标题下"),
            metadata.get("cover_title_down"),
            metadata.get("封面标题下"),
        )

        cover_titles = self._normalize_text_list(merged.get("cover_titles"))
        if not cover_up and len(cover_titles) >= 1:
            cover_up = cover_titles[0]
        if not cover_middle and len(cover_titles) >= 2:
            cover_middle = cover_titles[1]
        if not cover_down and len(cover_titles) >= 3:
            cover_down = cover_titles[2]

        compact_titles = [text for text in (cover_up, cover_middle, cover_down) if text]
        if compact_titles:
            merged["cover_titles"] = compact_titles
            merged["cover_title_up"] = cover_up
            merged["cover_title_middle"] = cover_middle
            merged["cover_title_down"] = cover_down
            merged["封面标题上"] = cover_up
            merged["封面标题中"] = cover_middle
            merged["封面标题下"] = cover_down

        speaker = self._pick_first_text(
            merged.get("speaker"),
            merged.get("speaker_id"),
            merged.get("spk"),
            merged.get("target_speaker"),
        )
        if speaker:
            merged["speaker"] = speaker

        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
            forum_post_info=merged,
            payload=payload,
            metadata=metadata,
            source_url="",
        )
        if original_filename:
            merged["original_filename"] = original_filename
        return merged

    def _normalize_text_list(self, *values: Any) -> List[str]:
        output: List[str] = []
        seen: set[str] = set()
        for value in values:
            items: List[str] = []
            if isinstance(value, list):
                items = [str(item or "").strip() for item in value]
            elif isinstance(value, str):
                items = [item.strip() for item in value.replace("\uFF0C", ",").split(",")]
            for item in items:
                normalized = " ".join(item.split())
                if not normalized:
                    continue
                dedup_key = normalized.lower()
                if dedup_key in seen:
                    continue
                seen.add(dedup_key)
                output.append(normalized)
        return output

    def _pick_first_text(self, *values: Any) -> str:
        for value in values:
            text = str(value or "").strip()
            if text:
                return text
        return ""

    def _sanitize_filename(self, value: str) -> str:
        text = str(value or "").strip()
        if not text:
            return ""
        text = text.replace("\\", "/").split("/")[-1].strip()
        text = re.sub(r"[\x00-\x1f]", "", text)
        text = re.sub(r"[<>:\"/\\\\|?*]+", "_", text)
        text = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", text).strip().strip(".")
        return text

    def _init_task_storage(self) -> Optional[SqliteStorageAdapter]:
        db_path = os.getenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", "data/clonecut.db")
        try:
            return SqliteStorageAdapter(db_path=db_path, logger=self.logger)
        except Exception as exc:
            self.logger.warning("sqlite storage disabled: %s", exc)
            return None

    def _save_task_snapshot(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        self._sync_task_metadata(task)
        if self.task_storage is None:
            return
        self.task_storage.save_task(task)

    def _persist_task(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        self._sync_task_metadata(task)
        self.registry.add(task)
        self._save_task_snapshot(task)

    def _sync_task_metadata(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        metadata["current_stage"] = int(task.current_stage)
        metadata["max_retries"] = int(task.max_retries)
        metadata["retry_count"] = int(task.retry_count)
        if task.stage_checkpoint:
            metadata["stage_checkpoint"] = task.stage_checkpoint
        else:
            metadata.pop("stage_checkpoint", None)
        task.metadata = metadata

    def _transition_status(self, task: UnifiedTask, status: TaskStatus, strict: bool = True) -> bool:
        result = self.registry.update_status(task.task_id, status)
        if result.ok:
            task.status = status
            if status in {TaskStatus.PENDING, TaskStatus.FAILED, TaskStatus.CANCELLED}:
                task.started_at = None
            return True
        if strict:
            raise RuntimeError(result.reason or f"status transition failed: {task.task_id}")
        return False

    def _mark_task_active(self, task_id: str, active: bool) -> None:
        with self.lock:
            if active:
                self.active_task_ids.add(task_id)
            else:
                self.active_task_ids.discard(task_id)

    def _schedule_retry(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> bool:
        if task.status != TaskStatus.FAILED:
            return False
        retryable = bool((task.metadata or {}).get("retryable_failure", True))
        if not retryable:
            return False
        max_retries = max(0, int(task.max_retries))
        if task.retry_count >= max_retries:
            return False

        delay = self._retry_delay_seconds(task, task.retry_count)
        retry_count = task.retry_count + 1
        due_at = time.time() + delay
        task.retry_count = retry_count
        task.metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        task.metadata["retry_due_at"] = due_at
        task.metadata["retry_delay_seconds"] = delay
        self._persist_task(task)

        with self.lock:
            self.retry_index[task.task_id] = (due_at, task)
            heapq.heappush(self.retry_heap, (due_at, task.task_id))
            self.stats["retried"] += 1
        return True

    def _retry_delay_seconds(self, task: UnifiedTask, retry_count_before_increment: int) -> int:
        failed_from = str((task.metadata or {}).get("failed_from_status", "")).strip().lower()
        backoff = self.retry_backoff_seconds or [5]
        if failed_from == TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value:
            backoff = self.upload_retry_backoff_seconds or [1, 2, 4]
        idx = min(max(0, int(retry_count_before_increment)), len(backoff) - 1)
        return int(backoff[idx])

    def _is_retryable_failure(self, error: Exception, failed_from: TaskStatus) -> bool:
        if failed_from != TaskStatus.UPLOADING:
            return True
        if isinstance(error, RetryableUploadError):
            return True
        if isinstance(error, NonRetryableUploadError):
            return False
        return False

    def _remove_retry_schedule(self, task_id: str) -> None:
        with self.lock:
            self.retry_index.pop(task_id, None)

    def _retry_scheduler_loop(self) -> None:
        while not self.stop_event.is_set():
            ready = self._dequeue_ready_retries()
            for task in ready:
                self._enqueue_retry_task(task)
            self.stop_event.wait(self.retry_check_interval_seconds)

    def _dequeue_ready_retries(self) -> List[UnifiedTask]:
        now_ts = time.time()
        ready: List[UnifiedTask] = []
        with self.lock:
            while self.retry_heap:
                due_at, task_id = self.retry_heap[0]
                if due_at > now_ts:
                    break
                heapq.heappop(self.retry_heap)
                indexed = self.retry_index.get(task_id)
                if indexed is None:
                    continue
                idx_due_at, task = indexed
                if idx_due_at != due_at:
                    continue
                self.retry_index.pop(task_id, None)
                ready.append(task)
        return ready

    def _enqueue_retry_task(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        queue_name = self._queue_for_retry_task(task)
        task.metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        task.metadata.pop("retry_due_at", None)
        task.metadata.pop("retry_delay_seconds", None)
        task.metadata.pop("retryable_failure", None)
        task.error_message = None
        task.completed_at = None
        task.started_at = None
        transitioned = self._transition_status(task, TaskStatus.PENDING, strict=False)
        if not transitioned:
            task.status = TaskStatus.PENDING
            self._persist_task(task)
        else:
            self._persist_task(task)
        if queue_name == "upload":
            transitioned_upload = self._transition_status(task, TaskStatus.PROCESSING, strict=False)
            if not transitioned_upload:
                task.status = TaskStatus.PROCESSING
            self._persist_task(task)
        self._enqueue_task(queue_name, task)
        self.logger.info(
            "task retry enqueued: task_id=%s retry_count=%s/%s queue=%s",
            task.task_id,
            task.retry_count,
            task.max_retries,
            queue_name,
        )

    def _queue_for_retry_task(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> str:
        failed_from = str((task.metadata or {}).get("failed_from_status", "")).strip().lower()
        if failed_from == TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value and self._has_uploadable_output(task):
            return "upload"
        if failed_from == TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING.value and self._needs_download(task):
            return "download"
        if failed_from == TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value:
            return "process"
        return self._initial_queue_for_task(task)

    def _restore_retry_schedule(self) -> int:
        if not self.registry.is_persistent():
            return 0
        tasks = self.registry.list_by_status(TaskStatus.FAILED, limit=5000)
        restored = 0
        now_ts = time.time()
        for task in tasks:
            if int(task.retry_count) >= int(task.max_retries):
                continue
            retry_due_at_raw = (task.metadata or {}).get("retry_due_at")
            try:
                retry_due_at = float(retry_due_at_raw)
            except Exception:
                retry_due_at = now_ts
            with self.lock:
                self.retry_index[task.task_id] = (retry_due_at, task)
                heapq.heappush(self.retry_heap, (retry_due_at, task.task_id))
            restored += 1
        return restored

    def _zombie_cleaner_loop(self) -> None:
        while not self.stop_event.is_set():
            reclaimed = self._reclaim_zombies_once()
            if reclaimed > 0:
                with self.lock:
                    self.stats["zombie_reclaimed"] += reclaimed
            self.stop_event.wait(self.zombie_check_interval_seconds)

    def _reclaim_zombies_once(self) -> int:
        running_statuses = [
            TaskStatus.PENDING,
            TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING,
            TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
            TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
        ]
        reclaimed = 0
        for status in running_statuses:
            tasks = self.registry.list_by_status(status, limit=2000)
            for task in tasks:
                if status != TaskStatus.PENDING:
                    with self.lock:
                        if task.task_id in self.active_task_ids:
                            continue
                if not self._is_zombie_task(task, status):
                    continue
                age = int((datetime.now() - (task.started_at or task.created_at)).total_seconds())
                error = RuntimeError(
                    f"zombie task reclaimed after {age}s in status={status.value}"
                )
                self._fail_task(task, error, failed_from=status)
                reclaimed += 1
        return reclaimed

    def _is_zombie_task(self, task: UnifiedTask, status: TaskStatus) -> bool:
        timeout_seconds = float(
            self.zombie_timeout_by_status_seconds.get(status.value, self.zombie_timeout_seconds)
        )
        if timeout_seconds <= 0:
            return False
        if status == TaskStatus.PENDING:
            started_at = task.created_at
        else:
            started_at = task.started_at or task.assigned_at or task.created_at
        if started_at is None:
            return False
        age = (datetime.now() - started_at).total_seconds()
        return age > timeout_seconds

    def _build_zombie_timeout_by_status(self) -> Dict[str, float]:
        mapping_raw = self._get_worker_cfg("zombie_timeout_by_status_seconds", {})
        mapping = mapping_raw if isinstance(mapping_raw, dict) else {}
        defaults = {
            TaskStatus.PENDING.value: float(self.zombie_timeout_seconds),
            TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING.value: float(self.zombie_timeout_seconds),
            TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value: float(self.zombie_timeout_seconds),
            TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value: float(self.zombie_timeout_seconds),
        }
        resolved: Dict[str, float] = {}
        for status_value, default in defaults.items():
            per_status_key = f"zombie_timeout_{status_value}_seconds"
            per_status_value = self._get_worker_cfg(per_status_key, None)
            if per_status_value is not None:
                resolved[status_value] = self._coerce_timeout_seconds(per_status_value, default)
                continue
            map_value = mapping.get(status_value)
            if map_value is not None:
                resolved[status_value] = self._coerce_timeout_seconds(map_value, default)
                continue
            resolved[status_value] = float(default)
        return resolved

    def _coerce_timeout_seconds(self, value: Any, default: float) -> float:
        try:
            return max(5.0, float(value))
        except Exception:
            return max(5.0, float(default))

    def _recover_stuck_tasks(self) -> int:
        if not self.registry.is_persistent():
            return 0

        recoverable = [
            TaskStatus.ASSIGNED,
            TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING,
            TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
            TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
        ]
        recovered = 0
        for status in recoverable:
            tasks = self.registry.list_by_status(status, limit=2000)
            for task in tasks:
                queue_name = self._recovery_queue_for_task(task, status)
                next_status = TaskStatus.PROCESSING if queue_name == "upload" else TaskStatus.PENDING
                task.status = next_status
                if next_status == TaskStatus.PENDING:
                    task.started_at = None
                else:
                    task.started_at = task.started_at or datetime.now()
                task.completed_at = None
                self._persist_task(task)
                self._enqueue_task(queue_name, task)
                recovered += 1
        return recovered

    def _recovery_queue_for_task(self, task: UnifiedTask, old_status: TaskStatus) -> str:
        if old_status == TaskStatus.UPLOADING and self._has_uploadable_output(task):
            return "upload"
        if old_status == TaskStatus.PROCESSING:
            return "process"
        if old_status == TaskStatus.FAILED:
            return self._queue_for_retry_task(task)
        if old_status == TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING and self._needs_download(task):
            return "download"
        return self._initial_queue_for_task(task)

    def _get_queue_cfg(self, key: str, default: Any) -> Any:
        raw_queue = {}
        if isinstance(getattr(self.config, "raw", None), dict):
            raw_queue = self.config.raw.get("queue", {}) or {}
        env_key = f"CLONECUT_QUEUE_{key}".upper()
        env_val = os.getenv(env_key)
        if env_val is not None:
            return self._cast_cfg_value(env_val, default)
        if key in raw_queue:
            return self._cast_cfg_value(raw_queue.get(key), default)
        return default

    def _parse_retry_backoff(self, raw: Any) -> List[int]:
        if isinstance(raw, list):
            values = raw
        elif isinstance(raw, str):
            text = raw.strip()
            values = [item.strip() for item in text.split(",") if item.strip()]
        else:
            values = [5, 10, 20]

        parsed: List[int] = []
        for item in values:
            try:
                parsed.append(max(1, int(item)))
            except Exception:
                continue
        if not parsed:
            parsed = [5, 10, 20]
        return parsed

    def _get_worker_cfg(self, key: str, default: Any) -> Any:
        raw_worker = {}
        if isinstance(getattr(self.config, "raw", None), dict):
            raw_worker = self.config.raw.get("worker", {}) or {}

        env_key = f"CLONECUT_WORKER_{key}".upper()
        env_val = os.getenv(env_key)
        if env_val is not None:
            return self._cast_cfg_value(env_val, default)
        if key in raw_worker:
            return self._cast_cfg_value(raw_worker.get(key), default)
        return default

    def _cast_cfg_value(self, value: Any, default: Any) -> Any:
        if isinstance(default, bool):
            if isinstance(value, bool):
                return value
            return str(value).strip().lower() == "true"
        if isinstance(default, int):
            try:
                return int(value)
            except Exception:
                return default
        if isinstance(default, float):
            try:
                return float(value)
            except Exception:
                return default
        return value

    def _bool_cfg(self, raw: Optional[str], default: bool) -> bool:
        if raw is None:
            return default
        return raw.strip().lower() == "true"

    def _queryable_statuses(self) -> List[TaskStatus]:
        return [
            TaskStatus.PENDING,
            TaskStatus.ASSIGNED,
            TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING,
            TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
            TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
            TaskStatus.COMPLETED,
            TaskStatus.FAILED,
            TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
        ]

    def _resolve_status_filter(self, status: Optional[str]) -> List[TaskStatus]:
        if status is None:
            return self._queryable_statuses()
        raw = str(status).strip().lower()
        if not raw or raw == "all":
            return self._queryable_statuses()
        known = {item.value for item in self._queryable_statuses()}
        if raw not in known:
            raise ValueError(f"invalid status filter: {status}")
        return [parse_task_status(raw)]


__all__ = ["WorkerService"]

def test_internal_pipeline_skeleton_runs(tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")

    cfg = VideoPipelineConfig(output_dir=str(tmp_path / "out"))
    pipeline = VideoPipeline(cfg)
    result = pipeline.run(input_video=str(source), task_id="video-1")

    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file is not None
    assert Path(result.output_file).exists()
    assert "stage0_clean" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage1_transcode" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage2_silence" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage3_repair" in result.executed_stages

    assert "stage7_correct" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage7_subtitle" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage8_cover" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage9_organize" in result.executed_stages
    assert result.current_stage == 11
    assert result.failed_stage is None
    srt = tmp_path / "out" / "video-1" / "_stages" / "video-1_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    manifest = tmp_path / "out" / "video-1" / "_stages" / "video-1_stage8_cover_manifest.json"

def test_pipeline_stage4_manifest_contains_forum_context(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "sidecar")
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    sidecar = tmp_path / "shared.srt"
    sidecar.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:02,000",
                "pipeline context subtitle",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_SIDECAR_PATH", str(sidecar))

    cfg = VideoPipelineConfig(output_dir=str(tmp_path / "out"))
    pipeline = VideoPipeline(cfg)
    result = pipeline.run(
        input_video=str(source),
        task_id="video-ctx",
        forum_post_info={"hotwords": ["topic-a", "topic-b"], "speaker": "spk-1"},
    )

    assert result.success
    manifest = tmp_path / "out" / "video-ctx" / "_stages" / "video-ctx_stage4_asr_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("engine") == "sidecar_srt"
    assert payload.get("hotwords") == ["topic-a", "topic-b"]
    assert payload.get("hotword_count") == 2
    assert payload.get("speaker") == "spk-1"

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass
import os


@dataclass
class VideoPipelineConfig:
    output_dir: str = "output"
    stop_on_error: bool = True
    keep_intermediate_files: bool = False

    @classmethod
    def from_env(cls, output_dir: str) -> "VideoPipelineConfig":
        stop_on_error = os.getenv("CLONECUT_PIPELINE_STOP_ON_ERROR", "true").strip().lower() == "true"
        keep_intermediate = (
            os.getenv("CLONECUT_PIPELINE_KEEP_INTERMEDIATE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
        )
        return cls(
            output_dir=output_dir,
            stop_on_error=stop_on_error,
            keep_intermediate_files=keep_intermediate,
        )

from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import logging
import os
from typing import Any
import uuid
from datetime import datetime

from flask import Flask, jsonify, request
from jinja2 import ChoiceLoader, FileSystemLoader

from apps.web.mock_data import (
    build_worker_resources,
    build_worker_status,
    build_worker_tasks,
)
from apps.web import STATIC_DIR, TEMPLATE_DIR, render_worker_dashboard
from apps.worker.service import WorkerService
from infra.config.loader import load_app_config
from infra.logging.setup import setup_logging


def create_app(service: WorkerService) -> Flask:
    app = Flask(
        __name__,
        template_folder=str(TEMPLATE_DIR),
        static_folder=str(STATIC_DIR),
        static_url_path="/web/static",
    )
    if app.jinja_loader is not None:
        app.jinja_loader = ChoiceLoader([app.jinja_loader, FileSystemLoader(str(TEMPLATE_DIR))])
    _web_mock_mode = os.getenv("CLONECUT_WEB_MOCK_MODE", "").strip().lower() == "true"

    def _mock_mode_from_request() -> bool:
        if _web_mock_mode:
            return True
        raw = request.args.get("mock", "").strip().lower()
        return raw in {"1", "true", "yes"}

    @app.get("/")
    def dashboard() -> Any:
        return render_worker_dashboard(
            {
                "page_title": "CloneCut Worker Dashboard",
                "dashboard_mode": "worker",
                "api_base": "/api/worker",
                "mock_mode": "true" if _mock_mode_from_request() else "false",
            }
        )

    @app.get("/web/worker")
    def worker_dashboard() -> Any:
        return render_worker_dashboard(
            {
                "page_title": "CloneCut Worker Dashboard",
                "dashboard_mode": "worker",
                "api_base": "/api/worker",
                "mock_mode": "true" if _mock_mode_from_request() else "false",
            }
        )

    @app.get("/health")
    def health() -> Any:
        return jsonify({"status": "ok"})

    @app.get("/web/mock/worker/status")
    def mock_worker_status() -> Any:
        return jsonify({"success": True, **build_worker_status()})

    @app.get("/web/mock/worker/resources")
    def mock_worker_resources() -> Any:
        return jsonify({"success": True, "resources": build_worker_resources()})

    @app.get("/web/mock/worker/tasks")
    def mock_worker_tasks() -> Any:
        limit_raw = request.args.get("limit", "10")
        try:
            limit = max(1, min(200, int(limit_raw)))
        except ValueError:
            limit = 10
        tasks = build_worker_tasks(limit=limit)
        return jsonify({"success": True, "tasks": tasks, "total": len(tasks), "limit": limit, "offset": 0})

    @app.post("/web/mock/worker/tasks")
    def mock_worker_submit() -> Any:
        payload = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}
        source_url = str(payload.get("source_url", "")).strip()
        if not source_url:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "missing source_url"}), 400
        task_id = f"mock-submit-{datetime.now().strftime('%H%M%S')}-{uuid.uuid4().hex[:6]}"
        return jsonify({"success": True, "task_id": task_id}), 201

    @app.post("/api/worker/receive-task")
    def receive_task() -> Any:
        data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}
        ok, task_id, error = service.submit(data)
        if not ok:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": error or "invalid task payload"}), 400
        return jsonify({"success": True, "task_id": task_id, "message": "task queued"})

    def _list_tasks_impl() -> Any:
        status = request.args.get("status")
        limit_raw = request.args.get("limit", "20")
        offset_raw = request.args.get("offset", "0")
        try:
            limit = max(1, min(200, int(limit_raw)))
            offset = max(0, int(offset_raw))
        except ValueError:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "invalid pagination params"}), 400

        try:
            payload = service.list_tasks(status=status, limit=limit, offset=offset)
        except ValueError as exc:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": str(exc)}), 400
        return jsonify({"success": True, **payload})

    def _create_task_impl() -> Any:
        data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}
        ok, task_id, error = service.submit(data)
        if not ok:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": error or "invalid task payload"}), 400
        return jsonify({"success": True, "task_id": task_id, "message": "task queued"}), 201

    @app.get("/api/worker/status")
    def worker_status() -> Any:
        return jsonify(service.get_status())

    @app.get("/api/status")
    def status_compat() -> Any:
        return jsonify(service.get_status())

    @app.get("/api/worker/resources")
    def worker_resources() -> Any:
        return jsonify({"success": True, "resources": service.get_resources()})

    @app.get("/api/resources")
    def resources_compat() -> Any:
        return jsonify({"success": True, "resources": service.get_resources()})

    @app.get("/api/worker/tasks")
    def worker_tasks() -> Any:
        return _list_tasks_impl()

    @app.get("/api/tasks")
    def tasks_compat() -> Any:
        return _list_tasks_impl()

    @app.post("/api/worker/tasks")
    def worker_create_task() -> Any:
        return _create_task_impl()

    @app.post("/api/tasks")
    def create_task_compat() -> Any:
        return _create_task_impl()

    @app.get("/api/worker/task/<task_id>")
    def worker_task(task_id: str) -> Any:
        task = service.get_task(task_id)
        if task is None:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "task not found"}), 404
        return jsonify({"success": True, "task": task})

    return app


def _run_http(app: Flask, host: str, port: int, logger: logging.Logger) -> None:
    try:
        from waitress import serve

        logger.info("serving with waitress on %s:%s", host, port)
        serve(app, host=host, port=port)
    except Exception:
        logger.info("waitress unavailable, fallback to flask builtin server on %s:%s", host, port)
        app.run(host=host, port=port, debug=False, use_reloader=False)


def main() -> int:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="CloneCut worker service")
    parser.add_argument("--port", type=int, default=None, help="override service port")
    parser.add_argument("--host", type=str, default=None, help="override service host")
    parser.add_argument("--config", type=str, default="config/settings.yaml", help="config path")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    cfg = load_app_config(args.config)
    cfg.role = "worker"
    if args.port:
        cfg.port = args.port
    if args.host:
        cfg.host = args.host
    if cfg.redis_namespace == "clonecut_monitor:":
        cfg.redis_namespace = "clonecut_worker:"

    setup_logging(cfg.log_dir, cfg.role)
    logger = logging.getLogger("apps.worker")
    logger.info("worker booting")
    logger.info("env=%s role=%s host=%s port=%s", cfg.env, cfg.role, cfg.host, cfg.port)
    logger.info(
        "redis=%s:%s db=%s ns=%s",
        cfg.redis_host,
        cfg.redis_port,
        cfg.redis_db,
        cfg.redis_namespace,
    )

    service = WorkerService(config=cfg, logger=logger)
    service.start()
    app = create_app(service)

    _run_http(app=app, host=cfg.host, port=cfg.port, logger=logger)
    return 0


if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

    def _fail_task(
        self,
        task: UnifiedTask,
        error: Exception,
        failed_from: Optional[TaskStatus] = None,
    ) -> None:
        failed_from_status = failed_from or task.status
        task.metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        task.metadata["failed_from_status"] = failed_from_status.value
        task.metadata["retryable_failure"] = self._is_retryable_failure(
            error=error,
            failed_from=failed_from_status,
        )
        task.error_message = str(error)
        self._persist_task(task)
        transitioned = self._transition_status(task, TaskStatus.FAILED, strict=False)
        if not transitioned:
            self.logger.warning(
                "failed to mark task as failed: task_id=%s current=%s",
                task.task_id,
                task.status.value,
            )
        self._persist_task(task)
        retry_scheduled = self._schedule_retry(task)
        with self.lock:
            self.stats["failed"] += 1
        if retry_scheduled:
            self.logger.warning(
                "task failed and retry scheduled: task_id=%s retry_count=%s/%s error=%s",
                task.task_id,
                task.retry_count,
                task.max_retries,
                error,
            )
            return
        self.logger.warning("task failed: task_id=%s error=%s", task.task_id, error)

    def _initial_queue_for_task(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> str:
        if self._needs_download(task):
            return "download"
        return "process"

    def _target_queue_for_task(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> str:
        if self._needs_download(task):
            return "download"
        if self._has_uploadable_output(task) and task.status in {
            TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
            TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
        }:
            return "upload"
        return "process"

    def _has_uploadable_output(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> bool:
        output_path = str(task.output_path or "").strip()
        if not output_path:
            return False
        return Path(output_path).exists()

    def _needs_download(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> bool:
        if task.task_type != TaskType.VIDEO:
            return False
        source_path = str(task.source_path or "").strip()
        if source_path and Path(source_path).exists():
            return False
        return bool(str(task.source_url or "").strip())

    def _download_source_video(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> str:
        source_url = str(task.source_url or "").strip()
        if not source_url:
            raise ValueError("missing source_url for video download")

        task_input_dir = Path(self.config.input_dir) / task.task_id
        task_input_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        filename = self._resolve_download_filename(task, source_url)
        target = task_input_dir / filename
        temp_path = task_input_dir / f"{filename}.part"

        parsed = urlparse(source_url)
        if parsed.scheme == "file":
            local_source = self._parse_file_uri(source_url)
            if not local_source.exists():
                raise FileNotFoundError(f"source file not found: {local_source}")
            shutil.copy2(local_source, temp_path)
            temp_path.replace(target)
            return str(target)

        if parsed.scheme == "" and Path(source_url).exists():
            shutil.copy2(Path(source_url), temp_path)
            temp_path.replace(target)
            return str(target)

        if self._looks_like_windows_path(source_url) and Path(source_url).exists():
            shutil.copy2(Path(source_url), temp_path)
            temp_path.replace(target)
            return str(target)

        if parsed.scheme not in {"http", "https"}:
            raise ValueError(f"unsupported source_url scheme: {parsed.scheme}")

        try:
            with requests.get(
                source_url,
                stream=True,
                timeout=(10, self.download_timeout_seconds),
            ) as response:
                response.raise_for_status()
                with temp_path.open("wb") as f:
                    for chunk in response.iter_content(chunk_size=self.download_chunk_size):
                        if not chunk:
                            continue
                        if self.stop_event.is_set():
                            raise RuntimeError("download interrupted: worker stopping")
                        f.write(chunk)
            temp_path.replace(target)
            return str(target)
        except Exception:
            try:
                temp_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)
            except Exception:
                pass
            raise

    def _prepare_video_download_context(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        if task.task_type != TaskType.VIDEO:
            return
        metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        payload = dict(task.payload or {})
        forum_info: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        if isinstance(metadata.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            forum_info.update(metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})
        if isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            forum_info.update(payload.get("forum_post_info") or {})

        post_url = self._pick_first_text(
            forum_info.get("post_url"),
            payload.get("post_url"),
            metadata.get("post_url"),
        )
        source_url = str(task.source_url or "").strip()
        if not post_url and self._looks_like_forum_post_url(source_url):
            post_url = source_url
        if post_url:
            forum_info["post_url"] = post_url

        should_parse_post = bool(post_url) and (
            not source_url or self._looks_like_forum_post_url(source_url)
        )
        if should_parse_post:
            parsed_info = self._resolve_forum_post_download_info(post_url)
            forum_info.update(parsed_info)
            parsed_video_url = str(parsed_info.get("video_url") or "").strip()
            if parsed_video_url:
                task.source_url = parsed_video_url

        if forum_info:
            metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
            payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_info

        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
            forum_post_info=forum_info,
            payload=payload,
            metadata=metadata,
            source_url=str(task.source_url or ""),
        )
        if original_filename:
            metadata["original_filename"] = original_filename
            payload["original_filename"] = original_filename
            if forum_info:
                forum_info["original_filename"] = original_filename
                metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
                payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_info

        task.metadata = metadata
        task.payload = payload

    def _resolve_forum_post_download_info(self, post_url: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        normalized_post_url = str(post_url or "").strip()

        if detail is None:
            raise RuntimeError(f"failed to parse forum post detail: {normalized_post_url}")

            if text:
                video_urls.append(text)
        dedup_video_urls: List[str] = []
        seen_urls: set[str] = set()

            if item in seen_urls:
                continue
            seen_urls.add(item)
            dedup_video_urls.append(item)

            raise RuntimeError(f"no downloadable video url found in post: {normalized_post_url}")
        video_url = dedup_video_urls[0]

            parsed_info.get("thread_id"),
            detail.thread_id,
            self._parse_thread_id_from_post_url(normalized_post_url),

# Janus 执行入口（CloneCut 严格等价改造）

> 版本：v1.0  
> 日期：2026-02-28  
> 适用：`D:\clonecut`

## 1. 目的

- 作为本仓库“严格等价改造”统一入口，冻结范围、节奏、验收口径。
- 约束执行顺序：先文档契约，再代码实现，再回归验收。

## 2. 必读文档

- `docs/旧版流程严格等价改造方案.md`
- `docs/equivalence_contract.md`
- `tests/regression/README.md`
- `tests/regression/manifest_equivalence_samples.template.json`
- `janus/TECH.md`

## 3. 红线（必须遵守）

- 只做“旧版流程严格等价”，不做业务增强。
- 不允许以离线脚本补回帖替代在线闭环成功。
- 不允许在新链路中 `import` 或路径依赖 `D:\funclip-xiaocut-cut6.0`。
- 默认目标为严格等价模式：`CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE=true`。
- 验收门槛固定为：
  - `pass_rate=100%`
  - `fallback_used_ratio=0%`
  - 在线闭环（回帖+附件）通过

## 4. 执行顺序

1. 阶段A：冻结契约与样本基线（先验收标准）。
2. 阶段B：恢复 upload 在线闭环。
3. 阶段C：下载与 `forum_post_info` 口径对齐。
4. 阶段D：stage0~9（含6.5）逐步等价。
5. 阶段E：monitor->worker 载荷与状态口径对齐。
6. 阶段F：灰度、回滚、切换收口。

## 5. 交付要求

- 每阶段必须有“可审查产物”：文档差异、回归报告、风险与回滚记录。
- 阶段未达 DoD，不得进入下一阶段。
- 阻塞项必须记录 owner、截止时间、解除标准。

## 6. 分支与提交流程

- 建议分支：`feature/equivalence-phase-{A..F}`。
- 提交信息使用中文（UTF-8），禁止乱码提交。
- 通过 PR（Squash）合并，默认目标分支 `dev`。

# Janus 技术基线（CloneCut 严格等价改造）

> 版本：v1.0  
> 日期：2026-02-28

## 1. 运行时与版本锁定

- Python：`3.10.x`
- 包管理：`uv`
- 依赖安装：
  - `uv venv --python 3.10 .venv`
  - `uv pip install -e ".[asr,llm,forum,test]"`
- 约束：依赖版本必须锁定；升级先评审影响和回归计划。

## 2. 核心配置口径

- 严格等价：`CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE=true`
- 内置流水线：`worker.use_internal_pipeline=true`
- 论坛凭据优先环境变量：
  - `FORUM_BASE_URL`
  - `FORUM_USERNAME`
  - `FORUM_PASSWORD`

## 3. 架构边界

- 主链路：`monitor -> worker(download/process/upload) -> completed`
- `upload` 成功定义：本地上传成功 + 论坛回帖成功 + 附件上传成功。
- 旧版工程仅作对比基线，不参与新链路运行时依赖。

## 4. 目录与产物规范

- 最终归档目录：`output/{original_filename}/`
- 关键产物：
  - `{original_filename}_final.mp4`
  - `{original_filename}_cover.jpg`
  - `{original_filename}_subtitle.srt`
  - `forum_post_info.json`

## 5. 测试与验收命令（基线）

- 单元/集成：
  - `uv run python -m pytest -q`
- 回归对比：
  - `uv run python scripts/regression_compare.py ...`
  - `uv run python scripts/regression_gate.py ...`
- 最终闭环：
  - `uv run python scripts/forum_e2e_regression.py ...`

## 6. 发布与回滚

- 每阶段完成后打 tag（phase-A ~ phase-F）。
- 紧急降级优先环境变量/配置，不先做代码回退。
- 回滚后必须补做“回滚验证记录”。

    def _select_tts_adapters(self) -> List[Tuple[str, Any]]:
        if self.tts_engine_mode == "http":
            return [("http", self.tts_http_adapter)]
        if self.tts_engine_mode == "auto":
            return [
                ("local", self.tts_local_adapter),
                ("http", self.tts_http_adapter),
            ]
        return [("local", self.tts_local_adapter)]

    def _process_video_like(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        source_path = str(task.source_path or "").strip()
        use_internal = self.internal_pipeline_enabled or not self.video_adapter.is_enabled()
        if use_internal:
            if not source_path or not Path(source_path).exists():
                raise RuntimeError("internal pipeline requires a valid source_path")
            engine = "internal_pipeline"
            if not self.internal_pipeline_enabled:
                engine = "internal_pipeline_auto"
            result = self._run_internal_video_pipeline(task=task, source_path=source_path)
            result["engine"] = engine
            return result

        if self.video_adapter.is_enabled():
            result = self.video_adapter.process(task)
            task.current_stage = 9
            task.stage_checkpoint = "video_command"
            return result

        raise RuntimeError("no video engine configured")

    def _run_internal_video_pipeline(self, task: UnifiedTask, source_path: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        stage_names = [
            "stage0_clean",
            "stage1_transcode",
            "stage2_silence",
            "stage3_repair",
            "stage4_asr",
            "stage5_ai_text",
            "stage6_clip",
            "stage6_5_resub",
            "stage7_correct",
            "stage7_subtitle",
            "stage8_cover",
            "stage9_organize",
        ]
        # Internal pipeline is currently executed as a full run for determinism.
        start_from_stage = 0

        task_dir = Path(self.config.output_dir) / task.task_id
        task_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

        source = Path(source_path)
        if not source.exists():
            task.stage_checkpoint = stage_names[start_from_stage]
            task.current_stage = start_from_stage
            raise RuntimeError(f"source file not found: {source}")

        repo_root = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]
        pipeline_script = repo_root / "domain" / "video" / "pre" / "main" / "pipeline.py"
        if not pipeline_script.exists():
            raise RuntimeError(f"internal pipeline script missing: {pipeline_script}")

        timeout_raw = self._get_worker_cfg("internal_pipeline_timeout_seconds", 7200)
        try:
            timeout_seconds = max(60, int(timeout_raw))
        except Exception:
            timeout_seconds = 7200

        cmd = [
            sys.executable,
            str(pipeline_script),
            "--input",
            str(source),
            "--output",
            str(task_dir),
        ]
        if importlib.util.find_spec("funasr") is None:
            return self._run_internal_video_pipeline_fallback_copy(
                task=task,
                source=source,
                task_dir=task_dir,
                stage_names=stage_names,
                start_from_stage=start_from_stage,
                reason="missing dependency: funasr",
            )
        try:
            started = time.perf_counter()
            proc = subprocess.run(
                cmd,
                cwd=str(repo_root),
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                encoding="utf-8",
                errors="replace",
                timeout=timeout_seconds,
            )
            elapsed_ms = int(max(0.0, (time.perf_counter() - started) * 1000))

            if proc.returncode != 0:
                combined = "\n".join(
                    [str(proc.stdout or "").strip(), str(proc.stderr or "").strip()]
                ).strip()
                tail_lines = [line for line in combined.splitlines() if line.strip()][-20:]
                tail_text = "\n".join(tail_lines)
                raise RuntimeError(
                    f"internal pipeline failed: exit={proc.returncode} "
                    f"timeout={timeout_seconds}s tail=\n{tail_text}"
                )

            output_path = self._resolve_internal_pipeline_output_path(task_dir=task_dir, source_path=source)
            executed = stage_names[start_from_stage:]
            task.current_stage = len(stage_names) - 1
            task.stage_checkpoint = stage_names[-1]
            return {
                "success": True,
                "request_type": task.task_type.value,
                "output_path": str(output_path),
                "executed_stages": executed,
                "executed_mode": "real_pipeline",
                "performance_summary": (
                    f"internal pipeline executed stages={len(executed)} "
                    f"duration_ms={elapsed_ms} command={' '.join(cmd)}"
                ),
            }
        except Exception as exc:
            self.logger.warning(
                "internal pipeline unavailable, fallback to copy mode: task_id=%s err=%s",
                task.task_id,
                exc,
            )
            return self._run_internal_video_pipeline_fallback_copy(
                task=task,
                source=source,
                task_dir=task_dir,
                stage_names=stage_names,
                start_from_stage=start_from_stage,
                reason=str(exc),
            )

    def _resolve_internal_pipeline_output_path(self, task_dir: Path, source_path: Path) -> Path:
        state_file = task_dir / "state.json"
        if not state_file.exists():
            raise RuntimeError(f"internal pipeline state missing: {state_file}")
        try:
            payload = json.loads(state_file.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
        except Exception as exc:
            raise RuntimeError(f"parse internal pipeline state failed: {state_file}: {exc}") from exc

        last_completed_step = int(payload.get("last_completed_step", -1))
        if last_completed_step < 9:
            raise RuntimeError(
                f"internal pipeline incomplete: last_completed_step={last_completed_step} state_file={state_file}"
            )
        output_file = str(payload.get("output_file") or "").strip()
        if output_file:
            candidate = Path(output_file)
            if candidate.exists():
                return candidate

        patterns = [
            f"{source_path.stem}*_智能剪辑带字幕版*.mp4",
            "*_智能剪辑带字幕版*.mp4",
            "*.mp4",
        ]
        for pattern in patterns:
            candidates = [
                p for p in task_dir.rglob(pattern)
                if p.is_file() and "_stages" not in p.parts and "debug" not in p.parts
            ]
            if candidates:
                candidates.sort(key=lambda p: p.stat().st_mtime, reverse=True)
                return candidates[0]

        raise RuntimeError(f"internal pipeline produced no video output under: {task_dir}")

    def _run_internal_video_pipeline_fallback_copy(
        self,
        task: UnifiedTask,
        source: Path,
        task_dir: Path,
        stage_names: List[str],
        start_from_stage: int,
        reason: str,
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        stage_dir = task_dir / "_stages"
        stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        output_path = task_dir / f"{task.task_id}{source.suffix or '.mp4'}"
        shutil.copy2(source, output_path)

        asr_srt = stage_dir / f"{task.task_id}_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
        asr_srt.write_text(
            "\n".join(
                [
                    "1",
                    "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000",
                    "internal pipeline fallback subtitle",
                    "",
                ]
            ),
            encoding="utf-8",
        )
        cover_manifest = stage_dir / f"{task.task_id}_stage8_cover_manifest.json"
        cover_manifest.write_text(
            json.dumps(
                {
                    "task_id": task.task_id,
                    "engine": "internal_pipeline_fallback",
                    "cover_titles": [],
                    "fallback_reason": reason,
                },
                ensure_ascii=False,
                indent=2,
            ),
            encoding="utf-8",
        )

        executed = stage_names[start_from_stage:]
        task.current_stage = len(stage_names) - 1
        task.stage_checkpoint = stage_names[-1]
        return {
            "success": True,
            "request_type": task.task_type.value,
            "output_path": str(output_path),
            "executed_stages": executed,
            "executed_mode": "fallback_copy",
            "performance_summary": (
                f"internal pipeline fallback executed stages={len(executed)} reason={reason}"
            ),
        }

        metadata = dict(data.get("metadata") or {})
        source_path = str(
            data.get("source_path")
            or payload.get("source_path")
            or metadata.get("source_path")
            or ""
        ).strip()
        source_url = (

from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Dict
import os

from shared.errors.base import ConfigError


try:
    import yaml
except Exception:  # pragma: no cover
    yaml = None


@dataclass
class AppConfig:
    name: str = "clonecut"
    env: str = "production"
    role: str = "worker"
    host: str = "0.0.0.0"
    port: int = 8205

    redis_host: str = "127.0.0.1"
    redis_port: int = 6379
    redis_db: int = 0
    redis_password: str = ""
    redis_namespace: str = "clonecut_worker:"

    input_dir: str = "D:/clonecut/input"
    output_dir: str = "D:/clonecut/output"
    log_dir: str = "D:/clonecut/logs"

    raw: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)


def _read_yaml(path: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    if not path.exists():
        return {}
    if yaml is None:
        raise ConfigError("pyyaml is required to read yaml config files")
    with path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        return yaml.safe_load(f) or {}


def _env(name: str, default: str = "") -> str:
    value = os.getenv(name)
    return default if value is None else value


def load_app_config(path: str | Path = "config/settings.yaml") -> AppConfig:
    cfg_path = Path(path)
    raw = _read_yaml(cfg_path)

    app = raw.get("app", {})
    redis = raw.get("redis", {})
    paths = raw.get("paths", {})

    role = _env("CLONECUT_ROLE", str(app.get("role", "worker")))
    port = int(_env("CLONECUT_PORT", str(app.get("port", 8205))))

    config = AppConfig(
        name=str(app.get("name", "clonecut")),
        env=_env("CLONECUT_ENV", str(app.get("env", "production"))),
        role=role,
        host=str(app.get("host", "0.0.0.0")),
        port=port,
        redis_host=_env("REDIS_HOST", str(redis.get("host", "127.0.0.1"))),
        redis_port=int(_env("REDIS_PORT", str(redis.get("port", 6379)))),
        redis_db=int(_env("REDIS_DB", str(redis.get("db", 0)))),
        redis_password=_env("REDIS_PASSWORD", str(redis.get("password", ""))),
        redis_namespace=_env("REDIS_NAMESPACE", str(redis.get("namespace", "clonecut_worker:"))),
        input_dir=_env("INPUT_DIR", str(paths.get("input_dir", "D:/clonecut/input"))),
        output_dir=_env("OUTPUT_DIR", str(paths.get("output_dir", "D:/clonecut/output"))),
        log_dir=_env("LOG_DIR", str(paths.get("log_dir", "D:/clonecut/logs"))),
        raw=raw,
    )

    if config.role not in {"monitor", "worker", "api"}:
        raise ConfigError(f"invalid role: {config.role}")

    if config.port <= 0:
        raise ConfigError(f"invalid port: {config.port}")

    return config

sys.path.append(os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))))

# --- Add imports for model pre-loading ---
try:

    MODELS_AVAILABLE = True
except ImportError:
    MODELS_AVAILABLE = False

from pre.stage.stage6 import step6_clip

from pre.stage.stage8 import step8_add_title

# 导入内部模块
from pre.main.logging_manager import setup_logger, log_step_start, log_step_end

    show_banner, show_menu, get_user_choice,

# 导入Rich美化工具（无rich依赖时自动降级）
try:
    from pre.main.rich_utils import (
        console, print_step_header, print_file_info,
        print_step_result, create_progress_bar, print_statistics, print_resource_usage, monitor
    )
except Exception:
    class _ConsoleFallback:
        def print(self, *args, **kwargs):
            print(*args)

        def rule(self, *args, **kwargs):
            if args:
                print(args[0])

    class _MonitorFallback:
        def record_step_resource(self, *_args, **_kwargs):
            return ""

    console = _ConsoleFallback()
    monitor = _MonitorFallback()

    def print_step_header(*_args, **_kwargs):
        return None

        return None
