        return None

    def print_resource_usage(*_args, **_kwargs):
        return None


def _build_funasr_model(config):
    """Create FunASR model without depending on removed lightweight modules."""
    if not MODELS_AVAILABLE:
        return None
    try:
        model_name = config.get(
            "funasr_model_asr",
            "iic/speech_seaco_paraformer_large_asr_nat-zh-cn-16k-common-vocab8404-pytorch",
        )
        vad_model = config.get("funasr_model_vad", "damo/speech_fsmn_vad_zh-cn-16k-common-pytorch")
        punc_model = config.get(
            "funasr_model_punc",
            "damo/punc_ct-transformer_zh-cn-common-vocab272727-pytorch",
        )
        spk_model = config.get("funasr_model_spk", "damo/speech_campplus_sv_zh-cn_16k-common")
        kwargs = {
            "model": model_name,
            "vad_model": vad_model,
            "punc_model": punc_model,
        }
        if spk_model:
            kwargs["spk_model"] = spk_model
        return AutoModel(**kwargs)
    except Exception:
        return None


def init_pipeline():
    """
    初始化流水线环境
    
    Returns:
        tuple: (config, logger, timer, audio_clipper) 配置、日志记录器、计时器和模型处理器
    """
    # 加载环境变量
    load_env()
    
    # 获取配置参数
    config = get_config()
    
    # 检测GPU并更新配置
    has_gpu = check_gpu_available()
    if has_gpu:
        logging.info("检测到NVIDIA GPU，已启用GPU加速")
        config["use_gpu"] = True
    else:
        logging.info("未检测到NVIDIA GPU，使用CPU模式")
        config["use_gpu"] = False
        # 如果没有GPU，将编码器改回CPU版本
        if config["silence_codec_v"] == "h264_nvenc":
            config["silence_codec_v"] = "h264"
    
    # 确保输出目录存在
    ensure_output_dir(config["output_dir"])
    
    # 设置日志记录器
    logger = setup_logger(config["output_dir"])
    logger.info("开始视频处理流水线")
    
    # 初始化计时器
    timer = StepTimer()
    
    # Pre-load FunASR model using global model manager
    audio_clipper = None
    if MODELS_AVAILABLE:
        console.print("\n[info]正在初始化语音识别模型...[/info]")
        try:
            funasr_model = _build_funasr_model(config)

            if funasr_model is not None:
                audio_clipper = VideoClipper(funasr_model)
                audio_clipper.lang = 'zh' # default to Chinese
                console.print("[green]✅ 语音识别模型加载成功[/green]")
            else:
                console.print("[red]❌ 语音识别模型加载失败[/red]")
                audio_clipper = None
        except Exception as e:
            console.print(f"[red]❌ 语音识别模型加载失败: {e}[/red]")
            audio_clipper = None
    else:
        console.print("[warning]无法导入FunASR或FunClip模块，语音识别和剪辑功能将不可用。[/warning]")

    # 确保所有步骤的enable配置都存在，默认都为True
    if "enable_step1" not in config:
        config["enable_step1"] = True
    if "enable_step8" not in config:
        config["enable_step8"] = True
    if "enable_step9" not in config:
        config["enable_step9"] = True
    
    return config, logger, timer, audio_clipper


def run_step(step_number, step_name, step_func, current_video, config, timer, audio_clipper, enabled=True):
    """
    运行单个流水线步骤
    
    Args:
        step_number: 步骤编号
        step_name: 步骤名称
        step_func: 步骤函数
        current_video: 当前处理的视频路径
        config: 配置字典
        timer: 计时器
        audio_clipper: 预加载的模型处理器
        enabled: 步骤是否启用
        
    Returns:
        tuple: (success, output_file, duration_str) 是否成功、输出文件路径、用时
    """
    if not enabled:
        console.print(f"[warning]跳过步骤{step_number}: {step_name} (已禁用)[/warning]")
        logging.getLogger("FunClip").info(f"跳过步骤{step_number}: {step_name} (已禁用)")
        return True, current_video, None
    
    # 显示步骤标题
    print_step_header(step_number, step_name)
    
    # 如果当前视频不为空，显示输入文件信息
    if current_video:
        print_file_info("输入文件", current_video)
    
    # 开始计时并记录日志
    timer.start_step()
    log_step_start(step_number, step_name, current_video)
    
    # 运行步骤
    success = False
    output_file = current_video
    try:
        # Special handling for steps that need the clipper
        if step_number in [4, 6, 6.5]:
            if audio_clipper is None:
                console.print(f"\n[error]步骤{step_number} ({step_name}) 需要的模型未成功加载，已跳过。[/error]")
                success = False
                output_file = current_video
            else:
                if step_number == 4 or step_number == 6.5: # 语音识别
                    success, _ = step_func(current_video, config, audio_clipper)
                    output_file = current_video
                elif step_number == 6: # 视频剪辑
                    success, output_file = step_func(current_video, config, audio_clipper)
        # 第5步不改变视频文件，但返回的是文本文件路径
        elif step_number == 5:
            success, output_file = step_func(current_video, config)
        # 其他步骤
        else:
            success, output_file = step_func(current_video, config)
    except Exception as e:
        logger = logging.getLogger("FunClip")
        logger.error(f"步骤{step_number}异常: {str(e)}")
        console.print(f"\n[error]步骤{step_number}异常: {str(e)}[/error]")
        success = False
    
    # 结束计时
    duration_str = timer.end_step(step_number, step_name)
    
    # 记录日志
    log_step_end(step_number, step_name, success, duration_str, output_file)
    
    # 打印结果
    print_step_result(step_number, success, duration_str, 
                     output_file if step_number not in [4, 5] else None)
    
    if success:
        # 增加健壮性检查：确保输出是文件而不是目录
        if output_file and os.path.isdir(output_file):
            logger.error(f"步骤{step_number} ({step_name}) 返回了一个目录路径 '{output_file}' 而不是文件路径。")
            console.print(f"[error]错误：步骤{step_number} ({step_name}) 处理失败，返回了无效的输出路径。[/error]")
            return False, current_video, duration_str # 返回失败

        # 保存状态
        if step_number == 4:
            # 语音识别不生成新视频，使用相同输入输出
            save_state(step_number, current_video, current_video, config["output_dir"], step_name)
        else:
            save_state(step_number, current_video, output_file, config["output_dir"], step_name)
        
        # 主动调用垃圾收集器释放内存
        gc.collect()
        logger = logging.getLogger("FunClip")
        logger.info(f"步骤{step_number}内存已释放")
        
        # 显示系统资源使用情况
        # 记录当前步骤的资源使用情况
        usage_str = monitor.record_step_resource(step_number, f"步骤{step_number}: {step_name}")
        print_resource_usage()
        
    return success, output_file, duration_str


def should_run_step(step_number, choice, is_pipeline=False):
    """
    判断是否应该运行指定步骤
    
    Args:
        step_number: 步骤编号
        choice: 用户选择
        is_pipeline: 是否是流水线模式
        
    Returns:
        bool: 是否应该运行该步骤
    """
    return str(step_number) == choice or (choice == "10" and is_pipeline)


def run_pipeline():
    """
    运行完整流水线

    Returns:
        bool: 流水线是否成功完成
    """
    # 解析命令行参数
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='视频处理流水线')
    parser.add_argument('--input', help='输入视频文件路径')
    parser.add_argument('--output', help='输出目录路径')
    args = parser.parse_args()

    # 如果有命令行参数，则使用非交互模式
    non_interactive_mode = args.input is not None

    show_banner()

    try:
        # 初始化
        config, logger, timer, audio_clipper = init_pipeline()

        # 如果指定了输出目录，更新配置
        if args.output:
            config["output_dir"] = args.output
            ensure_output_dir(config["output_dir"])
        
        # 非交互模式：直接运行完整流水线
        if non_interactive_mode:
            choice = "10"  # 完整流水线
            is_pipeline = True
        else:
            # 显示菜单并获取用户选择
            show_menu()
            choice = get_user_choice()

            # 判断是否为完整流水线模式
            is_pipeline = (choice == "10")

        # 如果是执行全部步骤(10)，先执行清理JSON文件
        if is_pipeline and config["enable_step0"]:
            success, _, _ = run_step(
                0, "清理输出目录JSON文件", step0_clean_json, None, config, timer, audio_clipper,
                enabled=True
            )
            if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
                console.print("[error]清理JSON文件失败，根据配置终止流水线[/error]")
                logger.error("清理JSON文件失败，根据配置终止流水线")
                return False
                
            # 清理完成后输出提示
            console.print("\n[info]JSON文件清理完成，请输入需要处理的视频文件路径[/info]")
        
        # 如果单独执行清理JSON操作
        elif choice == "0":
            success, _, _ = run_step(
                0, "清理输出目录JSON文件", step0_clean_json, None, config, timer, audio_clipper,
                enabled=True
            )
            if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
                console.print("[error]清理JSON文件失败，根据配置终止流水线[/error]")
                logger.error("清理JSON文件失败，根据配置终止流水线")
                return False
                
            console.print("\n[success]清理JSON文件完成，流水线结束[/success]")
            return True
        
        # 获取上次状态
        last_state = None
        if choice != "10":  # 执行全部步骤时不使用上次状态
            last_state = load_state(config["output_dir"])
        
        # 根据用户选择获取输入视频
        if non_interactive_mode:
            # 非交互模式：使用命令行参数中的输入文件
            input_video = args.input
            if not input_video:
                console.print("[error]非交互模式下必须指定 --input 参数[/error]")
                return False
            if not os.path.exists(input_video):
                console.print(f"[error]错误: 找不到视频文件 {input_video}[/error]")
                return False
        elif choice == "10":
            # 全部步骤：强制要求用户输入新视频路径，不使用历史记录
            console.print("\n[info]请输入要处理的视频文件路径:[/info]")
            input_video = input("> ").strip()
            if not input_video:
                console.print("[error]未输入视频路径，程序退出[/error]")
                return False
            if not os.path.exists(input_video):
                console.print(f"[error]错误: 找不到视频文件 {input_video}[/error]")
                return False
        elif choice != "0":  # 不是清理JSON的单独操作
            input_video = get_input_video(config["output_dir"], int(choice) if choice.isdigit() else None, last_state)
            if not input_video:
                logger.error("未能获取有效的输入视频，流水线终止")
                return False
        else:
            # 清理JSON操作不需要输入视频
            input_video = None
        
        # 保存原始输入视频路径（用于后续文件整理）
        original_input_video = input_video if input_video else ""
        
        # 当前处理的视频路径
        current_video = input_video if input_video else ""
        
        # 步骤0: 清理JSON文件 - 如果不是执行全部步骤也不是单独执行步骤0，单独选择了其他步骤时才执行
        if not is_pipeline and choice != "0" and should_run_step(0, choice, is_pipeline=False):
            success, _, _ = run_step(
                0, "清理输出目录JSON文件", step0_clean_json, None, config, timer, audio_clipper,
                enabled=True
            )
            if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
                console.print("[error]清理JSON文件失败，根据配置终止流水线[/error]")
                logger.error("清理JSON文件失败，根据配置终止流水线")
                return False
        
        # 流水线处理
        # 步骤1: 视频转码
        success, current_video, _ = run_step(
            1, "视频转码", step1_transcode, current_video, config, timer, audio_clipper,
            enabled=should_run_step(1, choice, is_pipeline) and config["enable_step1"]
        )
        if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
            if not is_pipeline: return False # 单步执行失败则退出
            console.print("[error]视频转码失败，根据配置终止流水线[/error]")
            logger.error("视频转码失败，根据配置终止流水线")
            return False
        if not is_pipeline and choice == "1": return True # 单步执行成功则退出
            
        # 步骤2: 剪辑气口
        success, current_video, _ = run_step(
            2, "剪辑气口", step2_remove_silence, current_video, config, timer, audio_clipper,
            enabled=should_run_step(2, choice, is_pipeline) and config["enable_step2"]
        )
        if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
            if not is_pipeline: return False
            console.print("[error]剪辑气口失败，根据配置终止流水线[/error]")
            logger.error("剪辑气口失败，根据配置终止流水线")
            return False
        if not is_pipeline and choice == "2": return True
            
        # 步骤3: 视频修复
        success, current_video, _ = run_step(
            3, "视频修复", step3_fix_video, current_video, config, timer, audio_clipper,
            enabled=should_run_step(3, choice, is_pipeline) and config["enable_step3"]
        )
        if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
            if not is_pipeline: return False
            console.print("[error]视频修复失败，根据配置终止流水线[/error]")
            logger.error("视频修复失败，根据配置终止流水线")
            return False
        if not is_pipeline and choice == "3": return True
            
        # 步骤4: 生成未修改字幕
        success, current_video, _ = run_step(
            4, "生成未修改字幕", step4_recognize, current_video, config, timer, audio_clipper,
            enabled=should_run_step(4, choice, is_pipeline) and config["enable_step4"]
        )
        if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
            if not is_pipeline: return False
            console.print("[error]生成未修改字幕失败，根据配置终止流水线[/error]")
            logger.error("生成未修改字幕失败，根据配置终止流水线")
            return False
        if not is_pipeline and choice == "4": return True
            
        # 步骤5: 剪辑文本中的停顿词重复内容
        success, current_video, _ = run_step(
            5, "剪辑文本中的停顿词重复内容", step5_ai_processing, current_video, config, timer, audio_clipper,
            enabled=should_run_step(5, choice, is_pipeline) and config["enable_step5"]
        )
        if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
            if not is_pipeline: return False
            console.print("[error]剪辑文本中的停顿词重复内容失败，根据配置终止流水线[/error]")
            logger.error("剪辑文本中的停顿词重复内容失败，根据配置终止流水线")
            return False
        if not is_pipeline and choice == "5": return True
            
        # 步骤6: 大模型剪辑成片
        success, current_video, _ = run_step(
            6, "大模型剪辑成片", step6_clip, current_video, config, timer, audio_clipper,
            enabled=should_run_step(6, choice, is_pipeline) and config["enable_step6"]
        )
        if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
            if not is_pipeline: return False
            console.print("[error]大模型剪辑成片失败，根据配置终止流水线[/error]")
            logger.error("大模型剪辑成片失败，根据配置终止流水线")
            return False
        if not is_pipeline and choice == "6": return True

        # 新增步骤：在第6步剪辑成功后，为剪辑后的视频重新生成字幕，以确保时间轴同步
        # This step runs only if step 6 was successful and was intended to run.
        if success and (should_run_step(6, choice, is_pipeline) or should_run_step(7, choice, is_pipeline)):
            # 标记为6.5，以便在日志中区分
            # 添加更详细的日志记录
            logger.info("步骤6.5开始：为剪辑后视频重新生成字幕，将记录详细日志")
            success, _, _ = run_step(
                6.5, "重新生成剪辑后字幕", step4_recognize, current_video, config, timer, audio_clipper,
                enabled=True  # 此处直接启用，因为外部if已判断
            )
            if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
                if not is_pipeline: return False
                console.print("[error]重新生成剪辑后字幕失败，根据配置终止流水线[/error]")
                logger.error("重新生成剪辑后字幕失败，根据配置终止流水线")
                return False
            
        # 步骤7: 添加修正后的字幕
        success, current_video, _ = run_step(
            7, "添加修正后的字幕", step7_add_subtitle, current_video, config, timer, audio_clipper,
            enabled=should_run_step(7, choice, is_pipeline) and config["enable_step7"]
        )
        if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
            if not is_pipeline: return False
            console.print("[error]添加修正后的字幕失败，根据配置终止流水线[/error]")
            logger.error("添加修正后的字幕失败，根据配置终止流水线")
            return False
        if not is_pipeline and choice == "7": return True
            
        # 步骤8: 添加封面标题
        success, current_video, _ = run_step(
            8, "添加封面标题", step8_add_title, current_video, config, timer, audio_clipper,
            enabled=should_run_step(8, choice, is_pipeline) and config["enable_step8"]
        )
        if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
            if not is_pipeline: return False
            console.print("[error]添加封面标题失败，根据配置终止流水线[/error]")
            logger.error("添加封面标题失败，根据配置终止流水线")
            return False
        if not is_pipeline and choice == "8": return True
            
        # 步骤9: 文件整理
        success, final_video, _ = run_step(
            9, "文件整理", step9_organize_files, current_video, config, timer, audio_clipper,
            enabled=should_run_step(9, choice, is_pipeline) and config["enable_step9"]
        )
        if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
            if not is_pipeline: return False
            console.print("[error]文件整理失败，根据配置终止流水线[/error]")
            logger.error("文件整理失败，根据配置终止流水线")
            return False
        if not is_pipeline and choice == "9": return True
            
        # 最终结果
        timer.end_timer()
        total_time = timer.get_total_time()
        console.print("\n[success]✨ 流水线处理完成! ✨[/success]")
        console.print(f"总耗时: {format_time(total_time)}")
        console.print(f"最终输出文件: {final_video}")
        logger.info(f"流水线处理完成，总耗时: {format_time(total_time)}，最终输出: {final_video}")
        
        # 打印时间统计
        timer.print_statistics()
        
        # 使用Rich美化的方式打印统计信息
        print_statistics(timer.step_times, timer.get_total_time())
        
        return True

    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        console.print("\n[warning]用户中断，流水线已停止[/warning]")
        logger = logging.getLogger("FunClip")
        logger.warning("用户中断，流水线已停止")
        return False
    except Exception as e:
        console.print(f"[error]流水线执行异常: {str(e)}[/error]")
        logger = logging.getLogger("FunClip")
        logger.error(f"流水线执行异常: {str(e)}", exc_info=True)
        return False


if __name__ == "__main__":
    # 当直接运行此文件时，执行流水线
    run_pipeline()

from __future__ import annotations

import json
from pathlib import Path

from domain.video.stages import stage4_asr, stage5_ai_text


def test_stage4_prefers_sidecar_subtitle(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "sidecar")
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    sidecar = tmp_path / "input.srt"
    sidecar.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,500",
                "hello world",
                "",
                "2",
                "00:00:01,500 --> 00:00:03,000",
                "second line",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    result = stage4_asr.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v1")
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file
    assert Path(str(result.output_file)).exists()

    srt = out_dir / "v1" / "_stages" / "v1_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    transcript = out_dir / "v1" / "_stages" / "v1_stage4_asr_transcript.txt"
    manifest = out_dir / "v1" / "_stages" / "v1_stage4_asr_manifest.json"
    assert srt.exists()
    assert transcript.exists()
    assert manifest.exists()
    assert "hello world" in srt.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("engine") == "sidecar_srt"
    assert payload.get("fallback_used") is False
    attempts = payload.get("attempts") or []
    assert attempts and attempts[0].get("backend") == "sidecar"

def test_stage5_rule_based_script_generation(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.delenv("OPENAI_API_KEY", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_LLM_MODEL", raising=False)

    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    stage_dir = out_dir / "v2" / "_stages"
    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    srt = stage_dir / "v2_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    srt.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:02,000",
                "build a clear workflow",
                "",
                "2",
                "00:00:02,000 --> 00:00:04,000",
                "validate every stage with tests",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    result = stage5_ai_text.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v2")

    assert result.output_file
    assert Path(str(result.output_file)).exists()

    manifest = stage_dir / "v2_stage5_ai_manifest.json"
    pointer = stage_dir / "v2_stage5_script_path.txt"
    assert script.exists()
    assert manifest.exists()
    assert pointer.exists()

    content = script.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    assert "Script Draft" in content
    assert "Key Points:" in content
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("engine") == "rule_based"

    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    task_id = "v2"

    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE2_MODE", "auto")
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage2_silence, "_command_exists", lambda name: name == "auto-editor")
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage2_silence, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: False)

    captured = {"cmd": []}

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured["cmd"] = list(args)
        out_idx = args.index("--output") + 1
        Path(args[out_idx]).write_bytes(b"auto-editor-output")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage2_silence, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

    result = stage2_silence.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id=task_id)
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file
    assert Path(str(result.output_file)).exists()
    assert "--margin" in captured["cmd"]

    report = out_dir / task_id / "_stages" / f"{task_id}_stage2_silence_report.json"
    payload = json.loads(report.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("method") == "auto_editor"

    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    target = tmp_path / "out.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE2_VIDEO_CODEC", "h264_nvenc")

    captured: list[list[str]] = []
    calls = {"count": 0}

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured.append(list(args))
        calls["count"] += 1
        if calls["count"] == 1:
            return False, "No NVENC capable devices found"
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage2_silence, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)
    ok, error = stage2_silence._run_ffmpeg_silence_remove(source=source, target=target)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]

    assert ok is True
    assert error == ""
    assert len(captured) == 2
    codecs = [cmd[cmd.index("-c:v") + 1] for cmd in captured]
    assert codecs == ["h264_nvenc", "libx264"]

    srt.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000",
                "hello srt",
                "",

    ass.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "[Script Info]",
                "Title: ass subtitle",
                "",
                "[Events]",
                "Format: Layer, Start, End, Style, Name, MarginL, MarginR, MarginV, Effect, Text",
                "Dialogue: 0,0:00:00.00,0:00:01.00,Default,,0,0,0,,hello ass",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE7_MODE", "burn")
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage7_subtitle, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: True)
    captured = {"cmd": []}

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured["cmd"] = list(args)
        Path(args[-1]).write_bytes(b"burned-video")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage7_subtitle, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)
    result = stage7_subtitle.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id=task_id)
    assert result.success
    vf_expr = captured["cmd"][captured["cmd"].index("-vf") + 1]
    assert vf_expr.startswith("ass=")

    assert manifest.exists()

    assert payload.get("cover_title_lines") == ["主标题", "副标题"]


def test_stage8_applies_video_title_overlay_with_subtitle_timing(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    task_id = "v8_overlay"

    subtitle = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage7_correct_subtitles.srt"
    subtitle.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:02,000 --> 00:00:04,000",
                "first subtitle",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage8_cover, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: True)
    captured = {"cmds": []}

    def fake_render_overlay(output_path, width, height, lines):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        Path(output_path).parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        Path(output_path).write_bytes(b"overlay-image")
        return True, ""

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured["cmds"].append(list(args))
        Path(args[-1]).parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        Path(args[-1]).write_bytes(b"generated")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage8_cover, "_render_title_overlay_image", fake_render_overlay)
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage8_cover, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

    result = stage8_cover.run(
        input_video=str(source),
        output_dir=str(out_dir),
        task_id=task_id,
        forum_post_info={"cover_titles": ["up-line", "down-line"]},
    )
    assert result.success

    manifest = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage8_cover_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert "video_title_overlay" in str(payload.get("method", ""))
    assert payload.get("overlay_duration_seconds") == 1.7

    overlay_cmd = captured["cmds"][-1]
    filter_expr = overlay_cmd[overlay_cmd.index("-filter_complex") + 1]
    assert "between(t,0,1.700)" in filter_expr

def test_build_clip_ranges_respects_max_duration(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_PAD_BEFORE_SECONDS", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_PAD_AFTER_SECONDS", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_MERGE_GAP_SECONDS", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_MIN_CLIP_SECONDS", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_MAX_SEGMENTS", raising=False)

    subtitle = tmp_path / "sample.srt"
    subtitle.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000",
                "line a",
                "",
                "2",
                "00:00:03,000 --> 00:00:04,000",
                "line b",
                "",
                "3",
                "00:00:08,000 --> 00:00:09,000",
                "line c",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    ranges, detail = stage6_clip._build_clip_ranges(  # type: ignore[attr-defined]
        subtitle_path=subtitle,
        video_duration=12.0,
        max_duration=3,
    )
    assert ranges
    total = sum(max(0.0, end - start) for start, end in ranges)
    assert total <= 3.01
    assert "merged=" in detail

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

def test_stage6_trim_gpu_codec_failure_downgrades_to_libx264(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    target = tmp_path / "out.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"input-video")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_VIDEO_CODEC", "h264_nvenc")

    captured: list[list[str]] = []
    calls = {"count": 0}

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured.append(list(args))
        calls["count"] += 1
        if calls["count"] == 1:
            return False, "No NVENC capable devices found"
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)
    ok, error = stage6_clip._render_trim_seconds(source=source, target=target, target_seconds=3.0)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]

    assert ok is True
    assert error == ""
    codecs = [cmd[cmd.index("-c:v") + 1] for cmd in captured]
    assert codecs == ["h264_nvenc", "libx264"]

        out = Path(args[-1])

        out.write_bytes(b"trimmed-video")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

    assert result.success

    assert output_path.exists()

@pytest.fixture(autouse=True)
def _set_fast_pipeline_env(monkeypatch) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    # Keep stage execution deterministic in CI/local without heavyweight ASR inference.
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "sidecar")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE2_MODE", "copy")


def _build_config(tmp_path) -> SimpleNamespace:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    ns_hash = hashlib.md5(str(tmp_path).encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
    namespace = f"clonecut_worker_unit_{ns_hash}:"
    return SimpleNamespace(
        redis_host="127.0.0.1",
        redis_port=6379,
        redis_db=0,
        redis_password="",
        redis_namespace=namespace,
        input_dir=str(tmp_path / "input"),
        output_dir=str(tmp_path / "output"),
        log_dir=str(tmp_path / "logs"),
        raw={
            "queue": {
                "max_retries": 2,
                "retry_backoff_seconds": [1, 1, 1],
            },
            "worker": {
                "max_download_workers": 1,
                "max_process_workers": 1,
                "max_upload_workers": 1,
                "download_timeout_seconds": 30,
                "download_chunk_size": 4096,
                "tts_enable": True,
                "tts_engine": "local",
                "use_internal_pipeline": False,
                "video_command_template": "",
                "retry_check_interval_seconds": 0.2,
                "zombie_timeout_seconds": 1,
                "zombie_check_interval_seconds": 0.2,
            },
        },
    )


def test_video_task_flows_download_process_upload(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    source = tmp_path / "source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video-content")

    service.start()
    try:
        ok, task_id, error = service.submit(
            {
                "task_type": "video",
                "source_url": str(source),
                "metadata": {"source": "unit"},
            }
        )
        assert ok
        assert not error
        assert task_id

        deadline = time.time() + 10
        final_task = None
        while time.time() < deadline:
            final_task = service.get_task(task_id)
            if final_task and final_task.get("status") == "completed":
                break
            time.sleep(0.05)

        assert isinstance(final_task, dict)
        assert final_task.get("status") == "completed"
        assert Path(str(final_task.get("source_path"))).exists()

        result = final_task.get("result")
        assert isinstance(result, dict)
        assert result.get("engine") == "internal_pipeline_auto"
        upload = result.get("upload")
        assert isinstance(upload, dict)
        uploaded_path = upload.get("uploaded_path")
        assert isinstance(uploaded_path, str) and uploaded_path
        assert Path(uploaded_path).exists()
    finally:
        service.stop()


def test_failed_task_auto_retries_until_success(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_retry.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)
    source = tmp_path / "retry-source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video-content")

    original = service._process_video_like
    attempts = {"count": 0}

    def flaky_process(task):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        attempts["count"] += 1
        if attempts["count"] == 1:
            raise RuntimeError("inject process failure")
        return original(task)

    service._process_video_like = flaky_process  # type: ignore[method-assign]

    service.start()
    try:
        ok, task_id, error = service.submit(
            {
                "task_type": "video",
                "source_url": str(source),
                "metadata": {"source": "retry-test"},
            }
        )
        assert ok
        assert not error

        deadline = time.time() + 15
        final_task = None
        while time.time() < deadline:
            final_task = service.get_task(task_id)
            if final_task and final_task.get("status") == "completed" and attempts["count"] >= 2:
                break
            time.sleep(0.1)

        assert attempts["count"] >= 2
        assert isinstance(final_task, dict)
        assert final_task.get("status") == "completed"
        assert int(final_task.get("retry_count", 0)) >= 1
    finally:
        service.stop()


def test_zombie_task_reclaimed_then_requeued(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_zombie.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    zombie = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="zombie-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        source_url=str(tmp_path / "missing.mp4"),
        status=TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
        current_stage=3,
        stage_checkpoint="stage3_repair",
        max_retries=1,
    )
    zombie.started_at = datetime.now() - timedelta(seconds=40)
    service._persist_task(zombie)

    reclaimed = service._reclaim_zombies_once()
    assert reclaimed == 1

    time.sleep(1.2)
    ready = service._dequeue_ready_retries()
    assert len(ready) == 1
    service._enqueue_retry_task(ready[0])

    queued = service.queue_adapter.pop_process(timeout=0.1)
    assert queued is not None
    assert queued.task_id == "zombie-1"
    loaded = service.get_task("zombie-1")
    assert isinstance(loaded, dict)
    assert loaded.get("status") == "pending"


def test_zombie_reclaim_uses_status_specific_thresholds(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_zombie_threshold.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    cfg.raw["worker"]["zombie_timeout_by_status_seconds"] = {
        "pending": 1,
        "downloading": 120,
        "processing": 120,
        "uploading": 120,
    }
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    pending_task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="pending-zombie-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        source_url=str(tmp_path / "pending.mp4"),
        status=TaskStatus.PENDING,
    )
    pending_task.created_at = datetime.now() - timedelta(seconds=10)
    service._persist_task(pending_task)

    processing_task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="processing-fresh-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        source_url=str(tmp_path / "processing.mp4"),
        status=TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
    )
    processing_task.started_at = datetime.now() - timedelta(seconds=10)
    service._persist_task(processing_task)

    reclaimed = service._reclaim_zombies_once()
    assert reclaimed == 1

    pending_loaded = service.get_task("pending-zombie-1")
    processing_loaded = service.get_task("processing-fresh-1")
    assert isinstance(pending_loaded, dict)
    assert isinstance(processing_loaded, dict)
    assert pending_loaded.get("status") == TaskStatus.FAILED.value
    assert processing_loaded.get("status") == TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value

    failed = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="manual-retry-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        source_path=str(source),
        status=TaskStatus.FAILED,
        metadata={"failed_from_status": TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value},
    )
    service._persist_task(failed)

    ok, error = service.retry_task("manual-retry-1")
    assert ok
    assert error == ""

    assert isinstance(task, dict)
    assert task.get("status") == TaskStatus.PENDING.value
    metadata = task.get("metadata") or {}
    assert metadata.get("manual_retry") is True

    queued = service.queue_adapter.pop_process(timeout=0.1)
    assert queued is not None
    assert queued.task_id == "manual-retry-1"

    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    pending = UnifiedTask(task_id="pending-1", task_type=TaskType.VIDEO, source="unit")
    failed = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="failed-2",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        status=TaskStatus.FAILED,
    )
    service._persist_task(pending)
    service._persist_task(failed)

    only_failed = service.list_tasks(status="failed", limit=20, offset=0)
    assert int(only_failed.get("total", 0)) >= 1
    tasks = only_failed.get("tasks") or []
    assert tasks
    assert all(item.get("status") == TaskStatus.FAILED.value for item in tasks)


def test_get_status_exposes_legacy_status_metrics(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_status_metrics.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    service._persist_task(UnifiedTask(task_id="status-pending", task_type=TaskType.VIDEO, source="unit"))
    service._persist_task(
        UnifiedTask(
            task_id="status-processing",
            task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
            source="unit",
            status=TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
        )
    )
    service._persist_task(
        UnifiedTask(
            task_id="status-failed",
            task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
            source="unit",
            status=TaskStatus.FAILED,
        )
    )
    service._persist_task(
        UnifiedTask(
            task_id="status-completed",
            task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
            source="unit",
            status=TaskStatus.COMPLETED,
        )
    )

    with service.lock:
        service.stats["received"] = 6
        service.stats["retried"] = 2
        service.stats["zombie_reclaimed"] = 1

    payload = service.get_status()
    metrics = payload.get("status_metrics") or {}
    assert metrics.get("total") == 4
    assert metrics.get("completed") == 1
    assert metrics.get("failed") == 1
    assert metrics.get("active") == 2
    assert metrics.get("zombie") == 1
    assert metrics.get("retried") == 2
    assert metrics.get("received") == 6

    def _remember(task, ttl_seconds=None):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        _ = task
        captured["ttl"] = int(ttl_seconds or 0)

    service.queue_adapter.remember_dedup = _remember  # type: ignore[assignment]
    service._enqueue_task = lambda queue_name, task: None  # type: ignore[assignment]

    ok, task_id, error = service.submit(
        {
            "task_type": "video",

            "metadata": {"source": "unit"},
        }
    )
    assert ok
    assert not error
    assert task_id
    assert captured.get("ttl") == 321

def test_build_task_normalizes_forum_post_info_and_source_url(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_forum_normalize.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    task = service._build_task(
        {
            "task_type": "video",
            "source_url": "https://forum.example.com/thread-123-1-1.html",
            "payload": {
                "video_urls": ["https://cdn.example.com/demo_source.mp4"],
                "hotwords": ["快剪", "AI", "ai"],
                "cover_title_up": "上标题",
                "cover_title_down": "下标题",
                "original_filename": "demo_source.mp4",
            },
            "metadata": {
                "source": "forum",
                "forum_post_info": {
                    "hotwords": ["快剪", "论坛"],
                    "封面标题中": "中标题",
                    "original_filename": "demo_source.mp4",
                },
            },
        }
    )

    assert task.source_url == "https://forum.example.com/thread-123-1-1.html"
    info = task.metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {}
    assert info.get("hotwords") == ["快剪", "论坛", "AI"]
    assert info.get("cover_title_up") == "上标题"
    assert info.get("cover_title_middle") == "中标题"
    assert info.get("cover_title_down") == "下标题"
    assert info.get("封面标题上") == "上标题"
    assert info.get("封面标题中") == "中标题"
    assert info.get("封面标题下") == "下标题"
    assert task.metadata.get("original_filename") == "demo_source.mp4"
    assert task.payload.get("original_filename") == "demo_source.mp4"

def test_run_process_stage_applies_original_filename_naming(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_forum_naming.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    source = tmp_path / "source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video")
    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-name-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        source_path=str(source),
        metadata={
            "source": "forum",
            "original_filename": "forum_final.mp4",
            "forum_post_info": {"original_filename": "forum_final.mp4"},
        },
    )
    service._persist_task(task)

    stage_output = Path(cfg.output_dir) / task.task_id / f"{task.task_id}.mp4"
    stage_output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    stage_output.write_bytes(b"processed-video")

    def fake_process_video_like(_task):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        return {
            "success": True,
            "request_type": "video",
            "engine": "internal_pipeline",
            "output_path": str(stage_output),
        }

    enqueued: dict[str, str] = {}

    def fake_enqueue(queue_name, queued_task):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        enqueued["queue"] = queue_name
        enqueued["task_id"] = queued_task.task_id

    service._process_video_like = fake_process_video_like  # type: ignore[method-assign]
    service._enqueue_task = fake_enqueue  # type: ignore[method-assign]

    service._run_process_stage(task)

    assert enqueued.get("queue") == "upload"
    assert enqueued.get("task_id") == task.task_id
    assert task.output_path is not None
    final_output = Path(task.output_path)
    assert final_output.exists()
    assert final_output.name == "forum_final.mp4"
    assert final_output.read_bytes() == b"processed-video"
    assert stage_output.exists()
    assert task.result is not None
    assert task.result.get("output_path") == str(final_output)
    assert task.result.get("original_output_path") == str(stage_output)
    assert task.result.get("named_output_path") == str(final_output)


def test_apply_video_output_naming_keeps_equivalent_final_output(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_forum_keep_final.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    final_output = tmp_path / "out" / "论坛样本视频" / "论坛样本视频_final.mp4"
    final_output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    final_output.write_bytes(b"processed-video")

    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-keep-final-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        source_path=str(tmp_path / "source.mp4"),
        metadata={
            "source": "forum",
            "original_filename": "论坛样本视频.mp4",
            "forum_post_info": {"original_filename": "论坛样本视频.mp4"},
        },
        payload={"original_filename": "论坛样本视频.mp4"},
    )
    task.source_path and Path(task.source_path).write_bytes(b"video")

    result = service._apply_video_output_naming(
        task,
        {
            "success": True,
            "request_type": "video",
            "engine": "internal_pipeline",
            "output_path": str(final_output),
        },
    )

    assert result.get("output_path") == str(final_output)
    assert result.get("named_output_path") is None
    assert not result.get("original_output_path")
    assert (task.metadata or {}).get("named_output_path") == str(final_output)


def test_upload_output_replies_forum_with_strict_attachment(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_upload_forum.db"))
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_BASE_URL", "https://forum.example.com")
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_USERNAME", "tester")
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_PASSWORD", "secret")
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    output_file = tmp_path / "forum-output.mp4"
    output_file.write_bytes(b"video-bytes")
    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-upload-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        output_path=str(output_file),
        metadata={"forum_post_info": {"thread_id": "12345"}},
    )

    captured: dict[str, object] = {}

    class FakeReplier:
        def __init__(self, http_client, logger=None) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            _ = logger
            captured["base_url"] = http_client.base_url

        def reply_with_attachments(self, thread_id, content, video_files, strict_attachment=False):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            captured["thread_id"] = thread_id
            captured["content"] = content
            captured["video_files"] = list(video_files)
            captured["strict_attachment"] = bool(strict_attachment)
            return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.worker.service.ForumReplier", FakeReplier)

    upload_result = service._upload_output(task)
    forum_reply = upload_result.get("forum_reply") or {}

    assert upload_result.get("success") is True
    assert upload_result.get("storage") == "local"
    assert forum_reply.get("attempted") is True
    assert forum_reply.get("success") is True
    assert forum_reply.get("thread_id") == "12345"
    assert captured.get("base_url") == "https://forum.example.com"
    assert captured.get("thread_id") == "12345"
    content = str(captured.get("content") or "")
    assert "🎬 AI智能剪辑完成！" in content
    assert "📝 原始视频: 未知文件" in content
    assert "🎯 处理结果: 1 个版本" in content
    assert "📹 forum-output.mp4" in content
    assert "🕒 处理时间:" in content
    assert "🤖 AI剪辑助手 - 智能视频处理完成" in content
    assert captured.get("strict_attachment") is True


def test_upload_output_replies_forum_prefers_user_report(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_upload_forum_user_report.db"))
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_BASE_URL", "https://forum.example.com")
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_USERNAME", "tester")
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_PASSWORD", "secret")
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    output_file = tmp_path / "forum-output-user-report.mp4"
    output_file.write_bytes(b"video-bytes")
    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-upload-user-report-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        output_path=str(output_file),
        metadata={
            "forum_post_info": {"thread_id": "12345"},
            "user_report": "这是用户侧报告内容",
        },
    )

    captured: dict[str, object] = {}

    class FakeReplier:
        def __init__(self, http_client, logger=None) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            _ = http_client
            _ = logger

        def reply_with_attachments(self, thread_id, content, video_files, strict_attachment=False):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            captured["thread_id"] = thread_id
            captured["content"] = content
            captured["video_files"] = list(video_files)
            captured["strict_attachment"] = bool(strict_attachment)
            return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.worker.service.ForumReplier", FakeReplier)

    upload_result = service._upload_output(task)
    forum_reply = upload_result.get("forum_reply") or {}

    assert upload_result.get("success") is True
    assert forum_reply.get("attempted") is True
    assert forum_reply.get("success") is True
    assert forum_reply.get("thread_id") == "12345"
    assert captured.get("thread_id") == "12345"
    assert captured.get("content") == "这是用户侧报告内容"
    assert captured.get("strict_attachment") is True


def test_upload_output_forum_4xx_is_non_retryable(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_upload_forum_4xx.db"))
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_BASE_URL", "https://forum.example.com")
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_USERNAME", "tester")
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_PASSWORD", "secret")
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    output_file = tmp_path / "forum-output-4xx.mp4"
    output_file.write_bytes(b"video-bytes")
    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-upload-4xx",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        output_path=str(output_file),
        metadata={"forum_post_info": {"thread_id": "12345"}},
    )

    class FakeReplier:
        def __init__(self, http_client, logger=None) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            _ = http_client
            _ = logger

        def reply_with_attachments(self, thread_id, content, video_files, strict_attachment=False):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            _ = thread_id
            _ = content
            _ = video_files
            _ = strict_attachment
            return False, "attachment upload failed: traditional upload failed: status=403"

    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.worker.service.ForumReplier", FakeReplier)

    with pytest.raises(NonRetryableUploadError):
        service._upload_output(task)


def test_fail_task_skips_retry_for_non_retryable_upload_error(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_upload_non_retryable.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="upload-no-retry-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        status=TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
        max_retries=2,
    )
    service._persist_task(task)

    service._fail_task(
        task=task,
        error=NonRetryableUploadError("attachment upload failed: status=403"),
        failed_from=TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
    )

    assert task.status == TaskStatus.FAILED
    assert task.retry_count == 0
    assert (task.metadata or {}).get("retryable_failure") is False
    assert "retry_due_at" not in (task.metadata or {})


def test_retry_delay_uses_upload_backoff_series(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_upload_backoff.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    cfg.raw["queue"]["retry_backoff_seconds"] = [9, 9, 9]
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    upload_task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="upload-backoff-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        metadata={"failed_from_status": TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value},
    )
    process_task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="process-backoff-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        metadata={"failed_from_status": TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value},
    )

    assert service._retry_delay_seconds(upload_task, 0) == 1
    assert service._retry_delay_seconds(upload_task, 1) == 2
    assert service._retry_delay_seconds(upload_task, 2) == 4
    assert service._retry_delay_seconds(process_task, 0) == 9


def test_run_download_stage_parses_forum_post_and_writes_forum_info_snapshot(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_forum_parse_download.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    source_media = tmp_path / "post-source.mp4"
    source_media.write_bytes(b"forum-video")

    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-parse-download-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        source_url="https://forum.example.com/thread-9876-1-1.html",
        status=TaskStatus.PENDING,
        metadata={"source": "forum"},
        payload={},
    )
    service._persist_task(task)

    parsed_called: dict[str, str] = {}

    def fake_parse(post_url):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        parsed_called["post_url"] = post_url
        return {
            "post_url": post_url,
            "thread_id": "9876",
            "post_id": "9876",
            "video_url": str(source_media),
            "video_urls": [str(source_media)],
            "original_filename": "forum_topic.mp4",
            "title": "forum title",
            "author_name": "alice",
        }

    queued: dict[str, str] = {}

    def fake_enqueue(queue_name, queued_task):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        queued["queue"] = queue_name
        queued["task_id"] = queued_task.task_id

    service._resolve_forum_post_download_info = fake_parse  # type: ignore[method-assign]
    service._enqueue_task = fake_enqueue  # type: ignore[method-assign]

    service._run_download_stage(task)

    assert parsed_called.get("post_url") == "https://forum.example.com/thread-9876-1-1.html"
    assert queued.get("queue") == "process"
    assert queued.get("task_id") == task.task_id
    assert task.source_path is not None
    downloaded_path = Path(task.source_path)
    assert downloaded_path.exists()
    assert downloaded_path.name == "forum_topic.mp4"
    assert downloaded_path.read_bytes() == b"forum-video"
    info_path = Path(str((task.metadata or {}).get("forum_post_info_path", "")))
    assert info_path.exists()
    snapshot = info_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    assert '"thread_id": "9876"' in snapshot
    assert '"original_filename": "forum_topic.mp4"' in snapshot


def test_run_download_stage_direct_source_skips_forum_parse_and_still_writes_snapshot(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_forum_direct_download.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    source_media = tmp_path / "direct-source.mp4"

            "source": "forum",

            },
        },
        payload={},
    )
    service._persist_task(task)

    def should_not_call(_post_url):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        raise AssertionError("forum post parser should not be called for direct media source")

    queued: dict[str, str] = {}

    def fake_enqueue(queue_name, queued_task):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        queued["queue"] = queue_name
        queued["task_id"] = queued_task.task_id

    service._resolve_forum_post_download_info = should_not_call  # type: ignore[method-assign]
    service._enqueue_task = fake_enqueue  # type: ignore[method-assign]

    service._run_download_stage(task)

    assert queued.get("queue") == "process"
    assert queued.get("task_id") == task.task_id
    assert task.source_path is not None
    downloaded_path = Path(task.source_path)
    assert downloaded_path.exists()
    assert downloaded_path.name == "direct_source.mp4"
    info_path = Path(str((task.metadata or {}).get("forum_post_info_path", "")))
    assert info_path.exists()

62:    ].

66:    .

68:    try:.

70:        exit_code = os.system(cmd_str).
71:        .
72:        if exit_code == 0:.
73:            logging.info("语音识别成功完成").
74:            return True, input_video.
75:        else:.

269:def run_command(cmd, step_name="", show_output=True, config=None):.
270:    """.
271:    运行命令并处理输出.
272:    .
273:    参数:.
274:        cmd: 要执行的命令（列表或字符串）.
275:        step_name: 步骤名称，用于日志记录.
276:        show_output: 是否显示输出.
277:        config: 配置参数字典.
278:        .
279:    返回:.
280:        (成功标志, 输出消息, stdout内容).
281:    """.
282:    if isinstance(cmd, list):.
283:        cmd_str = " ".join(cmd).
284:    else:.
285:        cmd_str = cmd.
286:        cmd = cmd.split().
287:    .
288:    if config and config.get("show_command", True):.
289:        logging.info(f"执行命令: {cmd_str}").
290:    elif config is None:.
291:        logging.info(f"执行命令: {cmd_str}").
292:    .
293:    try:.
294:        start_time = datetime.datetime.now().
295:        .
296:        # 执行命令并捕获输出.
297:        process = subprocess.Popen(.
298:            cmd,.
299:            stdout=subprocess.PIPE,.
300:            stderr=subprocess.PIPE,.
301:            universal_newlines=True.
302:        ).
303:        .
304:        # 实时显示输出.
305:        stdout_lines = [].
306:        stderr_lines = [].
307:        .
308:        # 读取并处理标准输出.
309:        has_progress_output = False.
310:        last_progress_line = ""  # 存储最后一行进度信息，避免重复显示同类信息.
311:        .
312:        for line in iter(process.stdout.readline, ""):.
313:            if not line:.
314:                break.
315:            stdout_lines.append(line.strip()).
316:            if show_output:.
317:                # 检查是否为进度信息（通常包含百分比或进度条）.
318:                is_progress = any(keyword in line for keyword in ['%', 'progress', '进度', '[=']).
319:                if is_progress:.
320:                    # 只有当进度信息与上一行不同时才打印，避免刷屏.
321:                    if line.strip() != last_progress_line:.
322:                        print(line.strip(), end='\r').
323:                        last_progress_line = line.strip().
324:                        has_progress_output = True.
325:                else:.
326:                    # 如果之前有进度信息，先打印一个换行，然后再打印非进度信息.
327:                    if has_progress_output:.
328:                        print().
329:                        has_progress_output = False.
330:                    print(line.strip()).
331:        .
332:        # 读取并处理标准错误.
333:        last_progress_line = ""  # 重置进度信息跟踪.
334:        for line in iter(process.stderr.readline, ""):.
335:            if not line:.
336:                break.
337:            stderr_lines.append(line.strip()).
338:            if show_output:.
339:                # 检查是否为进度信息（通常包含百分比或进度条）.
340:                is_progress = any(keyword in line for keyword in ['%', 'progress', '进度', 'time=', '[=']).
341:                if is_progress:.
342:                    # 只有当进度信息与上一行不同时才打印，避免刷屏.
343:                    if line.strip() != last_progress_line:.
344:                        print(line.strip(), end='\r', file=sys.stderr).
345:                        last_progress_line = line.strip().
346:                        has_progress_output = True.
347:                else:.
348:                    # 如果之前有进度信息，先打印一个换行，然后再打印非进度信息.
349:                    if has_progress_output:.
350:                        print().
351:                        has_progress_output = False.
352:                    print(line.strip(), file=sys.stderr).
353:        .
354:        # 如果有进度输出，打印换行确保后续内容从新行开始.
355:        if has_progress_output:.
356:            print().
357:        .
358:        # 等待进程完成.
359:        return_code = process.wait().
360:        end_time = datetime.datetime.now().

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import asdict, dataclass, field
from datetime import datetime
from enum import Enum
import json
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional


class TaskType(str, Enum):
    VIDEO = "video"
    TTS = "tts"
    VOICE_CLONE = "voice_clone"
    IMAGE = "image"


class TaskStatus(str, Enum):
    PENDING = "pending"
    ASSIGNED = "assigned"
    DOWNLOADING = "downloading"
    PROCESSING = "processing"
    UPLOADING = "uploading"
    COMPLETED = "completed"
    FAILED = "failed"
    CANCELLED = "cancelled"


ALLOWED_STATUS_TRANSITIONS = {
    TaskStatus.PENDING: {
        TaskStatus.ASSIGNED,
        TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING,
        TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
        TaskStatus.FAILED,
        TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
    },
    TaskStatus.ASSIGNED: {
        TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING,
        TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
        TaskStatus.FAILED,
        TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
    },
    TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING: {
        TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
        TaskStatus.FAILED,
        TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
    },
    TaskStatus.PROCESSING: {
        TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
        TaskStatus.COMPLETED,
        TaskStatus.FAILED,
        TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
    },
    TaskStatus.UPLOADING: {
        TaskStatus.COMPLETED,
        TaskStatus.FAILED,
        TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
    },
    TaskStatus.COMPLETED: set(),
    TaskStatus.FAILED: {
        TaskStatus.PENDING,
        TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
    },
    TaskStatus.CANCELLED: set(),
}


class TaskPriority(int, Enum):
    URGENT = 0
    HIGH = 1
    NORMAL = 2
    LOW = 3


def parse_task_type(value: Any) -> TaskType:
    if isinstance(value, TaskType):
        return value
    if isinstance(value, str):
        lowered = value.strip().lower()
        try:
            return TaskType(lowered)
        except ValueError:
            try:
                return TaskType[value.strip().upper()]
            except KeyError:
                return TaskType.VIDEO
    return TaskType.VIDEO


def parse_task_status(value: Any) -> TaskStatus:
    if isinstance(value, TaskStatus):
        return value
    if isinstance(value, str):
        lowered = value.strip().lower()
        try:
            return TaskStatus(lowered)
        except ValueError:
            try:
                return TaskStatus[value.strip().upper()]
            except KeyError:
                return TaskStatus.PENDING
    return TaskStatus.PENDING


def parse_task_priority(value: Any) -> TaskPriority:
    if isinstance(value, TaskPriority):
        return value
    if isinstance(value, int):
        try:
            return TaskPriority(value)
        except ValueError:
            return TaskPriority.NORMAL
    if isinstance(value, str):
        v = value.strip().lower()
        name_map = {
            "urgent": TaskPriority.URGENT,
            "high": TaskPriority.HIGH,
            "normal": TaskPriority.NORMAL,
            "low": TaskPriority.LOW,
        }
        if v in name_map:
            return name_map[v]
        if v.isdigit():
            try:
                return TaskPriority(int(v))
            except ValueError:
                return TaskPriority.NORMAL
    return TaskPriority.NORMAL


def can_transition_status(old_status: Any, new_status: Any) -> bool:
    old = parse_task_status(old_status)
    new = parse_task_status(new_status)
    if old == new:
        return True
    return new in ALLOWED_STATUS_TRANSITIONS.get(old, set())


@dataclass(order=True)
class UnifiedTask:
    sort_key: tuple = field(init=False, repr=False)

    task_id: str
    task_type: TaskType
    source: str

    source_url: Optional[str] = None
    source_path: Optional[str] = None

    status: TaskStatus = TaskStatus.PENDING
    priority: TaskPriority = TaskPriority.NORMAL

    created_at: datetime = field(default_factory=datetime.now)
    assigned_at: Optional[datetime] = None
    started_at: Optional[datetime] = None
    completed_at: Optional[datetime] = None

    payload: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)

    result: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    error_message: Optional[str] = None

    retry_count: int = 0
    max_retries: int = 3
    current_stage: int = 0
    stage_checkpoint: Optional[str] = None

    worker_id: Optional[str] = None
    worker_url: Optional[str] = None

    output_path: Optional[str] = None
    output_files: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)

    def __post_init__(self) -> None:
        self.task_type = parse_task_type(self.task_type)
        self.status = parse_task_status(self.status)
        self.priority = parse_task_priority(self.priority)
        try:
            self.current_stage = max(0, int(self.current_stage))
        except Exception:
            self.current_stage = 0
        if self.stage_checkpoint is not None:
            self.stage_checkpoint = str(self.stage_checkpoint).strip() or None
        self.sort_key = (int(self.priority), self.created_at)

    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        data = asdict(self)
        # sort_key is an internal ordering field and must not be part of serialized payload.
        data.pop("sort_key", None)
        data["task_type"] = self.task_type.value
        data["status"] = self.status.value
        data["priority"] = int(self.priority)
        data["created_at"] = self.created_at.isoformat()
        data["assigned_at"] = self.assigned_at.isoformat() if self.assigned_at else None
        data["started_at"] = self.started_at.isoformat() if self.started_at else None
        data["completed_at"] = self.completed_at.isoformat() if self.completed_at else None
        return data

    @classmethod
    def from_dict(cls, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> "UnifiedTask":
        copy = dict(data)
        copy.pop("sort_key", None)
        for key in ("created_at", "assigned_at", "started_at", "completed_at"):
            if copy.get(key) and isinstance(copy[key], str):
                copy[key] = datetime.fromisoformat(copy[key])
        return cls(**copy)

    def to_json(self) -> str:
        return json.dumps(self.to_dict(), ensure_ascii=False)

    @classmethod
    def from_json(cls, payload: str) -> "UnifiedTask":
        parsed = json.loads(payload)
        if not isinstance(parsed, dict):
            raise ValueError("invalid task json payload")
        return cls.from_dict(parsed)
