from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from datetime import datetime
from queue import Empty, PriorityQueue
import logging
import os
from threading import Event, RLock, Thread
import time
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
import uuid

from adapters.queue_redis import DispatchQueueAdapter, build_redis_client
from adapters.forum_discuz import ForumDiscoveryAdapter
from adapters.worker_client_http import WorkerHttpClient, extract_queue_size
from domain.task.models import parse_task_priority, parse_task_type


@dataclass
class Machine:
    host: str
    port: int
    priority: int = 1
    is_online: bool = False
    is_busy: bool = False
    current_tasks: int = 0
    last_check: str = ""
    response_time: float = 0.0
    last_error: Optional[str] = None

    @property
    def url(self) -> str:
        return f"http://{self.host}:{self.port}"

    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "url": self.url,
            "host": self.host,
            "port": self.port,
            "priority": self.priority,
            "is_online": self.is_online,
            "is_busy": self.is_busy,
            "current_tasks": self.current_tasks,
            "last_check": self.last_check,
            "response_time": self.response_time,
            "last_error": self.last_error,
        }


@dataclass(order=True)
class QueuedTask:
    sort_key: Tuple[int, float]
    task_data: Dict[str, Any] = field(compare=False)
    task_id: str = field(compare=False, default="")


class MonitorService:
    def __init__(
        self,
        config: Any,
        machines_file: Optional[str] = None,
        logger: Optional[logging.Logger] = None,
    ) -> None:
        self.config = config
        self.logger = logger or logging.getLogger("clonecut.monitor.service")
        self.client = WorkerHttpClient(
            timeout_seconds=float(self._get_monitor_cfg("dispatch_timeout_seconds", 5))
        )

        self.machines_file = machines_file or os.getenv("CLONECUT_MACHINES_FILE", "machines.txt")
        if not os.path.exists(self.machines_file) and os.path.exists("machines.txt.example"):
            self.machines_file = "machines.txt.example"

        self.machines: List[Machine] = self._load_machines(self.machines_file)
        self.redis_client = build_redis_client(
            host=str(getattr(config, "redis_host", "127.0.0.1")),
            port=int(getattr(config, "redis_port", 6379)),
            db=int(getattr(config, "redis_db", 0)),
            password=str(getattr(config, "redis_password", "")),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.dispatch_queue = DispatchQueueAdapter(
            redis_client=self.redis_client,
            namespace=str(getattr(config, "redis_namespace", "clonecut_monitor:")),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.use_redis_dispatch = self.dispatch_queue.is_persistent()
        self.task_queue: PriorityQueue[QueuedTask] = PriorityQueue()
        self.task_index: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]] = {}
        restored = self._restore_pending_tasks()

        self.lock = RLock()
        self._stop_event = Event()
        self._threads: List[Thread] = []
        self.monitoring_active = False

        self.dispatch_interval_seconds = float(self._get_monitor_cfg("dispatch_interval_seconds", 2))
        # Accept legacy key name `check_interval_seconds` for smoother migration.
        self.health_check_interval_seconds = float(
            self._get_monitor_cfg_alias(
                ("health_check_interval_seconds", "check_interval_seconds"),
                5,
            )
        )
        self.discovery_interval_seconds = float(
            self._get_monitor_cfg("forum_check_interval_seconds", 10)
        )
        self.discovery_enabled = self._bool_cfg(
            os.getenv("FORUM_DISCOVERY_ENABLED"),
            bool(self._get_monitor_cfg("forum_discovery_enabled", False)),
        )
        self.discovery_adapter: Optional[ForumDiscoveryAdapter] = None
        if self.discovery_enabled:
            self.discovery_adapter = ForumDiscoveryAdapter(
                config_path=os.getenv("FORUM_CONFIG_PATH", "config/forum_settings.yaml"),
                logger=self.logger,
            )

        self.stats: Dict[str, int] = {
            "total_tasks_received": 0,
            "total_tasks_sent": 0,
            "successful_tasks": 0,
            "failed_tasks": 0,
            "discovery_tasks": 0,
        }
        if restored > 0:
            self.logger.info("monitor restored pending dispatch tasks: %s", restored)

    def start(self) -> None:
        with self.lock:
            if self.monitoring_active:
                return
            self.monitoring_active = True
            self._stop_event.clear()

        self._threads = [
            Thread(target=self._health_check_loop, name="monitor-health", daemon=True),
            Thread(target=self._dispatch_loop, name="monitor-dispatch", daemon=True),
        ]
        if self.discovery_adapter is not None:
            self._threads.append(
                Thread(target=self._discovery_loop, name="monitor-discovery", daemon=True)
            )

        for thread in self._threads:
            thread.start()

        self.logger.info(
            "monitor service started: machines=%s discovery=%s redis_dispatch=%s",
            len(self.machines),
            self.discovery_enabled,
            self.use_redis_dispatch,
        )

    def stop(self) -> None:
        with self.lock:
            if not self.monitoring_active:
                return
            self.monitoring_active = False
        self._stop_event.set()
        for thread in self._threads:
            thread.join(timeout=2.0)
        self.logger.info("monitor service stopped")

    def submit_task(self, task_data: Dict[str, Any], source: str = "manual") -> str:
        normalized = self._normalize_task_data(task_data, source=source)
        if normalized["task_type"] == "video" and not normalized["source_url"]:
            raise ValueError("missing source url for video task")
        task_id = normalized["task_id"]
        priority = parse_task_priority(normalized.get("priority", "normal"))

        queued = QueuedTask(
            sort_key=(int(priority), time.time()),
            task_data=normalized,
            task_id=task_id,
        )

        with self.lock:
            if self.use_redis_dispatch:
                self.dispatch_queue.push(normalized)
            else:
                self.task_queue.put(queued)
            self.task_index[task_id] = normalized
            self.stats["total_tasks_received"] += 1
            if source == "discovery":
                self.stats["discovery_tasks"] += 1

        self.logger.info("task queued: task_id=%s type=%s source=%s", task_id, normalized["task_type"], source)
        return task_id

    def dispatch_once(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        self._check_all_machines()
        machine = self._select_best_machine()
        if machine is None:
            return {"success": False, "error": "no available machine"}

        task_data = self._dequeue_dispatch_task()
        if task_data is None:
            return {"success": False, "error": "queue is empty"}
        task_id = str(task_data.get("task_id", "")).strip()
        if not task_id:
            return {"success": False, "error": "invalid queued task"}
        result = self.client.send_task(machine.url, task_data)

        with self.lock:
            self.stats["total_tasks_sent"] += 1

        if result.ok:
            with self.lock:
                self.stats["successful_tasks"] += 1
                self.task_index.pop(task_id, None)
            self.logger.info("task dispatched: task_id=%s machine=%s", task_id, machine.url)
            return {
                "success": True,
                "task_id": task_id,
                "machine": machine.to_dict(),
                "response": result.payload,
            }

        with self.lock:
            self.stats["failed_tasks"] += 1
            # put back to queue for retry
            self._requeue_dispatch_task(task_data)
        self.logger.warning(
            "dispatch failed: task_id=%s machine=%s error=%s",
            task_id,
            machine.url,
            result.error,
        )
        return {
            "success": False,
            "task_id": task_id,
            "machine": machine.to_dict(),
            "error": result.error or "dispatch failed",
            "status_code": result.status_code,
        }

    def _dequeue_dispatch_task(self) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        if self.use_redis_dispatch:
            return self.dispatch_queue.pop(timeout=0.05)
        try:
            queued = self.task_queue.get_nowait()
            return queued.task_data
        except Empty:
            return None

    def _requeue_dispatch_task(self, task_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:
        if self.use_redis_dispatch:
            self.dispatch_queue.push(task_data)
            return
        priority = parse_task_priority(task_data.get("priority", "normal"))
        queued = QueuedTask(
            sort_key=(int(priority), time.time()),
            task_data=dict(task_data),
            task_id=str(task_data.get("task_id", "")),
        )
        self.task_queue.put(queued)

    def get_cluster_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        with self.lock:
            stats_copy = dict(self.stats)
            queue_size = self.dispatch_queue.size() if self.use_redis_dispatch else self.task_queue.qsize()
            monitoring_active = self.monitoring_active
            machines = [m.to_dict() for m in self.machines]

        return {
            "monitoring_active": monitoring_active,
            "queue_size": queue_size,
            "stats": stats_copy,
            "machines": machines,
            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
        }

    def get_machines_status(self) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        with self.lock:
            return [m.to_dict() for m in self.machines]

    def get_dashboard_payload(self, limit: int = 20) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        safe_limit = max(1, min(200, int(limit)))
        cluster = self.get_cluster_status()
        pending_tasks = self.get_pending_tasks(limit=safe_limit)
        forum_trace = self._build_forum_trace(pending_tasks)
        cluster_map = self._build_cluster_map(cluster.get("machines") or [])
        return {
            "cluster": cluster,
            "pending_tasks": pending_tasks,
            "pending_count": len(pending_tasks),
            "forum_trace": forum_trace,
            "cluster_map": cluster_map,
            "timestamp": cluster.get("timestamp"),
        }

    def get_pending_tasks(self, limit: int = 50) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        if self.use_redis_dispatch:
            pending = self.dispatch_queue.list_pending(limit=limit)
            with self.lock:
                self.task_index = {
                    str(item.get("task_id", "")): item
                    for item in pending
                    if isinstance(item, dict) and str(item.get("task_id", "")).strip()
                }
            return pending
        with self.lock:
            values = list(self.task_index.values())[:limit]
        return values

    def _normalize_task_data(self, task_data: Dict[str, Any], source: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        data = dict(task_data or {})
        metadata = dict(data.get("metadata") or {})
        payload = dict(data.get("payload") or {})

        task_id = str(data.get("task_id") or uuid.uuid4())
        task_type = parse_task_type(data.get("task_type", metadata.get("task_type", "video"))).value
        priority = str(data.get("priority", "normal"))

        source_url = (
            data.get("url")
            or data.get("source_url")
            or data.get("post_url")
            or metadata.get("post_url")
            or ""
        )

        category = data.get("category", metadata.get("category", ""))
        if category and "category" not in metadata:
            metadata["category"] = category

        if "source" not in metadata:
            metadata["source"] = source
        metadata["task_type"] = task_type

        forum_post_info = self._normalize_forum_post_info(data=data, payload=payload, metadata=metadata)
        if forum_post_info:
            metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_post_info
            payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_post_info
            hotwords = self._normalize_text_list(forum_post_info.get("hotwords"))
            if hotwords:
                metadata["hotwords"] = hotwords
                payload["hotwords"] = hotwords
            for key in ("cover_title_up", "cover_title_middle", "cover_title_down", "original_filename"):
                value = str(forum_post_info.get(key, "")).strip()
                if value:
                    metadata[key] = value
                    payload[key] = value

        normalized = {
            "task_id": task_id,
            "task_type": task_type,
            "priority": priority,
            "source_url": source_url,
            "url": source_url,
            "post_url": source_url,
            "metadata": metadata,
            "payload": payload,
            "forum_post_info": forum_post_info,
            "category": category,
        }
        return normalized

    def _build_forum_trace(self, tasks: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        output: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
        for item in tasks:
            if not isinstance(item, dict):
                continue
            metadata = item.get("metadata")
            payload = item.get("payload")
            info = {}
            if isinstance(metadata, dict) and isinstance(metadata.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
                info.update(metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})
            if isinstance(payload, dict) and isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
                info.update(payload.get("forum_post_info") or {})
            if not info:
                continue
            hotwords = self._normalize_text_list(info.get("hotwords"), item.get("hotwords"))
            output.append(
                {
                    "task_id": str(item.get("task_id", "")).strip(),
                    "hotwords": hotwords,
                    "cover_title_up": self._pick_first_text(info.get("cover_title_up"), info.get("封面标题上")),
                    "cover_title_middle": self._pick_first_text(
                        info.get("cover_title_middle"),
                        info.get("封面标题中"),
                    ),
                    "cover_title_down": self._pick_first_text(info.get("cover_title_down"), info.get("封面标题下")),
                    "original_filename": self._pick_first_text(info.get("original_filename")),
                }
            )
        return output

    def _build_cluster_map(self, machines: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        default_coords = [
            (31.2304, 121.4737),
            (39.9042, 116.4074),
            (22.5431, 114.0579),
            (23.1291, 113.2644),
            (30.5728, 104.0668),
            (34.3416, 108.9398),
        ]
        monitor_raw = {}
        if isinstance(getattr(self.config, "raw", None), dict):
            monitor_raw = self.config.raw.get("monitor", {}) or {}
        configured_nodes = monitor_raw.get("map_nodes", {}) or {}

        nodes: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
        for idx, machine in enumerate(machines):
            if not isinstance(machine, dict):
                continue
            host = str(machine.get("host", "")).strip()
            key = host or str(machine.get("url", "")).strip()
            cfg = configured_nodes.get(key, {}) if isinstance(configured_nodes, dict) else {}
            lat = self._safe_float(cfg.get("lat")) if isinstance(cfg, dict) else None
            lng = self._safe_float(cfg.get("lng")) if isinstance(cfg, dict) else None
            if lat is None or lng is None:
                lat, lng = default_coords[idx % len(default_coords)]
            current_tasks = int(machine.get("current_tasks", 0) or 0)
            port = int(machine.get("port", 0) or 0)
            priority = int(machine.get("priority", 1) or 1)
            nodes.append(
                {
                    "id": key or f"node-{idx + 1}",
                    "name": key or f"node-{idx + 1}",
                    "host": host,
                    "port": port,
                    "priority": priority,
                    "lat": lat,
                    "lng": lng,
                    "group": str((cfg.get("group") if isinstance(cfg, dict) else "") or "default"),
                    "load": min(1.0, max(0.0, current_tasks / 10.0)),
                    "online": bool(machine.get("is_online", False)),
                    "current_tasks": current_tasks,
                }
            )
        return {"enabled": bool(nodes), "nodes": nodes, "generated_at": datetime.now().isoformat()}

    def _safe_float(self, value: Any) -> Optional[float]:
        try:
            if value is None:
                return None
            return float(value)
        except Exception:
            return None

    def _normalize_forum_post_info(
        self,
        data: Dict[str, Any],
        payload: Dict[str, Any],
        metadata: Dict[str, Any],
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        merged: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        if isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            merged.update(payload.get("forum_post_info") or {})
        if isinstance(metadata.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            merged.update(metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})
        if isinstance(data.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            merged.update(data.get("forum_post_info") or {})

        hotwords = self._normalize_text_list(
            merged.get("hotwords"),
            payload.get("hotwords"),
            metadata.get("hotwords"),
            payload.get("keywords"),
            metadata.get("keywords"),
        )
        if hotwords:
            merged["hotwords"] = hotwords

        cover_up = self._pick_first_text(
            merged.get("cover_title_up"),
            merged.get("封面标题上"),
            data.get("cover_title_up"),
            data.get("封面标题上"),
            payload.get("cover_title_up"),
            payload.get("封面标题上"),
            metadata.get("cover_title_up"),
            metadata.get("封面标题上"),
        )
        cover_middle = self._pick_first_text(
            merged.get("cover_title_middle"),
            merged.get("封面标题中"),
            data.get("cover_title_middle"),
            data.get("封面标题中"),
            payload.get("cover_title_middle"),
            payload.get("封面标题中"),
            metadata.get("cover_title_middle"),
            metadata.get("封面标题中"),
        )
        cover_down = self._pick_first_text(
            merged.get("cover_title_down"),
            merged.get("封面标题下"),
            data.get("cover_title_down"),
            data.get("封面标题下"),
            payload.get("cover_title_down"),
            payload.get("封面标题下"),
            metadata.get("cover_title_down"),
            metadata.get("封面标题下"),
        )
        cover_titles = self._normalize_text_list(merged.get("cover_titles"))
        if not cover_up and len(cover_titles) >= 1:
            cover_up = cover_titles[0]
        if not cover_middle and len(cover_titles) >= 2:
            cover_middle = cover_titles[1]
        if not cover_down and len(cover_titles) >= 3:
            cover_down = cover_titles[2]
        if cover_up or cover_middle or cover_down:
            merged["cover_title_up"] = cover_up
            merged["cover_title_middle"] = cover_middle
            merged["cover_title_down"] = cover_down
            merged["封面标题上"] = cover_up
            merged["封面标题中"] = cover_middle
            merged["封面标题下"] = cover_down
            merged["cover_titles"] = [text for text in (cover_up, cover_middle, cover_down) if text]

        original_filename = self._pick_first_text(
            merged.get("original_filename"),
            data.get("original_filename"),
            payload.get("original_filename"),
            metadata.get("original_filename"),
        )
        if original_filename:
            merged["original_filename"] = original_filename

        return merged

    def _normalize_text_list(self, *values: Any) -> List[str]:
        output: List[str] = []
        seen: set[str] = set()
        for value in values:
            items: List[str] = []
            if isinstance(value, list):
                items = [str(item or "").strip() for item in value]
            elif isinstance(value, str):
                items = [item.strip() for item in value.replace("\uFF0C", ",").split(",")]
            for item in items:
                text = str(item or "").strip()
                if not text:
                    continue
                dedup_key = text.lower()
                if dedup_key in seen:
                    continue
                seen.add(dedup_key)
                output.append(text)
        return output

    def _pick_first_text(self, *values: Any) -> str:
        for value in values:
            text = str(value or "").strip()
            if text:
                return text
        return ""

    def _check_all_machines(self) -> None:
        for machine in self.machines:
            self._check_machine_status(machine)

    def _check_machine_status(self, machine: Machine) -> None:
        result = self.client.fetch_status(machine.url)
        now = datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M:%S")

        machine.last_check = now
        machine.response_time = round(result.response_ms, 2)
        if not result.ok:
            machine.is_online = False
            machine.is_busy = False
            machine.current_tasks = 0
            machine.last_error = result.error
            return

        payload = result.payload
        machine.is_online = True
        machine.is_busy = bool(payload.get("is_busy", False))
        machine.current_tasks = extract_queue_size(payload)
        machine.last_error = None

    def _select_best_machine(self) -> Optional[Machine]:
        online = [m for m in self.machines if m.is_online]
        if not online:
            return None

        idle = [m for m in online if not m.is_busy]
        if idle:
            return min(idle, key=lambda m: (m.priority, m.current_tasks))
        return min(online, key=lambda m: (m.current_tasks, m.priority))

    def _health_check_loop(self) -> None:
        while not self._stop_event.is_set():
            try:
                self._check_all_machines()
            except Exception as exc:
                self.logger.warning("health check loop error: %s", exc)
            self._stop_event.wait(self.health_check_interval_seconds)

    def _dispatch_loop(self) -> None:
        while not self._stop_event.is_set():
            try:
                queue_size = self.dispatch_queue.size() if self.use_redis_dispatch else self.task_queue.qsize()
                if queue_size > 0:
                    self.dispatch_once()
            except Exception as exc:
                self.logger.warning("dispatch loop error: %s", exc)
            self._stop_event.wait(self.dispatch_interval_seconds)

    def _discovery_loop(self) -> None:
        assert self.discovery_adapter is not None
        while not self._stop_event.is_set():
            try:
                tasks = self.discovery_adapter.discover_tasks()
                for task in tasks:
                    self.submit_task(task, source="discovery")
            except Exception as exc:
                self.logger.warning("discovery loop error: %s", exc)
            self._stop_event.wait(self.discovery_interval_seconds)

    def _restore_pending_tasks(self) -> int:
        if not self.use_redis_dispatch:
            return 0
        pending = self.dispatch_queue.list_pending(limit=5000)
        restored = 0
        for task in pending:
            if not isinstance(task, dict):
                continue
            task_id = str(task.get("task_id", "")).strip()
            if not task_id:
                continue
            self.task_index[task_id] = task
            restored += 1
        return restored

    def _load_machines(self, file_path: str) -> List[Machine]:
        machines: List[Machine] = []
        if not os.path.exists(file_path):
            self.logger.warning("machines file not found: %s", file_path)
            return machines

        with open(file_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            for raw in f:
                line = raw.strip()
                if not line or line.startswith("#"):
                    continue
                parts = line.split(":")
                if len(parts) < 2:
                    continue
                host = parts[0].strip()
                try:
                    port = int(parts[1].strip())
                except ValueError:
                    continue
                priority = 1
                if len(parts) >= 3:
                    try:
                        priority = int(parts[2].strip())
                    except ValueError:
                        priority = 1
                machines.append(Machine(host=host, port=port, priority=priority))
        return machines

    def _get_monitor_cfg(self, key: str, default: Any) -> Any:
        return self._get_monitor_cfg_alias((key,), default)

    def _get_monitor_cfg_alias(self, keys: Tuple[str, ...], default: Any) -> Any:
        raw_monitor = {}
        if isinstance(getattr(self.config, "raw", None), dict):
            raw_monitor = self.config.raw.get("monitor", {}) or {}
        for key in keys:
            env_key = f"CLONECUT_MONITOR_{key}".upper()
            env_val = os.getenv(env_key)
            if env_val is not None:
                return self._cast_cfg_value(env_val, default)
        for key in keys:
            if key in raw_monitor:
                return self._cast_cfg_value(raw_monitor.get(key), default)
        return default

    def _cast_cfg_value(self, value: Any, default: Any) -> Any:
        if isinstance(default, bool):
            if isinstance(value, bool):
                return value
            return str(value).strip().lower() == "true"
        if isinstance(default, int):
            try:
                return int(value)
            except Exception:
                return default
        if isinstance(default, float):
            try:
                return float(value)
            except Exception:
                return default
        return value

    def _bool_cfg(self, raw: Optional[str], default: bool) -> bool:
        if raw is None:
            return default
        return raw.strip().lower() == "true"

"""
ForumIntegration — 论坛自动监控 + 回帖集成管理器
将 MultiForumCrawler、ForumReplier、TTS 适配器串联成完整的自动化流水线。

from __future__ import annotations

import logging
import threading
import time
from typing import Any, Callable, Dict, List, Optional

from domain.forum.models import ForumPost

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


class ReplyStrategy:
    """回帖内容生成策略基类"""

    def generate(self, post: ForumPost) -> Optional[str]:
        """返回回帖内容，None 表示跳过该帖"""
        raise NotImplementedError


class EchoReplyStrategy(ReplyStrategy):
    """简单回显策略（测试用）"""

    def __init__(self, template: str = "感谢分享！已收到帖子：{title}"):
        self.template = template

    def generate(self, post: ForumPost) -> Optional[str]:
        return self.template.format(
            title=post.title,
            author=post.author_name,
            post_id=post.post_id,
        )


class ForumIntegration:
    """
    论坛集成管理器。

    职责：
    1. 启动 MultiForumCrawler 监控多个论坛
    2. 新帖回调 → 过滤 → 生成回帖内容 → ForumReplier 发帖
    3. 可选：触发 TTS/语音克隆任务

    用法::

        integration = ForumIntegration(
            config_manager=cfg_mgr,
            reply_strategy=MyStrategy(),
        )
        integration.start()
        ...
        integration.stop()
    """

    def __init__(
        self,
        config_manager: Any,                          # ForumConfigManager
        reply_strategy: Optional[ReplyStrategy] = None,
        on_new_post: Optional[Callable[[ForumPost], None]] = None,
        on_reply_sent: Optional[Callable[[ForumPost, bool, str], None]] = None,
        dry_run: bool = False,
    ) -> None:
        self._config_manager = config_manager
        self._reply_strategy = reply_strategy or EchoReplyStrategy()
        self._on_new_post_cb = on_new_post
        self._on_reply_sent_cb = on_reply_sent
        self._dry_run = dry_run

        self._multi_crawler: Optional[Any] = None
        self._repliers: Dict[str, Any] = {}   # forum_id -> ForumReplier
        self._running = False
        self._lock = threading.Lock()

        # 统计
        self._stats: Dict[str, int] = {
            "posts_seen": 0,
            "posts_skipped": 0,
            "replies_sent": 0,
            "reply_errors": 0,
        }

    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
    # Lifecycle
    # ------------------------------------------------------------------

    def start(self) -> None:
        with self._lock:
            if self._running:
                return
            self._setup_repliers()
            self._start_crawler()
            self._running = True
        logger.info("ForumIntegration started (dry_run=%s)", self._dry_run)

    def stop(self, timeout: float = 10.0) -> None:
        with self._lock:
            if not self._running:
                return
            if self._multi_crawler:
                self._multi_crawler.stop(timeout=timeout)
                self._multi_crawler = None
            self._running = False
        logger.info("ForumIntegration stopped. stats=%s", self._stats)

    def is_running(self) -> bool:
        return self._running

    def stats(self) -> Dict[str, int]:
        return dict(self._stats)

    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
    # Internal setup
    # ------------------------------------------------------------------

    def _setup_repliers(self) -> None:
        try:
            from adapters.forum_discuz.http_client import ForumHttpClient
            from adapters.forum_discuz.replier import ForumReplier
        except ImportError:
            logger.warning("ForumReplier not available; replies will be skipped")
            return

        for cfg in self._config_manager.all():
            if not cfg.auto_reply:
                continue
            try:
                client = ForumHttpClient(
                    base_url=cfg.base_url,
                    username=cfg.username,
                    password=cfg.password,
                )
                self._repliers[cfg.forum_id] = ForumReplier(http_client=client)
                logger.debug("ForumIntegration: replier ready for %s", cfg.forum_id)
            except Exception as exc:
                logger.error("ForumIntegration: failed to init replier for %s: %s", cfg.forum_id, exc)

    def _start_crawler(self) -> None:
        try:
            from adapters.forum_discuz.multi_crawler import MultiForumCrawler
        except ImportError:
            logger.error("MultiForumCrawler not available")
            return

        self._multi_crawler = MultiForumCrawler(
            config_manager=self._config_manager,
            on_new_post=self._handle_new_post,
        )
        self._multi_crawler.start()

    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
    # Post handling
    # ------------------------------------------------------------------

    def _handle_new_post(self, post: ForumPost) -> None:
        self._stats["posts_seen"] += 1

        # 外部回调
        if self._on_new_post_cb:
            try:
                self._on_new_post_cb(post)
            except Exception as exc:
                logger.warning("on_new_post callback error: %s", exc)

        # 生成回帖内容
        content = self._reply_strategy.generate(post)
        if not content:
            self._stats["posts_skipped"] += 1
            logger.debug("ForumIntegration: skipped post %s (strategy returned None)", post.post_id)
            return

        # 找到对应论坛的 replier
        replier = self._repliers.get(post.thread_id) or self._repliers.get(
            self._guess_forum_id(post)
        )
        if not replier:
            self._stats["posts_skipped"] += 1
            logger.debug("ForumIntegration: no replier for post %s", post.post_id)
            return

        self._send_reply(replier, post, content)

    def _send_reply(self, replier: Any, post: ForumPost, content: str) -> None:
        if self._dry_run:
            logger.info(
                "[DRY-RUN] would reply to thread=%s: %s",
                post.thread_id, content[:80],
            )
            self._stats["replies_sent"] += 1
            if self._on_reply_sent_cb:
                self._on_reply_sent_cb(post, True, "")
            return

        try:
            ok, err = replier.reply(post.thread_id, content)
            if ok:
                self._stats["replies_sent"] += 1
                logger.info("ForumIntegration: replied to thread=%s", post.thread_id)
            else:
                self._stats["reply_errors"] += 1
                logger.warning("ForumIntegration: reply failed thread=%s err=%s", post.thread_id, err)
            if self._on_reply_sent_cb:
                self._on_reply_sent_cb(post, ok, err)
        except Exception as exc:
            self._stats["reply_errors"] += 1
            logger.error("ForumIntegration: reply exception thread=%s: %s", post.thread_id, exc)

    def _guess_forum_id(self, post: ForumPost) -> str:
        """从帖子 URL 猜测 forum_id（简单匹配）"""
        for forum_id in self._repliers:
            if forum_id in (post.post_url or ""):
                return forum_id
        # 返回第一个可用的
        return next(iter(self._repliers), "")


__all__ = ["ForumIntegration", "ReplyStrategy", "EchoReplyStrategy"]

    "下载",
    "链接",
    "附件",
    "内容",
    "请求",
    "标题",
    "中间",
    "下面",
    "上面",
    "cover",
    "title",
    "video",
    "audio",
    "file",
}


class ForumContentProcessor:
    """Extract structured metadata from forum post payloads."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        max_hotwords: int = 12,
        logger: logging.Logger | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        self.max_hotwords = max(1, int(max_hotwords))
        self.logger = logger or logging.getLogger("clonecut.forum.content_processor")

    def extract_cover_titles(self, post: Any) -> Dict[str, str]:
        data = _as_dict(post)
        result = {
            "cover_title_up": "",
            "cover_title_middle": "",
            "cover_title_down": "",
        }

        aliases = {
            "cover_title_up": ("cover_title_up", "封面标题上", "标题上"),
            "cover_title_middle": ("cover_title_middle", "封面标题中", "标题中"),
            "cover_title_down": ("cover_title_down", "封面标题下", "标题下"),
        }
        for key, names in aliases.items():
            result[key] = self._pick_first_text(data, names)

        cover_info = data.get("cover_info")
        if isinstance(cover_info, dict):
            for key in result:
                if not result[key]:
                    result[key] = _clean_text(cover_info.get(key))

        cover_titles = data.get("cover_titles")
        ordered_titles = self._extract_title_list(cover_titles)
        if ordered_titles:
            if not result["cover_title_up"] and len(ordered_titles) >= 1:
                result["cover_title_up"] = ordered_titles[0]
            if not result["cover_title_middle"] and len(ordered_titles) >= 2:
                result["cover_title_middle"] = ordered_titles[1]
            if not result["cover_title_down"] and len(ordered_titles) >= 3:
                result["cover_title_down"] = ordered_titles[2]

        text_blob = self._merge_text(data, fields=("content", "core_text", "title"))
        regex_rules = {
            "cover_title_up": r"(?:封面标题上|标题上|cover[_\s-]?title[_\s-]?up)\s*[:：=]\s*([^\r\n]+)",
            "cover_title_middle": r"(?:封面标题中|标题中|cover[_\s-]?title[_\s-]?middle)\s*[:：=]\s*([^\r\n]+)",
            "cover_title_down": r"(?:封面标题下|标题下|cover[_\s-]?title[_\s-]?down)\s*[:：=]\s*([^\r\n]+)",
        }
        for key, pattern in regex_rules.items():
            if result[key]:
                continue
            match = re.search(pattern, text_blob, re.IGNORECASE)
            if match:
                result[key] = _clean_text(match.group(1))

        if not any(result.values()):
            compact = self._extract_compact_cover_titles(text_blob)
            if compact:
                result["cover_title_up"] = compact[0] if len(compact) >= 1 else ""
                result["cover_title_middle"] = compact[1] if len(compact) >= 2 else ""
                result["cover_title_down"] = compact[2] if len(compact) >= 3 else ""

        if not any(result.values()):
            result["cover_title_up"] = _clean_text(data.get("title"))

        for key in result:
            result[key] = self._trim_cover_line(result[key])
        return result

    def extract_hotwords(self, post: Any) -> List[str]:
        data = _as_dict(post)
        output: List[str] = []
        seen: set[str] = set()

        explicit_value = data.get("hotwords")
        for item in self._iter_words(explicit_value):
            self._append_hotword(output, seen, item)

        text_blob = self._merge_text(data, fields=("title", "content", "core_text"))
        keyword_lines = re.findall(
            r"(?:热词|关键词|关键字|hotwords?)\s*[:：=]\s*([^\r\n]+)",
            text_blob,
            flags=re.IGNORECASE,
        )
        for line in keyword_lines:
            for item in self._iter_words(line):
                self._append_hotword(output, seen, item)

        for item in re.findall(r"#([^#\r\n]{1,24})#", text_blob):
            self._append_hotword(output, seen, item)
        for item in re.findall(r"[【\[]([^\]】\r\n]{1,24})[】\]]", text_blob):
            self._append_hotword(output, seen, item)

        if len(output) < self.max_hotwords:
            tokens = self._tokenize(text_blob)
            freq = Counter(token for token in tokens if token and token not in _TOKEN_STOPWORDS)
            for token, _ in freq.most_common(self.max_hotwords * 2):
                self._append_hotword(output, seen, token)
                if len(output) >= self.max_hotwords:
                    break

        return output[: self.max_hotwords]

    def extract_original_filename(self, post: Any) -> str:
        data = _as_dict(post)
        for key in ("original_filename", "filename", "file_name", "original_file"):
            value = _normalize_filename(data.get(key))
            if value:
                return value

        for key in ("video_urls", "audio_urls", "media_urls"):
            for item in self._iter_urls(data.get(key)):
                value = _filename_from_url(item)
                if value:
                    return value

        for key in ("source_url", "post_url"):
            value = _filename_from_url(data.get(key))
            if value:
                return value

        text_blob = self._merge_text(data, fields=("content", "core_text"))
        for item in re.findall(
            r"([0-9A-Za-z\u4e00-\u9fff][0-9A-Za-z\u4e00-\u9fff._ -]{1,150}\.(?:mp4|mkv|mov|avi|flv|wmv|m4v|ts|mp3|wav|m4a|aac|ogg))",
            text_blob,
            flags=re.IGNORECASE,
        ):
            value = _normalize_filename(item)
            if value:
                return value
        return ""

    def build_forum_post_info(self, post: Any) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        data = _as_dict(post)
        post_id = _clean_text(data.get("post_id")) or _clean_text(data.get("thread_id"))
        thread_id = _clean_text(data.get("thread_id")) or post_id
        cover = self.extract_cover_titles(data)
        hotwords = self.extract_hotwords(data)
        original_filename = self.extract_original_filename(data)

        cover_title_lines = [
            cover["cover_title_up"],
            cover["cover_title_middle"],
            cover["cover_title_down"],
        ]
        compact_cover_lines = [item for item in cover_title_lines if item]

        info: Dict[str, Any] = {
            "post_id": post_id,
            "thread_id": thread_id,
            "post_url": _clean_text(data.get("post_url")),
            "title": _clean_text(data.get("title")),
            "content": _clean_text(data.get("content")),
            "core_text": _clean_text(data.get("core_text") or data.get("content")),
            "hotwords": hotwords,
            "original_filename": original_filename,
            "original_filenames": [original_filename] if original_filename else [],
            "cover_title_up": cover["cover_title_up"],
            "cover_title_middle": cover["cover_title_middle"],
            "cover_title_down": cover["cover_title_down"],
            "封面标题上": cover["cover_title_up"],
            "封面标题中": cover["cover_title_middle"],
            "封面标题下": cover["cover_title_down"],
            "cover_titles": compact_cover_lines,
        }

        for key in ("author_id", "author_name", "category"):
            value = _clean_text(data.get(key))
            if value:
                info[key] = value

        for key in ("speaker", "speaker_id", "target_speaker", "spk"):
            value = _clean_text(data.get(key))
            if value:
                info["speaker"] = value
                break
        return info

    def _pick_first_text(self, data: Dict[str, Any], keys: Sequence[str]) -> str:
        for key in keys:
            value = _clean_text(data.get(key))
            if value:
                return value
        return ""

    def _extract_title_list(self, value: Any) -> List[str]:
        if not isinstance(value, list):
            return []
        result: List[str] = []
        for item in value:
            if isinstance(item, dict):
                text = _clean_text(item.get("text"))
            else:
                text = _clean_text(item)
            if text:
                result.append(self._trim_cover_line(text))
        return result[:3]

    def _extract_compact_cover_titles(self, text: str) -> List[str]:
        line = ""
        match = re.search(r"(?:封面标题|cover\s*title)\s*[:：=]\s*([^\r\n]+)", text, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
        if match:
            line = match.group(1)
        if not line:
            return []
        parts = [self._trim_cover_line(item) for item in re.split(r"[|｜/／,，、;；]", line) if _clean_text(item)]
        return [item for item in parts if item][:3]

    def _merge_text(self, data: Dict[str, Any], fields: Sequence[str]) -> str:
        parts = [str(data.get(field) or "").strip() for field in fields]
        return "\n".join(item for item in parts if item)

    def _iter_words(self, value: Any) -> Iterable[str]:
        if isinstance(value, list):
            for item in value:
                text = _clean_text(item)
                if text:
                    yield text
            return
        if isinstance(value, str):
            for item in re.split(r"[,\uFF0C、|｜/；;\s]+", value):
                text = _clean_text(item)
                if text:
                    yield text

    def _iter_urls(self, value: Any) -> Iterable[str]:
        if not isinstance(value, list):
            return []
        urls: List[str] = []
        for item in value:
            text = str(item or "").strip()
            if text:
                urls.append(text)
        return urls

    def _append_hotword(self, output: List[str], seen: set[str], item: str) -> None:
        if len(output) >= self.max_hotwords:
            return
        normalized = _normalize_hotword(item)
        if not normalized:
            return
        dedup_key = normalized.lower()
        if dedup_key in seen:
            return
        seen.add(dedup_key)
        output.append(normalized)

    def _tokenize(self, text: str) -> List[str]:
        if not text:
            return []
        if _JIEBA_AVAILABLE and _jieba is not None:
            raw = [str(item).strip() for item in _jieba.cut(text, cut_all=False)]
        else:
            raw = []

        if not raw:
            raw = re.findall(r"[A-Za-z][A-Za-z0-9_-]{2,20}|[\u4e00-\u9fff]{2,6}", text)

        tokens: List[str] = []
        for item in raw:
            normalized = _normalize_hotword(item)
            if not normalized:
                continue
            if normalized.isdigit():
                continue
            tokens.append(normalized)
        return tokens

    def _trim_cover_line(self, text: str) -> str:
        value = _clean_text(text)
        if not value:
            return ""
        value = re.sub(r"^[\-•·\d\.\)\(、\s]+", "", value)
        value = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", value).strip()
        if len(value) > 40:
            return value[:40].rstrip()
        return value


def _as_dict(post: Any) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    if isinstance(post, dict):
        return dict(post)
    to_dict = getattr(post, "to_dict", None)
    if callable(to_dict):
        try:
            mapped = to_dict()
            if isinstance(mapped, dict):
                return dict(mapped)
        except Exception:
            return {}
    return {}


def _clean_text(value: Any) -> str:
    text = str(value or "").strip()
    return re.sub(r"\s+", " ", text)


def _normalize_hotword(value: str) -> str:
    text = _clean_text(value)
    if not text:
        return ""
    text = re.sub(r"^[#@【\[\(（\s]+", "", text)
    text = re.sub(r"[#】\]\)）\s]+$", "", text)
    text = text.strip(".,，。;；:：!?！？")
    if len(text) < 2:
        return ""
    if len(text) > 24:
        return ""
    return text


def _filename_from_url(value: Any) -> str:
    if not value:
        return ""
    text = str(value).strip()
    if not text:
        return ""
    try:
        parsed = urlparse(text)
        path = unquote(parsed.path or "")
    except Exception:
        path = ""
    if not path:
        return ""
    name = PurePosixPath(path).name
    return _normalize_filename(name)


def _normalize_filename(value: Any) -> str:
    text = str(value or "").strip()
    if not text:
        return ""
    text = unquote(text)
    text = text.split("?", 1)[0].split("#", 1)[0].strip()
    text = text.replace("\\", "/").split("/")[-1].strip()
    text = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", text)
    if len(text) < 3:
        return ""
    if len(text) > 180:
        return ""
    _, _, suffix = text.rpartition(".")
    ext = f".{suffix.lower()}" if suffix else ""
    if ext not in _MEDIA_EXTENSIONS:
        return ""
    return text


__all__ = ["ForumContentProcessor"]

from __future__ import annotations

import logging
import os
from pathlib import Path
import re
import subprocess
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional

from domain.task.models import UnifiedTask


class ExternalVideoCommandAdapter:
    """Optional adapter that delegates video processing to an external command."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        output_dir: str,
        command_template: str = "",
        timeout_seconds: int = 7200,
        logger: Optional[logging.Logger] = None,
    ) -> None:
        self.output_dir = Path(output_dir)
        self.command_template = command_template.strip()
        self.timeout_seconds = max(30, int(timeout_seconds))
        self.logger = logger or logging.getLogger("clonecut.adapters.video_pipeline")

    def is_enabled(self) -> bool:
        return bool(self.command_template)

    def process(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        if not self.command_template:
            raise RuntimeError("video command template is not configured")

        expected_output = self.output_dir / f"{task.task_id}.mp4"
        cmd = self.command_template.format(
            task_id=task.task_id,
            source_url=task.source_url or "",
            source_path=task.source_path or "",
            output_dir=str(self.output_dir),
            output_file=str(expected_output),
        )
        self.logger.info("run video command for task=%s", task.task_id)
        completed = subprocess.run(
            cmd,
            shell=True,
            check=False,
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            timeout=self.timeout_seconds,
        )
        if completed.returncode != 0:
            stderr = (completed.stderr or "").strip()
            stdout = (completed.stdout or "").strip()
            details = stderr or stdout or f"return code {completed.returncode}"
            raise RuntimeError(f"video command failed: {details}")

        output_path = self._pick_output_path(
            stdout=completed.stdout or "",
            stderr=completed.stderr or "",
            expected_output=expected_output,
            task_id=task.task_id,
        )
        return {
            "success": True,
            "request_type": "video",
            "engine": "external_video_command",
            "output_path": output_path,
            "command": cmd,
        }

    def _pick_output_path(
        self,
        stdout: str,
        stderr: str,
        expected_output: Path,
        task_id: str,
    ) -> str:
        merged = f"{stdout}\n{stderr}"
        match = re.search(r"output_path\s*[:=]\s*(\S+)", merged, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
        if match:
            return match.group(1).strip()

        if expected_output.exists():
            return str(expected_output)

        candidates = []
        for ext in (".mp4", ".mov", ".mkv", ".avi", ".webm"):
            candidates.extend(self.output_dir.glob(f"{task_id}*{ext}"))
        if candidates:
            latest = max(candidates, key=lambda p: p.stat().st_mtime)
            return str(latest)
        raise RuntimeError("video command finished but output file not found")


def build_default_video_adapter(output_dir: str, logger: Optional[logging.Logger] = None) -> ExternalVideoCommandAdapter:
    template = os.getenv("CLONECUT_VIDEO_COMMAND_TEMPLATE", "")
    timeout_raw = os.getenv("CLONECUT_VIDEO_COMMAND_TIMEOUT_SECONDS", "7200")
    try:
        timeout = int(timeout_raw)
    except ValueError:
        timeout = 7200
    return ExternalVideoCommandAdapter(
        output_dir=output_dir,
        command_template=template,
        timeout_seconds=timeout,
        logger=logger,
    )


__all__ = [
    "ExternalVideoCommandAdapter",
    "build_default_video_adapter",
]

from __future__ import annotations

from collections import deque
from datetime import datetime
import logging
from pathlib import Path
import shutil
import subprocess
from threading import Event, RLock, Thread
import time
from typing import Any, Deque, Dict, List, Optional

import psutil


class ResourceMonitor:
    """Collect runtime resource snapshots with in-memory history."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        interval_seconds: float = 5.0,
        history_minutes: int = 60,
        memory_limit_percent: float = 95.0,
        disk_limit_percent: float = 95.0,
        disk_path: str = ".",
        logger: Optional[logging.Logger] = None,
    ) -> None:
        self.logger = logger or logging.getLogger("clonecut.telemetry.resource_monitor")
        self.interval_seconds = max(0.5, float(interval_seconds))
        self.history_minutes = max(1, int(history_minutes))
        self.memory_limit_percent = max(1.0, float(memory_limit_percent))
        self.disk_limit_percent = max(1.0, float(disk_limit_percent))
        self.disk_path = str(Path(disk_path).resolve())

        maxlen = max(60, int((self.history_minutes * 60) / self.interval_seconds))
        self._history: Deque[Dict[str, Any]] = deque(maxlen=maxlen)
        self._step_snapshots: Deque[Dict[str, Any]] = deque(maxlen=5000)
        self._lock = RLock()
        self._stop_event = Event()
        self._thread: Optional[Thread] = None

        self._last_net = psutil.net_io_counters()
        self._last_net_ts = time.time()
        psutil.cpu_percent(interval=None)

    def start(self) -> None:
        with self._lock:
            if self._thread is not None and self._thread.is_alive():
                return
            self._stop_event.clear()
            self._thread = Thread(target=self._collect_loop, name="resource-monitor", daemon=True)
            self._thread.start()

    def stop(self) -> None:
        self._stop_event.set()
        thread = self._thread
        if thread is not None:
            thread.join(timeout=2.0)

    def get_current(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return self._collect_snapshot(persist=False)

    def get_history(self, minutes: int = 60) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        lookback = max(1, int(minutes))
        now_ts = time.time()
        cutoff = now_ts - (lookback * 60)
        with self._lock:
            snapshots = list(self._history)
        return [self._strip_internal_fields(item) for item in snapshots if item.get("_ts", 0.0) >= cutoff]

    def can_start_new_task(
        self,
        memory_limit_percent: Optional[float] = None,
        disk_limit_percent: Optional[float] = None,
    ) -> bool:
        snapshot = self.get_current()
        memory_limit = self.memory_limit_percent if memory_limit_percent is None else float(memory_limit_percent)
        disk_limit = self.disk_limit_percent if disk_limit_percent is None else float(disk_limit_percent)
        if float(snapshot.get("memory_percent", 0.0)) > memory_limit:
            return False
        if float(snapshot.get("disk_percent", 0.0)) > disk_limit:
            return False
        return True

    def record_step_resource(
        self,
        step_num: int,
        step_name: str,
        task_id: str = "",
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        snapshot = self.get_current()
        payload = {
            "task_id": task_id,
            "step_num": int(step_num),
            "step_name": str(step_name),
            "snapshot": snapshot,
            "timestamp": snapshot.get("timestamp"),
        }
        with self._lock:
            self._step_snapshots.append(payload)
        return payload

    def get_step_history(self, task_id: str = "", limit: int = 200) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        n = max(1, int(limit))
        with self._lock:
            rows = list(self._step_snapshots)
        if task_id:
            rows = [item for item in rows if str(item.get("task_id", "")) == task_id]
        return rows[-n:]

    def _collect_loop(self) -> None:
        while not self._stop_event.is_set():
            try:
                self._collect_snapshot(persist=True)
            except Exception as exc:
                self.logger.warning("resource monitor collection failed: %s", exc)
            self._stop_event.wait(self.interval_seconds)

    def _collect_snapshot(self, persist: bool) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        now_ts = time.time()
        vm = psutil.virtual_memory()
        disk = psutil.disk_usage(self.disk_path if Path(self.disk_path).exists() else str(Path.cwd()))
        net = psutil.net_io_counters()
        cpu_percent = float(psutil.cpu_percent(interval=None))

        elapsed = max(0.001, now_ts - self._last_net_ts)
        sent_delta = max(0, int(net.bytes_sent - self._last_net.bytes_sent))
        recv_delta = max(0, int(net.bytes_recv - self._last_net.bytes_recv))
        sent_rate = sent_delta / elapsed
        recv_rate = recv_delta / elapsed

        self._last_net = net
        self._last_net_ts = now_ts

        snapshot = {
            "_ts": now_ts,
            "timestamp": datetime.fromtimestamp(now_ts).isoformat(),
            "cpu_percent": round(cpu_percent, 2),
            "memory_percent": round(float(vm.percent), 2),
            "memory_used_gb": round(float(vm.used) / (1024**3), 3),
            "memory_total_gb": round(float(vm.total) / (1024**3), 3),
            "disk_used_gb": round(float(disk.used) / (1024**3), 3),
            "disk_total_gb": round(float(disk.total) / (1024**3), 3),
            "disk_percent": round(float(disk.percent), 2),
            "gpu": self._get_gpu_stats(),
            "network": {
                "bytes_sent": int(net.bytes_sent),
                "bytes_recv": int(net.bytes_recv),
                "bytes_sent_rate": round(sent_rate, 3),
                "bytes_recv_rate": round(recv_rate, 3),
            },
        }
        if persist:
            with self._lock:
                self._history.append(snapshot)
        return self._strip_internal_fields(snapshot)

    def _strip_internal_fields(self, snapshot: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        payload = dict(snapshot)
        payload.pop("_ts", None)
        return payload

    def _get_gpu_stats(self) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        gpu_stats = self._get_gpu_stats_gputil()
        if gpu_stats:
            return gpu_stats
        return self._get_gpu_stats_nvidia_smi()

    def _get_gpu_stats_gputil(self) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        try:
            import GPUtil  # type: ignore

            gpus = GPUtil.getGPUs()
            result: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
            for gpu in gpus:
                result.append(
                    {
                        "id": int(getattr(gpu, "id", 0)),
                        "name": str(getattr(gpu, "name", "")),
                        "utilization_percent": round(float(getattr(gpu, "load", 0.0)) * 100, 2),
                        "memory_used_mb": int(getattr(gpu, "memoryUsed", 0)),
                        "memory_total_mb": int(getattr(gpu, "memoryTotal", 0)),
                        "temperature_c": float(getattr(gpu, "temperature", 0.0)),
                    }
                )
            return result
        except Exception:
            return []

    def _get_gpu_stats_nvidia_smi(self) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        if shutil.which("nvidia-smi") is None:
            return []
        args = [
            "nvidia-smi",
            "--query-gpu=index,name,utilization.gpu,memory.used,memory.total,temperature.gpu",
            "--format=csv,noheader,nounits",
        ]
        try:
            completed = subprocess.run(
                args,
                check=False,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=3,
            )
            if completed.returncode != 0:
                return []
            rows = (completed.stdout or "").splitlines()
            result: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
            for raw in rows:
                parts = [item.strip() for item in raw.split(",")]
                if len(parts) < 6:
                    continue
                result.append(
                    {
                        "id": int(parts[0]),
                        "name": parts[1],
                        "utilization_percent": float(parts[2]),
                        "memory_used_mb": int(parts[3]),
                        "memory_total_mb": int(parts[4]),
                        "temperature_c": float(parts[5]),
                    }
                )
            return result
        except Exception:
            return []

我把 apps/、adapters/、domain/、infra/、tests/ 和这份报告都过了一遍。结论先说：这份审计报告作为“旧 domain/video/pre/stage 目录级审计”基本成立，但如果把它当成“当前整个 CloneCut 视频链路的仓库级评估”，它还差三块关键内容。

1. 报告漏掉了当前最大的系统级风险：Worker 默认走旧流水线，而且会把失败伪装成成功。
当前生产入口不是直接调一个干净的模块，而是 WorkerService 在处理阶段用子进程执行旧的 [pipeline.py](D:/clonecut/domain/video/pre/main/pipeline.py)，配置里默认 use_internal_pipeline: true，一旦缺 funasr 或子进程异常，又会回退到 fallback_copy 并返回 success=True。这比单个 stage bug 更危险，因为它会把“没真正处理”包装成“任务完成”。看 [service.py#L1270](D:/clonecut/apps/worker/service.py#L1270)、[service.py#L1319](D:/clonecut/apps/worker/service.py#L1319)、[service.py#L1436](D:/clonecut/apps/worker/service.py#L1436)、[settings.yaml.example#L50](D:/clonecut/config/settings.yaml.example#L50)。

2. 仓库正处在“想模块化，但实现没闭环”的断裂态，这一点报告没写出来。
一边有 [pipeline.py#L9](D:/clonecut/domain/video/pipeline.py#L9) 和多组测试在依赖 domain.video.stages，另一边仓库里根本没有这个目录；同时 [__init__.py#L3](D:/clonecut/domain/video/__init__.py#L3) 又明确不再暴露旧入口。也就是说，目标架构已经写进测试和文档，但代码没接上，这是你们从旧流水线走向可复用模块的真正阻塞点。

3. 报告里“主流程阶段基本没有自动化测试”的表述已经过时，但应该改成“测试资产和实现漂移”。
现在仓库里已经有 [test_stage4_stage5.py](D:/clonecut/tests/unit/test_stage4_stage5.py)、[test_stage2_stage7_stage9.py](D:/clonecut/tests/unit/test_stage2_stage7_stage9.py)、[test_stage6_clip.py](D:/clonecut/tests/unit/test_stage6_clip.py)、[test_stage6_5_resub.py](D:/clonecut/tests/unit/test_stage6_5_resub.py)、[test_stage7_correct.py](D:/clonecut/tests/unit/test_stage7_correct.py) 以及 worker/api/forum/monitor 的测试。更准确的结论不是“没测试”，而是“测试意图已经有了，但当前 .venv 里连 pytest 都没有，且部分测试依赖缺失模块，导致测试闭环断了”。报告原文见 [视频预处理阶段代码审计报告.md#L8](D:/clonecut/domain/video/pre/stage/视频预处理阶段代码审计报告.md#L8)。

4. 报告对旧 stage/ 目录本身的高风险判断，大体是对的。
我核对了几处关键点，像 [stage4.py#L57](D:/clonecut/domain/video/pre/stage/stage4.py#L57) 的 os.system、[utils.py#L158](D:/clonecut/domain/video/pre/stage/utils.py#L158) 和 [utils.py#L297](D:/clonecut/domain/video/pre/stage/utils.py#L297) 的顺序读管道、[stage5.py#L96](D:/clonecut/domain/video/pre/stage/stage5.py#L96) 的 wait_time、[stage8.py#L42](D:/clonecut/domain/video/pre/stage/stage8.py#L42) / [stage9.py#L24](D:/clonecut/domain/video/pre/stage/stage9.py#L24) 的全局日志副作用、[stage9.py#L352](D:/clonecut/domain/video/pre/stage/stage9.py#L352) 的 taskkill /IM python.exe、[stage5_0.py#L39](D:/clonecut/domain/video/pre/stage/stage5_0.py#L39) 和 [stage5_1.py#L39](D:/clonecut/domain/video/pre/stage/stage5_1.py#L39) 的运行时写源码，这些问题都还在。

如果目标是“从旧流水线变成边界清洗的可复用业务模块”，最短路径不是再造一套新架构，而是把仓库里已经暗示出来、但没实现完的 domain.video.stages 路线补完，并先加一层反腐层收编旧流水线。

1. 先定唯一公共边界。
定义 PreprocessRequest、ForumContext、StageContext、StageOutcome、PipelineResult。模块输入只收 source_path / task_id / forum_post_info / strict_equivalence / workspace；模块输出只返回 artifacts / warnings / metrics / status。

2. 把非业务边界全部剥出去。
apps/worker 只负责下载、排队、重试、上传；apps/monitor 只负责发现和派发；论坛抓取/回帖、Redis、SQLite、Telemetry 都留在外层。业务模块只做“视频预处理编排 + 论坛上下文注入 + 产物生成”。

3. 先做 LegacyPipelineAdapter，不要直接大拆。
让新模块先包住旧 [pre/main/pipeline.py](D:/clonecut/domain/video/pre/main/pipeline.py)，把 state.json、字幕、封面、最终视频统一映射成 typed artifacts。最重要的是把现在的 fallback_copy => success 改成显式 degraded 或 failed，不能再静默成功。

4. 按 stage 逐个绞杀，不要整条重写。
优先顺序建议是：stage9 organize、stage4 asr、stage5 ai_text、stage7 subtitle/stage8 cover、stage2/3、最后 stage6 clip。因为前几块边界最清晰，也已经有较多测试意图。

5. 让 domain/video/stages/ 成为真入口，而不是测试里的幻影。
现在测试已经在朝这个方向写了，那就顺着它落地：真正创建 domain/video/stages/，让 domain/video/__init__.py 正式导出稳定 API，同时删掉或修正失效的旧 domain/video/pipeline.py 路径。

6. 最后再把 Worker 从“子进程跑旧脚本”切到“进程内调用模块”。
等模块 API 和回归基线稳定后，WorkerService 直接调 PreprocessService.run()；CLI 只保留成一个薄壳，用来兼容手工执行，不再承载真实业务逻辑。

如果你要一个更落地的目标定义，我建议把“可复用业务模块”限定成这四件事：
- 接收标准化输入并创建任务工作区
- 执行 stage 编排并生成标准化 artifacts
- 明确区分 success / degraded / failed
- 对外暴露稳定的 Python API，不直接 input()、不改 sys.path、不碰全局 logger、不中途写源码树

这份报告我建议继续保留，但要补一个“仓库级补充结论”章节，至少加上：
- Worker 默认执行路径与 fallback 语义
- domain.video.stages 目标架构未闭环
- 测试资产存在但环境与实现漂移
- 配置漂移：[settings.yaml.example#L50](D:/clonecut/config/settings.yaml.example#L50) 默认开，[ .env.example#L11](D:/clonecut/.env.example#L11) 默认关

我没有直接跑 pytest，因为当前 .venv 里没有 pytest；但我用 uv run python 验证了导入状态，domain.video.pipeline 目前确实会因为缺失 domain.video.stages 而失败。
如果你愿意，我下一步可以直接给你出一版“可执行的重构蓝图”，把目标目录、接口定义、迁移顺序和每一步验收条件写成一份实施方案。
